package com.example.supermarket2.common.constants;

import java.time.Duration;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.time.LocalTime;

public class RedisKeyConstants {
    public static final String CART_USER_KEY = "cart:user:%s";
    public static final String SEARCH_HISTORY_KEY = "search:history:%s";
    public static final String SEARCH_HOT_KEY = "search:hot:keywords";
    public static final String STOCK_LOCK_KEY = "stock:lock:%s";

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇褰撳墠鏃堕棿鍒颁粖澶?23:59:59 鐨勫墿浣欑鏁?
     */
    public static final long getSecondsUntilEndOfDay() {
        LocalDateTime now = LocalDateTime.now();
        // 鑾峰彇褰撳ぉ鐨勬渶鍚庝竴鍒?(23:59:59.999999999)
        LocalDateTime endOfDay = now.with(LocalTime.MAX);

        // 璁＄畻鏃堕棿宸?
        long seconds = Duration.between(now, endOfDay).toSeconds();

        // 闃叉鏋佺鎯呭喌涓嬪嚭鐜拌礋鏁帮紙渚嬪鍒氬ソ鍦?23:59:59.999 瑙﹀彂锛?
        return Math.max(seconds, 1);
    }
}

package com.example.supermarket2.common.exception;

import com.example.supermarket2.common.result.ErrorCode;
import lombok.Getter;

/**
 * 缁熶竴涓氬姟寮傚父
 * 鎵€鏈変笟鍔￠€昏緫寮傚父鍧囨姏鍑烘寮傚父锛岀姝㈡姏鍑篟untimeException/鑷畾涔夊叾浠栧紓甯?
 */
@Getter
public class BusinessException extends RuntimeException {
    private final int code;
    private final String message;

    /**
     * 鎺ㄨ崘浣跨敤锛氱洿鎺ヤ紶鍏ラ敊璇爜鏋氫妇锛屽叏椤圭洰缁熶竴瑙勮寖
     */
    public BusinessException(ErrorCode errorCode) {
        super(errorCode.getMessage());
        this.code = errorCode.getCode();
        this.message = errorCode.getMessage();
    }

    /**
     * 娆℃帹鑽愶細鏀寔鍔ㄦ€佹浛鎹essage锛堟瘮濡傞渶瑕佹惡甯﹀弬鏁般€佹嫾鎺ヤ笟鍔′俊鎭級
     */
    public BusinessException(ErrorCode errorCode, String customMessage) {
        super(customMessage);
        this.code = errorCode.getCode();
        this.message = customMessage;
    }

    /**
     * 涓嶆帹鑽愶細鍏煎鏃ф柟寮忥紝浠呯壒娈婂満鏅娇鐢紝绂佹鏃ュ父寮€鍙戜娇鐢?
     */
    @Deprecated
    public BusinessException(int code, String message) {
        super(message);
        this.code = code;
        this.message = message;
    }

    /**
     * 閲嶅啓fillInStackTrace锛屼笟鍔″紓甯告棤闇€鎵撳嵃鍫嗘爤锛屾彁鍗囨€ц兘
     */
    @Override
    public synchronized Throwable fillInStackTrace() {
        return this;
    }
}

package com.example.supermarket2.common.exception;

import com.example.supermarket2.common.result.ErrorCode;
import com.example.supermarket2.common.result.Result;
import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import jakarta.validation.ConstraintViolation;
import jakarta.validation.ConstraintViolationException;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.slf4j.MDC;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
import org.springframework.core.Ordered;
import org.springframework.core.annotation.Order;
import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
import org.springframework.validation.FieldError;
import org.springframework.web.HttpMediaTypeNotAcceptableException;
import org.springframework.web.HttpMediaTypeNotSupportedException;
import org.springframework.web.HttpRequestMethodNotSupportedException;
import org.springframework.web.bind.MethodArgumentNotValidException;
import org.springframework.web.bind.MissingServletRequestParameterException;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.ExceptionHandler;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.ResponseStatus;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestControllerAdvice;
import org.springframework.web.servlet.NoHandlerFoundException;

import java.util.stream.Collectors;

/**
 * 鍏ㄥ眬寮傚父澶勭悊鍣?
 * 缁熶竴鎹曡幏骞跺鐞嗛」鐩腑鎵€鏈夊紓甯革紝杩斿洖鏍囧噯鍖栫殑Result鍝嶅簲浣?
 * 浼佷笟绾ц鑼冿細鍏ㄥ紓甯歌鐩栥€佹棩蹇楀垎绾с€侀摼璺拷韪€佸畨鍏ㄨ劚鏁忋€佺幆澧冮€傞厤
 */
@Slf4j
@RestControllerAdvice
@Order(Ordered.HIGHEST_PRECEDENCE) // 鏈€楂樹紭鍏堢骇锛岀‘淇濅紭鍏堟嫤鎴紓甯?
public class GlobalExceptionHandler {

    private static final String TRACE_ID_KEY = "traceId";

    /**
     * 璇诲彇褰撳墠鐜閰嶇疆锛屽尯鍒嗙敓浜?寮€鍙戠幆澧?
     */
    @Value("${spring.profiles.active:prod}")
    private String activeProfile;

    // ====================== 鏍稿績涓氬姟寮傚父澶勭悊锛堝凡鐭ュ彲棰勬湡寮傚父锛?======================
    /**
     * 鎹曡幏鑷畾涔変笟鍔″紓甯革紙鏍稿績涓氬姟寮傚父澶勭悊锛?
     */
    @ExceptionHandler(BusinessException.class)
    public Result<?> handleBusinessException(BusinessException e, HttpServletRequest request) {
        String traceId = MDC.get(TRACE_ID_KEY);
        // 涓氬姟寮傚父锛歸arn绾у埆锛屽彧鎵撳嵃涓氬姟淇℃伅锛屼笉鎵撳嵃鍫嗘爤锛堝凡鐭ュ紓甯革紝鏃犻渶鍫嗘爤瀹氫綅锛?
        log.warn("涓氬姟寮傚父 [traceId:{}] [{} {}] - 閿欒鐮?{}, 閿欒淇℃伅:{}",
                traceId,
                request.getMethod(),
                request.getRequestURI(),
                e.getCode(),
                e.getMessage());
        return Result.error(e.getCode(), e.getMessage()).setTraceId(traceId);
    }

    // ====================== 璇锋眰鍙傛暟鏍￠獙寮傚父澶勭悊 ======================
    /**
     * 璇锋眰浣揓SON鍙傛暟鏍￠獙澶辫触 (@Valid)
     */
    @ExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentNotValidException.class)
    @ResponseStatus(HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST)
    public Result<?> handleValidationException(MethodArgumentNotValidException e) {
        String traceId = MDC.get(TRACE_ID_KEY);
        String errorMsg = e.getBindingResult().getFieldErrors().stream()
                .map(FieldError::getDefaultMessage)
                .collect(Collectors.joining("; "));
        // 鍙傛暟寮傚父锛歸arn绾у埆锛屾墦鍗版牎楠屼俊鎭紝鏃犻渶瀹屾暣鍫嗘爤
        log.warn("鍙傛暟鏍￠獙澶辫触 [traceId:{}]: {}", traceId, errorMsg);
        return Result.error(ErrorCode.PARAM_ERROR, errorMsg).setTraceId(traceId);
    }

    /**
     * GET琛ㄥ崟鍙傛暟缁戝畾澶辫触 / @RequestParam鍙傛暟缂哄け
     */
    @ExceptionHandler({MissingServletRequestParameterException.class, ConstraintViolationException.class})
    @ResponseStatus(HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST)
    public Result<?> handleParamBindException(Exception e) {
        String traceId = MDC.get(TRACE_ID_KEY);
        String errorMsg;
        if (e instanceof MissingServletRequestParameterException ex) {
            errorMsg = "鍙傛暟[" + ex.getParameterName() + "]涓嶈兘涓虹┖";
        } else if (e instanceof ConstraintViolationException ex) {
            errorMsg = ex.getConstraintViolations().stream()
                    .map(ConstraintViolation::getMessage)
                    .collect(Collectors.joining("; "));
        } else {
            errorMsg = "璇锋眰鍙傛暟缁戝畾澶辫触";
        }
        log.warn("璇锋眰鍙傛暟缁戝畾澶辫触 [traceId:{}]: {}", traceId, errorMsg);
        return Result.error(ErrorCode.PARAM_ERROR, errorMsg).setTraceId(traceId);
    }

    // ====================== HTTP璇锋眰绯荤粺寮傚父澶勭悊 ======================
    /**
     * 404 鎺ュ彛涓嶅瓨鍦?
     */
    @ExceptionHandler(NoHandlerFoundException.class)
    @ResponseStatus(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND)
    public Result<?> handleNoHandlerFoundException(NoHandlerFoundException e, HttpServletRequest request) {
        String traceId = MDC.get(TRACE_ID_KEY);
        log.warn("璇锋眰鎺ュ彛涓嶅瓨鍦?[traceId:{}] [{} {}]", traceId, request.getMethod(), request.getRequestURI());
        return Result.error(ErrorCode.RESOURCE_NOT_FOUND).setTraceId(traceId);
    }

    /**
     * 璇锋眰鏂规硶涓嶆敮鎸?405
     */
    @ExceptionHandler(HttpRequestMethodNotSupportedException.class)
    @ResponseStatus(HttpStatus.METHOD_NOT_ALLOWED)
    public Result<?> handleMethodNotSupportedException(HttpRequestMethodNotSupportedException e, HttpServletRequest request) {
        String traceId = MDC.get(TRACE_ID_KEY);
        log.warn("璇锋眰鏂规硶涓嶆敮鎸?[traceId:{}] [{} {}], 鏀寔鐨勬柟娉?{}",
                traceId, request.getMethod(), request.getRequestURI(), e.getSupportedMethods());
        return Result.error(ErrorCode.METHOD_NOT_ALLOWED).setTraceId(traceId);
    }

    /**
     * 璇锋眰濯掍綋绫诲瀷涓嶆敮鎸?
     */
    @ExceptionHandler({HttpMediaTypeNotSupportedException.class, HttpMediaTypeNotAcceptableException.class})
    @ResponseStatus(HttpStatus.UNSUPPORTED_MEDIA_TYPE)
    public Result<?> handleMediaTypeException(Exception e) {
        String traceId = MDC.get(TRACE_ID_KEY);
        log.warn("璇锋眰濯掍綋绫诲瀷涓嶆敮鎸?[traceId:{}]: {}", traceId, e.getMessage());
        return Result.error(ErrorCode.MEDIA_TYPE_NOT_SUPPORTED).setTraceId(traceId);
    }

    // ====================== 鍏ㄥ眬鍏滃簳寮傚父澶勭悊锛堟湭鐭ョ郴缁熷紓甯革紝绂佹鍒犻櫎锛?======================
    /**
     * 鍏ㄥ眬鍏滃簳寮傚父澶勭悊锛屾崟鑾锋墍鏈夋湭琚笂闈㈡嫤鎴殑寮傚父
     * 褰诲簳閬垮厤寮傚父閫冮€稿鑷磋繑鍥為潪缁熶竴鏍煎紡銆佹硠闇插爢鏍堜俊鎭?
     */
    @ExceptionHandler(Exception.class)
    @ResponseStatus(HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR)
    public Result<?> handleGlobalException(Exception e, HttpServletRequest request) {
        String traceId = MDC.get(TRACE_ID_KEY);
        // 绯荤粺鏈煡寮傚父锛歟rror绾у埆锛屽繀椤绘墦鍗板畬鏁村爢鏍?鍏ㄤ笂涓嬫枃锛岀敤浜庣嚎涓婇棶棰樺畾浣?
        log.error("绯荤粺鏈煡寮傚父 [traceId:{}] [{} {}] [瀹㈡埛绔疘P:{}] [璇锋眰鍙傛暟:{}]",
                traceId,
                request.getMethod(),
                request.getRequestURI(),
                getClientIp(request),
                request.getParameterMap(),
                e); // 蹇呴』鎶婂紓甯稿璞′紶鍏og鏂规硶锛屾墠鑳芥墦鍗板畬鏁村爢鏍?

        // 鐜閫傞厤锛氱敓浜х幆澧冨彧杩斿洖閫氱敤鎻愮ず锛岄伩鍏嶆硠闇叉晱鎰熶俊鎭紱寮€鍙戠幆澧冭繑鍥炲紓甯镐俊鎭究浜庤皟璇?
        String errorMsg = "prod".equals(activeProfile)
                ? ErrorCode.SYSTEM_ERROR.getMessage()
                : e.getMessage();

        return Result.error(ErrorCode.SYSTEM_ERROR, errorMsg).setTraceId(traceId);
    }

    // ====================== 宸ュ叿鏂规硶 ======================
    /**
     * 鑾峰彇瀹㈡埛绔湡瀹濱P锛屽畬鍠勬棩蹇椾笂涓嬫枃
     */
    private String getClientIp(HttpServletRequest request) {
        String ip = request.getHeader("X-Forwarded-For");
        if (ip == null || ip.isEmpty() || "unknown".equalsIgnoreCase(ip)) {
            ip = request.getHeader("Proxy-Client-IP");
        }
        if (ip == null || ip.isEmpty() || "unknown".equalsIgnoreCase(ip)) {
            ip = request.getHeader("WL-Proxy-Client-IP");
        }
        if (ip == null || ip.isEmpty() || "unknown".equalsIgnoreCase(ip)) {
            ip = request.getRemoteAddr();
        }
        // 澶氫釜浠ｇ悊鐨勬儏鍐碉紝绗竴涓狪P涓哄鎴风鐪熷疄IP
        if (ip != null && ip.contains(",")) {
            ip = ip.split(",")[0].trim();
        }
        return ip;
    }
}

/**

 * 閿欒鐮佸垎娈佃鍒欙細
 * 200          閫氱敤鎴愬姛
 * 10000-19999  閫氱敤绯荤粺閿欒

package com.example.supermarket2.common.result;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonInclude;
import lombok.AccessLevel;
import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
import lombok.experimental.Accessors;

import java.io.Serial;
import java.io.Serializable;

/**
 * 鍏ㄥ眬缁熶竴鍝嶅簲浣?
 * 鎵€鏈塁ontroller鎺ュ彛缁熶竴杩斿洖璇ユ牸寮忥紝瑙勮寖鍓嶅悗绔氦浜?
 * 浼佷笟绾ф爣鍑嗭細寮虹害鏉熷疄渚嬪寲鍏ュ彛銆佸叏鍦烘櫙闈欐€佸伐鍘傘€佸簭鍒楀寲鍏煎銆侀摼寮忚皟鐢?
 */
@Data
@Accessors(chain = true) // 寮€鍚摼寮忚皟鐢紝鎵€鏈塻et鏂规硶鑷姩杩斿洖this锛屾棤闇€鎵嬪姩鍐檚etTraceId
@NoArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PRIVATE) // 绉佹湁鍖栨棤鍙傛瀯閫狅紝绂佹鎵嬪姩new
@AllArgsConstructor(access = AccessLevel.PRIVATE) // 绉佹湁鍖栧叏鍙傛瀯閫?
@JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL) // 搴忓垪鍖栨椂蹇界暐null鍊煎瓧娈碉紝鍑忓皯浼犺緭浣撶Н
public class Result<T> implements Serializable {

    // 淇搴忓垪鍖栬鍛婏紝JDK14+涓撶敤娉ㄨВ锛屼綆鐗堟湰JDK鍒犳帀杩欒娉ㄨВ鍗冲彲
    @Serial
    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;

    /**
     * 鍝嶅簲鐘舵€佺爜
     */
    private int code;
    /**
     * 鍝嶅簲鎻愮ず淇℃伅
     */
    private String message;
    /**
     * 鍝嶅簲鏁版嵁
     */
    private T data;
    /**
     * 閾捐矾杩借釜ID
     */
    private String traceId;

    // ====================== 鎴愬姛鍝嶅簲闈欐€佸伐鍘傛柟娉曪紙鍏ㄥ満鏅鐩栵級 ======================
    /**
     * 鏃犳暟鎹垚鍔熷搷搴?
     */
    public static <T> Result<T> success() {
        return new Result<>(ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getCode(), ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getMessage(), null, null);
    }

    /**
     * 甯︽暟鎹垚鍔熷搷搴?
     */
    public static <T> Result<T> success(T data) {
        return new Result<>(ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getCode(), ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getMessage(), data, null);
    }

    /**
     * 甯︽暟鎹?鑷畾涔夋彁绀烘垚鍔熷搷搴?
     */
    public static <T> Result<T> success(String message, T data) {
        return new Result<>(ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getCode(), message, data, null);
    }

    // ====================== 澶辫触鍝嶅簲闈欐€佸伐鍘傛柟娉曪紙寮虹粦瀹氶敊璇爜鏋氫妇锛?======================
    /**
     * 鑷畾涔夐敊璇爜+鎻愮ず澶辫触鍝嶅簲锛堝吋瀹瑰師鏈夊啓娉曪級
     */
    public static <T> Result<T> error(int code, String message) {
        return new Result<>(code, message, null, null);
    }

    /**
     * 閿欒鐮佹灇涓惧け璐ュ搷搴旓紙鎺ㄨ崘浣跨敤锛岀姝㈢‖缂栫爜锛?
     */
    public static <T> Result<T> error(ErrorCode errorCode) {
        return new Result<>(errorCode.getCode(), errorCode.getMessage(), null, null);
    }

    /**
     * 閿欒鐮佹灇涓?鑷畾涔夋彁绀哄け璐ュ搷搴?
     */
    public static <T> Result<T> error(ErrorCode errorCode, String message) {
        return new Result<>(errorCode.getCode(), message, null, null);
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\component\HuaweiAmqpListener.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.component;

import com.example.supermarket2.service.DeviceDataService;
import com.example.supermarket2.utils.HuaweiAmqpSignUtil;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.apache.qpid.jms.JmsConnectionFactory;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
import org.springframework.boot.CommandLineRunner;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import javax.jms.*;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;

/**
 * 鍗庝负浜慖oT AMQP 娑堟伅鐩戝惉鍣?
 * 涓ユ牸閬靛惊鍗庝负浜慉MQP鎺ュ叆瑙勮寖
 */
@Slf4j
@Component
public class HuaweiAmqpListener implements CommandLineRunner {

    @Value("${huawei.iot.amqp.url}")
    private String amqpUrl;

    @Value("${huawei.iot.amqp.accessKey}")
    private String accessKey;

    @Value("${huawei.iot.amqp.accessCode}")
    private String accessCode;

    @Value("${huawei.iot.amqp.queueName}")
    private String queueName;

    // 鍗庝负浜戝疄渚婭D锛堝熀纭€鐗堝～绌哄瓧绗︿覆锛屾爣鍑嗙増濉帶鍒跺彴鐨勫疄渚婭D锛?
    @Value("${huawei.iot.amqp.instanceId:}")
    private String instanceId;

    @Autowired
    private DeviceDataService deviceDataService;

    @Autowired
    private ObjectMapper objectMapper;

    // 杩炴帴鐘舵€佹爣璁?
    private final AtomicBoolean isRunning = new AtomicBoolean(false);
    private Connection connection;
    private Session session;

    @Override
    public void run(String... args) {
        log.info("=== 鍗庝负浜慖oT AMQP 寮€濮嬭繛鎺?===");
        try {
            // 1. 鐢熸垚鍚堣鐨勭敤鎴峰悕鍜屽瘑鐮?
            String userName = HuaweiAmqpSignUtil.generateUserName(accessKey, instanceId);
            String password = HuaweiAmqpSignUtil.generatePassword(accessCode, queueName);

            // 2. 鍒涘缓杩炴帴宸ュ巶
            JmsConnectionFactory factory = new JmsConnectionFactory(userName, password, amqpUrl);
            // 鍗庝负浜慉MQP蹇呴』璁剧疆鐨勫弬鏁?
            factory.setClientID(queueName + "_" + System.currentTimeMillis());
            factory.setReceiveLocalOnly(true);

            // 3. 鍒涘缓杩炴帴鍜屼細璇?
            connection = factory.createConnection();
            connection.setExceptionListener(this::handleConnectionException);
            connection.start();

            // 4. 鍒涘缓浼氳瘽锛堝鎴风鎵嬪姩ACK锛岀‘淇濇秷鎭笉涓㈠け锛?
            session = connection.createSession(false, Session.CLIENT_ACKNOWLEDGE);
            // 5. 缁戝畾闃熷垪
            Queue queue = session.createQueue(queueName);
            MessageConsumer consumer = session.createConsumer(queue);

            // 6. 璁剧疆娑堟伅鐩戝惉鍣?
            consumer.setMessageListener(this::handleMessage);

            isRunning.set(true);
            log.info("=== 鍗庝负浜慖oT AMQP 杩炴帴鎴愬姛锛岄槦鍒楋細{} ===", queueName);

        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("AMQP 杩炴帴澶辫触", e);
            closeConnection();
        }
    }

    /**
     * 澶勭悊鏀跺埌鐨勮澶囨秷鎭?
     */
    private void handleMessage(Message message) {
        try {
            if (message instanceof TextMessage textMessage) {
                String payload = textMessage.getText();
                log.info("鏀跺埌AMQP璁惧娑堟伅锛歿}", payload);
                // 璋冪敤璁惧鏁版嵁澶勭悊鏈嶅姟
                deviceDataService.processDeviceData(payload);
                // 鎵嬪姩ACK纭娑堟伅
                message.acknowledge();
            } else {
                log.warn("鏀跺埌闈炴枃鏈被鍨嬫秷鎭紝蹇界暐");
                message.acknowledge();
            }
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("AMQP娑堟伅澶勭悊澶辫触", e);
            // 寮傚父涓岮CK锛屾秷鎭細閲嶆柊鎶曢€?
        }
    }

    /**
     * 澶勭悊杩炴帴寮傚父
     */
    private void handleConnectionException(JMSException e) {
        log.error("AMQP杩炴帴寮傚父锛屽嵆灏嗛噸杩?, e);
        isRunning.set(false);
        closeConnection();
        // 绠€鍗曢噸杩為€昏緫锛岀敓浜х幆澧冨彲澧炲姞閲嶈繛闂撮殧鍜屾鏁伴檺鍒?
        try {
            Thread.sleep(5000);
            this.run();
        } catch (InterruptedException ex) {
            Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
        }
    }

    /**
     * 鍏抽棴杩炴帴
     */
    private void closeConnection() {
        try {
            if (session != null) session.close();
            if (connection != null) connection.close();
        } catch (JMSException e) {
            log.error("AMQP杩炴帴鍏抽棴寮傚父", e);
        }
        isRunning.set(false);
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\component\MqttMessageListener.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.component;

import com.example.supermarket2.service.DeviceDataService;
import org.eclipse.paho.client.mqttv3.IMqttMessageListener;
import org.eclipse.paho.client.mqttv3.MqttMessage;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Component
public class MqttMessageListener implements IMqttMessageListener {

    private static final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(MqttMessageListener.class);

    // 鏋勯€犲櫒娉ㄥ叆锛圫pring瀹樻柟鎺ㄨ崘锛岃В鍐冲瓧娈垫敞鍏ヨ鍛婏級
    private final DeviceDataService deviceDataService;

    public MqttMessageListener(DeviceDataService deviceDataService) {
        this.deviceDataService = deviceDataService;
    }

    @Override
    public void messageArrived(String topic, MqttMessage message) {
        try {
            String payload = new String(message.getPayload());
            logger.info("鏀跺埌鍗庝负浜慖oT娑堟伅: topic={}, payload={}", topic, payload);

            // 涓庢祴璇曠被瀹屽叏瀵归綈鐨?涓弬鏁拌皟鐢?
            deviceDataService.processDeviceData(topic, payload, null);

        } catch (Exception e) {
            logger.error("澶勭悊MQTT娑堟伅寮傚父锛宼opic={}", topic, e);
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\config\JacksonConfig.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.config;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonInclude;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.JsonParser;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.DeserializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.deser.LocalDateDeserializer;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.deser.LocalDateTimeDeserializer;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.ser.LocalDateSerializer;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.ser.LocalDateTimeSerializer;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Primary;
import org.springframework.util.StringUtils;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.text.SimpleDateFormat;
import java.time.LocalDate;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
import java.util.TimeZone;

/**
 * Jackson鍏ㄥ眬閰嶇疆
 * 鍏ㄩ」鐩敮涓€ObjectMapper鍗曚緥鍏ュ彛锛岀‘淇濇墍鏈夊満鏅簭鍒楀寲瑙勫垯缁熶竴
 * 鍖呮嫭锛歐eb璇锋眰銆丷edis瀛樺偍銆丮yBatis绫诲瀷杞崲銆丮QTT娑堟伅瑙ｆ瀽
 */
@Configuration
public class JacksonConfig {
    // 鏃ユ湡鏃堕棿鏍煎紡
    public static final String DEFAULT_DATE_TIME_FORMAT = "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss";
    // 鏃ユ湡鏍煎紡
    public static final String DEFAULT_DATE_FORMAT = "yyyy-MM-dd";
    // 鏃跺尯
    public static final String DEFAULT_TIME_ZONE = "GMT+8";

    /**
     * 鍏ㄥ眬鍞竴ObjectMapper Bean锛孈Primary纭繚浼樺厛娉ㄥ叆
     * 鎵€鏈夐渶瑕丱bjectMapper鐨勫満鏅紝蹇呴』閫氳繃@Autowired娉ㄥ叆姝ean锛岀姝ew ObjectMapper()
     */
    @Bean
    @Primary
    public ObjectMapper objectMapper() {
        ObjectMapper objectMapper = new ObjectMapper();

        // 1. 閰嶇疆鍏ㄥ眬鏃ユ湡鏃堕棿鏍煎紡鍖?
        // 澶勭悊java.util.Date绫诲瀷
        SimpleDateFormat dateFormat = new SimpleDateFormat(DEFAULT_DATE_TIME_FORMAT);
        dateFormat.setTimeZone(TimeZone.getTimeZone(DEFAULT_TIME_ZONE));
        objectMapper.setDateFormat(dateFormat);

        // 澶勭悊Java8鏃堕棿绫诲瀷锛圠ocalDateTime銆丩ocalDate锛?
        JavaTimeModule javaTimeModule = new JavaTimeModule();
        // 搴忓垪鍖朙ocalDateTime
        javaTimeModule.addSerializer(LocalDateTime.class, new LocalDateTimeSerializer(
                DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern(DEFAULT_DATE_TIME_FORMAT)));
        // 鍙嶅簭鍒楀寲LocalDateTime
        javaTimeModule.addDeserializer(LocalDateTime.class, new LocalDateTimeDeserializer(
                DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern(DEFAULT_DATE_TIME_FORMAT)));
        // 搴忓垪鍖朙ocalDate
        javaTimeModule.addSerializer(LocalDate.class, new LocalDateSerializer(
                DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern(DEFAULT_DATE_FORMAT)));
        // 鍙嶅簭鍒楀寲LocalDate
        javaTimeModule.addDeserializer(LocalDate.class, new LocalDateDeserializer(
                DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern(DEFAULT_DATE_FORMAT)));
        objectMapper.registerModule(javaTimeModule);

        // 2. 閰嶇疆搴忓垪鍖栫瓥鐣?
        // 蹇界暐鍊间负null鐨勫瓧娈碉紙鐢熶骇鐜鎺ㄨ崘锛屽噺灏戞姤鏂囦綋绉級
        objectMapper.setSerializationInclusion(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL);
        // 鍏佽搴忓垪鍖栫┖鐨凱OJO绫伙紙鍚﹀垯浼氭姏鍑哄紓甯革級
        objectMapper.disable(SerializationFeature.FAIL_ON_EMPTY_BEANS);
        // 搴忓垪鍖栨灇涓炬椂浣跨敤鏋氫妇鐨則oString()鏂规硶
        objectMapper.enable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_ENUMS_USING_TO_STRING);
        // 绂佺敤鏃ユ湡搴忓垪鍖栦负鏃堕棿鎴?
        objectMapper.disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);

        // 3. 閰嶇疆鍙嶅簭鍒楀寲绛栫暐
        // 蹇界暐JSON涓瓨鍦ㄤ絾Java瀵硅薄涓嶅瓨鍦ㄧ殑瀛楁锛堝墠鍚庣鍏煎蹇呭锛?
        objectMapper.disable(DeserializationFeature.FAIL_ON_UNKNOWN_PROPERTIES);
        // 鍏佽灏嗙┖瀛楃涓茶浆鎹负null
        objectMapper.enable(DeserializationFeature.ACCEPT_EMPTY_STRING_AS_NULL_OBJECT);
        // 鍏佽鍗曞紩鍙凤紙榛樿鍙敮鎸佸弻寮曞彿锛?
        objectMapper.enable(JsonParser.Feature.ALLOW_SINGLE_QUOTES);
        // 鍏佽JSON瀛楁鍚嶆病鏈夊紩鍙凤紙闈炴爣鍑咼SON锛?
        objectMapper.enable(JsonParser.Feature.ALLOW_UNQUOTED_FIELD_NAMES);
        // 鍏佽鏁板瓧鍓嶅闆?
        objectMapper.enable(JsonParser.Feature.ALLOW_NUMERIC_LEADING_ZEROS);

        // 4. 鑷畾涔夊弽搴忓垪鍖栧櫒锛氬瓧绗︿覆trim澶勭悊锛堝幓闄ゅ墠鍚庣┖鏍硷級
        javaTimeModule.addDeserializer(String.class, new com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonDeserializer<String>() {
            @Override
            public String deserialize(com.fasterxml.jackson.core.JsonParser p, com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.DeserializationContext ctxt) throws IOException {
                String value = p.getValueAsString();
                return StringUtils.hasText(value) ? value.trim() : null;
            }
        });

        return objectMapper;
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\config\LocationConfig.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.config;

import com.example.supermarket2.entity.location.BeaconConfig;
import com.example.supermarket2.utils.location.KalmanFilter2D;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.boot.context.properties.ConfigurationProperties;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;

/**
 * 瀹氫綅绯荤粺閰嶇疆绫?
 * 闆嗕腑绠＄悊瀹氫綅鐩稿叧鐨勯厤缃弬鏁板拰Bean鍒涘缓
 */
@Slf4j
@Data
@Configuration
@ConfigurationProperties(prefix = "location")
public class LocationConfig {

    // 瀹氫綅绠楁硶閰嶇疆
    private AlgorithmConfig algorithm = new AlgorithmConfig();

    // 淇″彿澶勭悊閰嶇疆
    private SignalConfig signal = new SignalConfig();

    // 璐ㄩ噺璇勪及閰嶇疆
    private QualityConfig quality = new QualityConfig();

    // 绯荤粺鎬ц兘閰嶇疆
    private PerformanceConfig performance = new PerformanceConfig();

    /**
     * 鍒涘缓鍗″皵鏇兼护娉㈠櫒Bean
     */
    @Bean
    public KalmanFilter2D kalmanFilter() {
        log.info("鍒濆鍖栧崱灏旀浖婊ゆ尝鍣? 杩囩▼鍣０={}, 娴嬮噺鍣０={}",
                algorithm.getKalmanProcessNoise(), algorithm.getKalmanMeasurementNoise());

        return new KalmanFilter2D(
                algorithm.getKalmanProcessNoise(),
                algorithm.getKalmanMeasurementNoise()
        );
    }

    /**
     * 鍒涘缓淇℃爣閰嶇疆Bean
     */
    @Bean
    public BeaconConfig beaconConfig() {
        BeaconConfig config = new BeaconConfig();

        // 璁剧疆RSSI閰嶇疆
        config.setRssi0(signal.getRssi0());
        config.setAttenuationFactor(signal.getAttenuationFactor());
        config.setRssiMin(signal.getRssiMin());
        config.setRssiMax(signal.getRssiMax());

        // 璁剧疆婊ゆ尝閰嶇疆
        config.setHistorySize(signal.getHistorySize());
        config.setOutlierThreshold(signal.getOutlierThreshold());
        config.setStabilityThreshold(signal.getStabilityThreshold());

        // 璁剧疆瀹氫綅绠楁硶閰嶇疆
        config.setKalmanProcessNoise(algorithm.getKalmanProcessNoise());
        config.setKalmanMeasurementNoise(algorithm.getKalmanMeasurementNoise());
        config.setMaxMovementDistance(algorithm.getMaxMovementDistance());

        // 璁剧疆璐ㄩ噺璇勪及閰嶇疆
        config.setHighQualityRssiThreshold(quality.getHighQualityRssiThreshold());
        config.setMediumQualityRssiThreshold(quality.getMediumQualityRssiThreshold());
        config.setLowQualityRssiThreshold(quality.getLowQualityRssiThreshold());

        // 璁剧疆鏉冮噸閰嶇疆
        config.setRssiWeightExponent(algorithm.getRssiWeightExponent());

        if (!config.isValid()) {
            log.warn("淇℃爣閰嶇疆鍙傛暟楠岃瘉澶辫触锛屼娇鐢ㄩ粯璁ゅ€?);
        }

        log.info("淇℃爣閰嶇疆鍒濆鍖栧畬鎴?);
        return config;
    }

    /**
     * 绠楁硶閰嶇疆
     */
    @Data
    public static class AlgorithmConfig {
        private Double kalmanProcessNoise = 1.0;
        private Double kalmanMeasurementNoise = 2.0;
        private Double maxMovementDistance = 5.0;
        private Double rssiWeightExponent = 0.2;
        private Integer minBeaconsForTrilateration = 3;
        private Integer minBeaconsForCentroid = 1;
        private Double predictionScale = 1.2;
    }

    /**
     * 淇″彿澶勭悊閰嶇疆
     */
    @Data
    public static class SignalConfig {
        private Double rssi0 = -55.0;
        private Double attenuationFactor = 3.2;
        private Integer rssiMin = -95;
        private Integer rssiMax = -35;
        private Integer historySize = 10;
        private Double outlierThreshold = 3.0;
        private Double stabilityThreshold = 0.6;
        private Integer movingAverageWindow = 5;
    }

    /**
     * 璐ㄩ噺璇勪及閰嶇疆
     */
    @Data
    public static class QualityConfig {
        private Double highQualityRssiThreshold = -65.0;
        private Double mediumQualityRssiThreshold = -70.0;
        private Double lowQualityRssiThreshold = -75.0;
        private Integer highQualityBeaconCount = 3;
        private Integer mediumQualityBeaconCount = 2;
        private Integer minConfidence = 50;
        private Double stabilityWeight = 0.3;
    }

    /**
     * 绯荤粺鎬ц兘閰嶇疆
     */
    @Data
    public static class PerformanceConfig {
        private Integer maxPositionHistory = 20;
        private Integer locationTimeout = 5000; // 姣
        private Boolean enableDetailedLogging = false;
        private Double maxAllowableError = 10.0; // 绫?
        private Integer cacheTimeout = 300; // 绉?
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇瀹屾暣鐨勯厤缃俊鎭紙鐢ㄤ簬鏃ュ織璁板綍锛?
     */
    public String getConfigSummary() {
        return String.format(
                "瀹氫綅绯荤粺閰嶇疆 - 绠楁硶: Kalman(%.1f,%.1f), 淇″彿: RSSI0=%.1f/n=%.1f, 璐ㄩ噺: 楂?%.1f/涓?%.1f/浣?%.1f",
                algorithm.getKalmanProcessNoise(),
                algorithm.getKalmanMeasurementNoise(),
                signal.getRssi0(),
                signal.getAttenuationFactor(),
                quality.getHighQualityRssiThreshold(),
                quality.getMediumQualityRssiThreshold(),
                quality.getLowQualityRssiThreshold()
        );
    }

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\config\MqttConfig.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.config;

import com.example.supermarket2.component.MqttMessageListener;
import jakarta.annotation.PreDestroy;
import org.eclipse.paho.client.mqttv3.MqttClient;
import org.eclipse.paho.client.mqttv3.MqttConnectOptions;
import org.eclipse.paho.client.mqttv3.MqttException;
import org.eclipse.paho.client.mqttv3.persist.MemoryPersistence;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;

@Configuration
public class MqttConfig {

    private static final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(MqttConfig.class);

    // ==================== 淇敼鐐?锛氬墠缂€浠?aliyun.iot 鏀逛负 huawei.iot.mqtt ====================
    @Value("${huawei.iot.mqtt.username}")
    private String username;

    @Value("${huawei.iot.mqtt.password}")
    private String password;

    @Value("${huawei.iot.mqtt.clientId}")
    private String clientId;

    @Value("${huawei.iot.mqtt.hostUrl}") // 淇敼鐐?锛氶厤缃」鍚嶄粠 mqttHostUrl 鏀逛负 hostUrl
    private String mqttHostUrl;

    @Value("${huawei.iot.mqtt.port:8883}")
    private int port;

    @Value("${huawei.iot.mqtt.subscribeTopic}") // 淇敼鐐?锛氶厤缃」鍚嶄粠 topic 鏀逛负 subscribeTopic
    private String subscribeTopic;

    @Autowired
    private MqttMessageListener mqttMessageListener;

    private MqttClient mqttClient;

    @Bean
    public MqttClient mqttClient() {
        try {
            logger.info("MQTT杩炴帴鍙傛暟 - Username: {}, ClientId: {}", username, clientId);

            // 鍗庝负浜慖oT MQTT 杩炴帴鍦板潃锛坰sl:// 鍓嶇紑淇濇寔涓嶅彉锛岀鍚圡QTTS鍗忚瑕佹眰锛?
            String broker = "ssl://" + mqttHostUrl + ":" + port;
            logger.info("杩炴帴MQTT鏈嶅姟鍣? {}", broker);

            mqttClient = new MqttClient(broker, clientId, new MemoryPersistence());

            MqttConnectOptions connOpts = new MqttConnectOptions();
            connOpts.setUserName(username);
            connOpts.setPassword(password.toCharArray());
            connOpts.setCleanSession(true);
            connOpts.setConnectionTimeout(30);
            connOpts.setKeepAliveInterval(60);
            connOpts.setAutomaticReconnect(true);
            connOpts.setHttpsHostnameVerificationEnabled(false);

            // 1. 鍏堣繛鎺?
            mqttClient.connect(connOpts);
            logger.info("鎴愬姛杩炴帴鍒板崕涓轰簯IoT MQTT鏈嶅姟鍣?);

            // 2. 鍚庤闃?(鍗曠嫭 try-catch锛岃闃呭け璐ヤ笉褰卞搷椤圭洰鍚姩)
            try {
                mqttClient.subscribe(subscribeTopic, 0, mqttMessageListener); // 淇敼鐐?锛氬彉閲忓悕浠?topic 鏀逛负 subscribeTopic
                logger.info("宸茶闃呬富棰? {}", subscribeTopic);
            } catch (MqttException e) {
                logger.error("璁㈤槄Topic澶辫触锛岃妫€鏌opic閰嶇疆: topic={}", subscribeTopic, e);
                logger.warn("椤圭洰灏嗙户缁惎鍔紝浣哅QTT娑堟伅鐩戝惉鏆備笉鍙敤銆?);
            }

            return mqttClient;

        } catch (MqttException e) {
            logger.error("MQTT瀹㈡埛绔垵濮嬪寲澶辫触: {}", e.getMessage(), e);
            throw new RuntimeException("MQTT瀹㈡埛绔垵濮嬪寲澶辫触", e);
        }
    }

    @PreDestroy
    public void destroy() {
        if (mqttClient != null && mqttClient.isConnected()) {
            try {
                mqttClient.disconnect();
                mqttClient.close();
                logger.info("MQTT瀹㈡埛绔凡鏂紑杩炴帴");
            } catch (MqttException e) {
                logger.error("鏂紑MQTT杩炴帴鏃跺嚭閿? {}", e.getMessage(), e);
            }
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\config\MybatisPlusConfig.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.config;

import com.baomidou.mybatisplus.annotation.DbType;
import com.baomidou.mybatisplus.core.handlers.MetaObjectHandler;
import com.baomidou.mybatisplus.extension.plugins.MybatisPlusInterceptor;
import com.baomidou.mybatisplus.extension.plugins.inner.PaginationInnerInterceptor;
import org.apache.ibatis.reflection.MetaObject;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.time.LocalDateTime;

@Configuration
public class MybatisPlusConfig {

    @Bean
    public MybatisPlusInterceptor mybatisPlusInterceptor() {
        MybatisPlusInterceptor interceptor = new MybatisPlusInterceptor();
        interceptor.addInnerInterceptor(new PaginationInnerInterceptor(DbType.MYSQL));
        return interceptor;
    }

    @Component
    public static class AutoFillHandler implements MetaObjectHandler {

        @Override
        public void insertFill(MetaObject metaObject) {
            this.strictInsertFill(metaObject, "createTime", LocalDateTime::now, LocalDateTime.class);
            this.strictInsertFill(metaObject, "updateTime", LocalDateTime::now, LocalDateTime.class);
        }

        @Override
        public void updateFill(MetaObject metaObject) {
            this.strictUpdateFill(metaObject, "updateTime", LocalDateTime::now, LocalDateTime.class);
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\config\RedisConfig.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.config;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonTypeInfo;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.DeserializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.jsontype.impl.LaissezFaireSubTypeValidator;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
import org.springframework.data.redis.connection.lettuce.LettuceConnectionFactory;
import org.springframework.data.redis.core.RedisTemplate;
import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer;
import org.springframework.data.redis.serializer.StringRedisSerializer;

@Configuration
public class RedisConfig {

    @Bean
    public RedisTemplate<String, Object> redisTemplate(LettuceConnectionFactory lettuceConnectionFactory) {
        RedisTemplate<String, Object> template = new RedisTemplate<>();
        template.setConnectionFactory(lettuceConnectionFactory);

        // Redis涓撶敤ObjectMapper
        ObjectMapper redisObjectMapper = new ObjectMapper();

        // 鍩虹閰嶇疆
        redisObjectMapper.registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
        redisObjectMapper.disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);
        redisObjectMapper.disable(DeserializationFeature.FAIL_ON_UNKNOWN_PROPERTIES);
        redisObjectMapper.enable(DeserializationFeature.ACCEPT_EMPTY_STRING_AS_NULL_OBJECT);

        // 鏍稿績淇锛氳嚜鍔ㄥ簭鍒楀寲绫诲瀷锛岃В鍐矻inkedHashMap寮鸿浆寮傚父
        redisObjectMapper.activateDefaultTyping(
                LaissezFaireSubTypeValidator.instance,
                ObjectMapper.DefaultTyping.NON_FINAL,
                JsonTypeInfo.As.PROPERTY
        );

        // 搴忓垪鍖栧櫒
        GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer jsonSerializer = new GenericJackson2JsonRedisSerializer(redisObjectMapper);
        StringRedisSerializer stringSerializer = new StringRedisSerializer();

        // 璁剧疆搴忓垪鍖栬鍒?
        template.setKeySerializer(stringSerializer);
        template.setValueSerializer(jsonSerializer);
        template.setHashKeySerializer(stringSerializer);
        template.setHashValueSerializer(jsonSerializer);

        template.afterPropertiesSet();
        return template;
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\config\SwaggerConfig.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.config;

import io.swagger.v3.oas.models.OpenAPI;
import io.swagger.v3.oas.models.info.Contact;
import io.swagger.v3.oas.models.info.Info;
import io.swagger.v3.oas.models.security.SecurityRequirement;
import io.swagger.v3.oas.models.security.SecurityScheme;
import org.springdoc.core.models.GroupedOpenApi;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;

@Configuration
public class SwaggerConfig {

    /**
     * 閰嶇疆鍏ㄥ眬 OpenAPI 淇℃伅锛堟爣棰樸€佺増鏈€丣WT 璁よ瘉绛夛級
     */
    @Bean
    public OpenAPI customOpenAPI() {
        // 1. 瀹氫箟 JWT 瀹夊叏璁よ瘉鏂规
        SecurityScheme jwtScheme = new SecurityScheme()
                .type(SecurityScheme.Type.HTTP)
                .scheme("bearer")
                .bearerFormat("JWT")
                .name("BearerAuth");

        // 2. 鍏ㄥ眬搴旂敤 JWT 璁よ瘉锛堟墍鏈夋帴鍙ｉ粯璁ら渶瑕?Token锛?
        SecurityRequirement securityRequirement = new SecurityRequirement().addList("BearerAuth");

        // 3. 鏋勫缓鏂囨。鍏冧俊鎭?
        return new OpenAPI()
                .info(new Info()
                        .title("Supermarket API")       // 鏂囨。鏍囬
                        .version("1.0")                // 鐗堟湰鍙?
                        .description("瓒呭競鍟嗗煄鎺ュ彛鏂囨。") // 鎻忚堪
                        .contact(new Contact()
                                .name("Developer")
                                .email("dev@example.com"))) // 浣滆€呬俊鎭?
                .addSecurityItem(securityRequirement) // 鍏ㄥ眬寮€鍚?JWT 璁よ瘉
                .components(new io.swagger.v3.oas.models.Components()
                        .addSecuritySchemes("BearerAuth", jwtScheme)); // 娉ㄥ唽 JWT 瀹夊叏鏂规
    }

    /**
     * 閰嶇疆銆宎dmin 妯″潡銆嶆帴鍙ｅ垎缁勶紙鎵弿鎸囧畾鍖呬笅鐨?Controller锛?
     */
    @Bean
    public GroupedOpenApi adminApi() {
        return GroupedOpenApi.builder()
                .group("admin") // 鍒嗙粍鍚嶇О锛堝乏渚у鑸樉绀猴級
                .packagesToScan("com.example.supermarket2.controller.admin") // Controller 鍖呰矾寰?
                .pathsToMatch("/admin/**") // 鎺ュ彛璺緞鍖归厤瑙勫垯
                .build();
    }

    /**
     * 閰嶇疆銆宎pp 妯″潡銆嶆帴鍙ｅ垎缁?
     */
    @Bean
    public GroupedOpenApi appApi() {
        return GroupedOpenApi.builder()
                .group("app")
                .packagesToScan("com.example.supermarket2.controller.app")
                .pathsToMatch("/app/**")
                .build();
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\config\TraceInterceptor.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.config;

import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
import org.slf4j.MDC;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.servlet.HandlerInterceptor;

import java.util.UUID;

/**
 * 閾捐矾杩借釜鎷︽埅鍣?
 * 涓烘瘡涓姹傜敓鎴愬敮涓€traceId锛岃疮绌垮叏璇锋眰閾捐矾
 */
@Component
public class TraceInterceptor implements HandlerInterceptor {

    private static final String TRACE_ID_KEY = "traceId";

    @Override
    public boolean preHandle(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response, Object handler) {
        // 鐢熸垚traceId锛屼紭鍏堝彇璇锋眰澶翠腑鐨則raceId锛屽惁鍒欑敓鎴愭柊鐨?
        String traceId = request.getHeader(TRACE_ID_KEY);
        if (traceId == null || traceId.isBlank()) {
            traceId = UUID.randomUUID().toString().replace("-", "");
        }
        MDC.put(TRACE_ID_KEY, traceId);
        // 鍝嶅簲澶磋繑鍥瀟raceId锛屾柟渚垮墠绔帓鏌ラ棶棰?
        response.setHeader(TRACE_ID_KEY, traceId);
        return true;
    }

    @Override
    public void afterCompletion(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response, Object handler, Exception ex) {
        // 璇锋眰缁撴潫鍚庢竻闄DC锛岄槻姝㈢嚎绋嬪鐢ㄥ鑷磘raceId閿欎贡
        MDC.remove(TRACE_ID_KEY);
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\config\WebMvcConfig.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.config;

import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
import org.springframework.web.servlet.config.annotation.CorsRegistry;
import org.springframework.web.servlet.config.annotation.InterceptorRegistry;
import org.springframework.web.servlet.config.annotation.ResourceHandlerRegistry;
import org.springframework.web.servlet.config.annotation.WebMvcConfigurer;

@Configuration
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class WebMvcConfig implements WebMvcConfigurer {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(WebMvcConfig.class);
    private final TraceInterceptor traceInterceptor;

    @Override
    public void addInterceptors(InterceptorRegistry registry) {
        // 娉ㄥ唽閾捐矾杩借釜鎷︽埅鍣紝鎷︽埅鎵€鏈夎姹?
        registry.addInterceptor(traceInterceptor)
                .addPathPatterns("/**")
                .excludePathPatterns("/webjars/**", "/doc.html", "/swagger-ui/**", "/images/**");
    }

    @Override
    public void addCorsMappings(CorsRegistry registry) {
        registry.addMapping("/**")
                .allowedOriginPatterns("*")
                .allowedMethods("GET", "POST", "PUT", "DELETE", "OPTIONS")
                .allowedHeaders("*")
                .allowCredentials(true)
                .maxAge(3600);
    }

    @Override
    public void addResourceHandlers(ResourceHandlerRegistry registry) {
        log.info("===== 寮€濮嬮厤缃?Knife4j 闈欐€佽祫婧愭槧灏?=====");
        // 1. 鏄犲皠 doc.html 鍒?classpath:/META-INF/resources/
        registry.addResourceHandler("doc.html")
                .addResourceLocations("classpath:/META-INF/resources/");
        // 2. 鏄犲皠 webjars 鍒?classpath:/META-INF/resources/webjars/
        registry.addResourceHandler("/webjars/**")
                .addResourceLocations("classpath:/META-INF/resources/webjars/");
        log.info("===== Knife4j 闈欐€佽祫婧愭槧灏勯厤缃畬鎴?=====");
        registry.addResourceHandler("/images/**")
                .addResourceLocations("classpath:/static/images/");
        log.info("===== 鐢ㄦ埛鍥剧墖闈欐€佽祫婧愭槧灏勯厤缃畬鎴?=====");
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\config\WebSocketConfig.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.config;

import com.example.supermarket2.handler.CartWebSocketHandler;
import com.example.supermarket2.handler.UniversalWebSocketHandler;
import com.example.supermarket2.interceptor.WebSocketHandshakeInterceptor;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration;
import org.springframework.web.socket.config.annotation.EnableWebSocket;
import org.springframework.web.socket.config.annotation.WebSocketConfigurer;
import org.springframework.web.socket.config.annotation.WebSocketHandlerRegistry;

/**
 * WebSocket 鍏ㄥ眬閰嶇疆
 * 鍏煎鍘熸湁璐墿杞﹀崟涓氬姟Handler锛屾柊澧為€氱敤鍏ㄤ笟鍔andler
 */
@Configuration
@EnableWebSocket // 寮€鍚疻ebSocket鏀寔
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class WebSocketConfig implements WebSocketConfigurer {

    private final WebSocketHandshakeInterceptor handshakeInterceptor;
    private final CartWebSocketHandler cartWebSocketHandler;
    private final UniversalWebSocketHandler universalWebSocketHandler;

    @Override
    public void registerWebSocketHandlers(WebSocketHandlerRegistry registry) {
        // 1. 鍘熸湁璐墿杞︿笓灞濿ebSocket绔偣锛堝吋瀹硅€佷唬鐮侊級
        registry.addHandler(cartWebSocketHandler, "/ws/cart")
                .addInterceptors(handshakeInterceptor) // 鎻℃墜鎷︽埅鍣紙韬唤鏍￠獙锛?
                .setAllowedOrigins("*"); // 鐢熶骇鐜璇烽厤缃叿浣撳煙鍚嶏紝绂佹鐢?

        // 2. 閫氱敤鍏ㄤ笟鍔ebSocket绔偣锛堝畾浣?瀵艰埅/璁惧/璐墿杞︾粺涓€鎺ュ叆锛?
        registry.addHandler(universalWebSocketHandler, "/ws/universal")
                .addInterceptors(handshakeInterceptor)
                .setAllowedOrigins("*");
    }
}

public class AdminMapController {

    }

    public Result<List<MapData>> getPublishedMaps() {
        List<MapData> list = mapService.getPublishedMaps();
        return Result.success(list);
    }

    @GetMapping("/list")
    @Operation(summary = "鑾峰彇鎵€鏈夊湴鍥?, description = "鑾峰彇鎵€鏈夊湴鍥惧垪琛紙鍚湭鍙戝竷锛?)
    public Result<List<MapData>> getAllMaps() {
        List<MapData> list = mapService.getAllMaps();
        return Result.success(list);
    }

    @PostMapping("/{id}/data")
    @Operation(summary = "淇濆瓨鍦板浘GeoJSON鏁版嵁", description = "鏇存柊鍦板浘鍏宠仈鐨勫湴鐞嗕俊鎭暟鎹紙GeoJSON鏍煎紡锛?)
    public Result<Boolean> saveMapData(
            @Parameter(description = "鍦板浘ID", required = true)
            @PathVariable @NotNull(message = "鍦板浘ID涓嶈兘涓虹┖") Long id,
            @Parameter(description = "GeoJSON鏍煎紡鐨勫湴鐞嗘暟鎹?, required = true)
            @RequestBody @NotBlank(message = "GeoJSON鏁版嵁涓嶈兘涓虹┖") String geoJson) {
        boolean result = mapService.saveMapData(id, geoJson);
        return Result.success(result ? "鍦板浘鏁版嵁淇濆瓨鎴愬姛" : "鍦板浘鏁版嵁淇濆瓨澶辫触", result);

    @Operation(summary = "鍒涘缓鍦板浘", description = "鍒濆鍖栦竴涓柊鍦板浘锛堝惈鍩虹淇℃伅锛?)
    public Result<Boolean> createMap(@Valid MapCreateDTO dto) {
        MapData mapData = new MapData();
        mapData.setName(dto.getName());
        mapData.setDescription(dto.getDescription());
        mapData.setFloor(dto.getFloor());
        mapData.setVersion("1.0.0");
        mapData.setStatus(0); // 榛樿鏈彂甯?
        boolean result = mapService.createMapWithImage(mapData, dto.getBaseImage());
        return Result.success(result ? "鍦板浘鍒涘缓鎴愬姛" : "鍦板浘鍒涘缓澶辫触", result);
    }

    @PutMapping("/{id}")

    public Result<Boolean> updateMap(

            @RequestBody @Valid MapUpdateDTO dto) {
        MapData mapData = new MapData();
        mapData.setId(id);

        mapData.setDescription(dto.getDescription());
        mapData.setFloor(dto.getFloor());
        mapData.setVersion(dto.getVersion());
        mapData.setStatus(dto.getStatus());
        boolean result = mapService.updateById(mapData);

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\controller\app\AppLocationController.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.controller.app;

import com.example.supermarket2.common.exception.BusinessException;
import com.example.supermarket2.common.result.ErrorCode;
import com.example.supermarket2.common.result.Result;
import com.example.supermarket2.dto.app.request.AppLocationCurrentQuery;
import com.example.supermarket2.dto.app.request.AppLocationHistoryQuery;
import com.example.supermarket2.dto.location.BeaconRequest;
import com.example.supermarket2.dto.location.LocationResult;
import com.example.supermarket2.entity.location.UserLocation;
import com.example.supermarket2.service.location.BluetoothLocationService;
import com.example.supermarket2.service.location.UserLocationService;
import io.swagger.v3.oas.annotations.Operation;
import io.swagger.v3.oas.annotations.tags.Tag;
import jakarta.validation.Valid;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.validation.annotation.Validated;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;

import java.util.Date;

/**
 * 瀹氫綅鎺ュ彛鎺у埗鍣?
 * 鏁村悎钃濈墮瀹氫綅鍜屼綅缃煡璇㈠姛鑳?
 */
@Slf4j
@Validated // 绫荤骇鍒牎楠屾敞瑙ｏ紝閰嶅悎鏂规硶鍙傛暟@Valid浣跨敤
@RestController
@RequestMapping("/app/location")
@Tag(name = "APP瀹氫綅绠＄悊", description = "绉诲姩绔鍐呰摑鐗欏畾浣嶇浉鍏虫帴鍙?)
@RequiredArgsConstructor // 鏇挎崲@Autowired锛屼娇鐢ㄦ瀯閫犲櫒娉ㄥ叆锛堜紒涓氱骇鏈€浣冲疄璺碉級
public class AppLocationController {

    private final BluetoothLocationService bluetoothLocationService;
    private final UserLocationService userLocationService;

    /**
     * 钃濈墮瀹氫綅鎺ュ彛
     * 澶勭悊钃濈墮淇℃爣鏁版嵁骞惰繑鍥炲畾浣嶇粨鏋?
     * 銆愬師鏈夊悎瑙勬帴鍙ｏ紝淇濈暀涓嶅彉銆?
     */
    @PostMapping("/bluetooth")
    @Operation(summary = "钃濈墮瀹氫綅", description = "涓婁紶钃濈墮淇℃爣鏁版嵁锛岃绠楀苟杩斿洖鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆")
    public Result<LocationResult> bluetoothLocation(@RequestBody @Valid BeaconRequest request) {
        log.info("鏀跺埌钃濈墮瀹氫綅璇锋眰: userId={}, mapId={}, 淇℃爣鏁伴噺={}",
                request.getUserId(), request.getMapId(),
                request.getBeacons() != null ? request.getBeacons().size() : 0);
        // 1. 澶勭悊瀹氫綅璇锋眰锛圫ervice灞傝嫢鍑洪敊鐩存帴鎶涘嚭BusinessException锛?
        LocationResult result = bluetoothLocationService.processBeaconData(request);
        // 2. 涓氬姟閫昏緫鏍￠獙锛氬畾浣嶅け璐ュ垯鎶涘嚭寮傚父
        if(!result.isSuccess()) {
            throw new BusinessException(ErrorCode.LOCATION_FAILED, result.getMessage());
        }
        if(!result.isValidPosition()){
            throw new BusinessException(ErrorCode.LOCATION_FAILED, "瀹氫綅鍧愭爣鏃犳晥");
        }
        // 3. 鏇存柊鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆鍒版暟鎹簱
        updateUserLocation(request, result);
        log.debug("瀹氫綅鎴愬姛骞舵洿鏂扮敤鎴蜂綅缃? ({}, {})", result.getX(), result.getY());
        return Result.success(result);
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鐢ㄦ埛褰撳墠浣嶇疆
     * 銆愭敼閫犵偣銆戯細鍏ュ弬灏佽涓篋TO锛屾坊鍔爑serId/mapId闀垮害鏍￠獙
     */
    @GetMapping("/current")
    @Operation(summary = "鑾峰彇褰撳墠浣嶇疆", description = "鏌ヨ鐢ㄦ埛鏈€鏂扮殑瀹氫綅璁板綍")
    public Result<UserLocation> getCurrentLocation(@Valid AppLocationCurrentQuery query) {
        log.debug("鏌ヨ鐢ㄦ埛褰撳墠浣嶇疆: userId={}, mapId={}", query.getUserId(), query.getMapId());
        UserLocation location = userLocationService.getLatestUserLocation(query.getUserId(), query.getMapId());
        if (location == null) {
            throw new BusinessException(ErrorCode.USER_LOCATION_NOT_FOUND);
        }
        return Result.success(location);
    }

    /**
     * 鏇存柊鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆锛堝師UserLocationController鍔熻兘锛?
     * 銆愬師鏈夊悎瑙勬帴鍙ｏ紝淇濈暀涓嶅彉銆?
     */
    @PostMapping("/update")
    @Operation(summary = "鏇存柊浣嶇疆", description = "鎵嬪姩鏇存柊鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆淇℃伅")
    public Result<String> updateUserLocation(@RequestBody @Valid UserLocation location) {
        log.debug("鏇存柊鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆: userId={}, mapId={}, position=({}, {})",
                location.getUserId(), location.getMapId(), location.getX(), location.getY());
        // 璁剧疆鏃堕棿鎴?
        if (location.getTimeStamp() == null) {
            location.setTimeStamp(new Date());
        }
        userLocationService.updateUserLocation(location);
        return Result.success("鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆鏇存柊鎴愬姛");
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆鍘嗗彶
     * 銆愭敼閫犵偣銆戯細鍏ュ弬灏佽涓篋TO锛屾坊鍔爑serId/mapId闀垮害鏍￠獙+limit鑼冨洿鏍￠獙
     */
    @GetMapping("/history")
    @Operation(summary = "鑾峰彇浣嶇疆鍘嗗彶", description = "鏌ヨ鐢ㄦ埛鐨勫巻鍙插畾浣嶈建杩?)
    public Result<Object> getLocationHistory(@Valid AppLocationHistoryQuery query) {
        log.debug("鏌ヨ鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆鍘嗗彶: userId={}, mapId={}, limit={}", query.getUserId(), query.getMapId(), query.getLimit());
        // 杩欓噷鍙互璋冪敤UserLocationService鐨勬墿灞曟柟娉曡幏鍙栧巻鍙茶褰?
        // 鏆傛椂鎶涘嚭涓氬姟寮傚父鎻愮ず寰呭疄鐜?
        throw new BusinessException(ErrorCode.RESOURCE_NOT_FOUND, "浣嶇疆鍘嗗彶鏌ヨ鍔熻兘寰呭疄鐜?);
    }

    /**
     * 鏇存柊鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆鍒版暟鎹簱
     * 銆愮鏈夋柟娉曪紝淇濈暀鍘熸湁閫昏緫銆?
     */
    private void updateUserLocation(BeaconRequest request, LocationResult result) {
        UserLocation userLocation = new UserLocation();
        userLocation.setUserId(request.getUserId());
        userLocation.setMapId(request.getMapId());
        userLocation.setX(result.getX().intValue());
        userLocation.setY(result.getY().intValue());
        userLocation.setTimeStamp(new Date());
        userLocationService.updateUserLocation(userLocation);
    }
}

package com.example.supermarket2.controller.app;

import com.example.supermarket2.common.exception.BusinessException;
import com.example.supermarket2.common.result.Result;
import com.example.supermarket2.dto.app.request.AppMapDataQuery;

import io.swagger.v3.oas.annotations.Operation;
import io.swagger.v3.oas.annotations.tags.Tag;
import jakarta.validation.Valid;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;

import java.util.List;

@Slf4j
@Validated // 绫荤骇鍒牎楠屾敞瑙ｏ紝閰嶅悎鏂规硶鍙傛暟@Valid浣跨敤
@RestController
@RequestMapping("/app/map")
@Tag(name = "APP鍦板浘绠＄悊", description = "绉诲姩绔湴鍥炬暟鎹浉鍏虫帴鍙?)
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class AppMapController {

    private final MapGridService mapGridService;

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鍦板浘缃戞牸鏁版嵁
     * 鏀归€犵偣锛氬叆鍙傚皝瑁呬负DTO锛屾坊鍔爉apId闀垮害鏍￠獙
     */
    @GetMapping("/data")
    @Operation(summary = "鑾峰彇鍦板浘缃戞牸鏁版嵁", description = "鏍规嵁鍦板浘ID鑾峰彇瀹屾暣鍦板浘缃戞牸鏁版嵁")
    public Result<List<MapGrid>> getMapData(@Valid AppMapDataQuery query) {
        log.debug("璇锋眰鍦板浘鏁版嵁: mapId={}", query.getMapId());
        List<MapGrid> gridList = mapGridService.getMapGridByMapId(query.getMapId());
        if (gridList.isEmpty()) {
            log.warn("鏈壘鍒板湴鍥炬暟鎹? mapId={}", query.getMapId());
            throw new BusinessException(ErrorCode.MAP_NOT_FOUND);
        }
        log.debug("杩斿洖鍦板浘鏁版嵁: mapId={}, 缃戞牸鏁伴噺={}", query.getMapId(), gridList.size());
        return Result.success(gridList);
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鍙€氳鍦板浘鏁版嵁
     * 鏀归€犵偣锛氬叆鍙傚皝瑁呬负DTO锛屾坊鍔爉apId闀垮害鏍￠獙
     */
    @GetMapping("/passable")
    @Operation(summary = "鑾峰彇鍙€氳鍦板浘鏁版嵁", description = "鏍规嵁鍦板浘ID鑾峰彇鍙€氳鐨勭綉鏍兼暟鎹?)
    public Result<List<MapGrid>> getPassableMapData(@Valid AppMapDataQuery query) {
        log.debug("璇锋眰鍙€氳鍦板浘鏁版嵁: mapId={}", query.getMapId());
        List<MapGrid> gridList = mapGridService.getMapGridByMapId(query.getMapId());
        // 杩囨护鍙€氳缃戞牸
        List<MapGrid> passableGrids = gridList.stream()
                .filter(grid -> grid.getPassable() == 1)
                .toList();
        if (passableGrids.isEmpty()) {
            log.warn("鏈壘鍒板彲閫氳鍦板浘鏁版嵁: mapId={}", query.getMapId());
            throw new BusinessException(ErrorCode.NO_PASSABLE_PATH);
        }
        log.debug("杩斿洖鍙€氳鍦板浘鏁版嵁: mapId={}, 鍙€氳缃戞牸鏁伴噺={}", query.getMapId(), passableGrids.size());
        return Result.success(passableGrids);
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ヤ綅缃槸鍚﹀彲閫氳
     * 鏀归€犵偣锛氬叆鍙傚皝瑁呬负DTO锛屾坊鍔爉apId闀垮害鏍￠獙+鍧愭爣鑼冨洿鏍￠獙
     */
    @GetMapping("/check-passable")
    @Operation(summary = "妫€鏌ヤ綅缃槸鍚﹀彲閫氳", description = "鏍￠獙鎸囧畾鍧愭爣鍦ㄥ搴斿湴鍥句腑鏄惁鍙€氳")
    public Result<Boolean> checkPositionPassable(@Valid AppMapPassableCheckQuery query) {
        log.debug("妫€鏌ヤ綅缃彲閫氳鎬? mapId={}, position=({}, {})", query.getMapId(), query.getX(), query.getY());
        boolean isPassable = mapGridService.isPositionPassable(query.getMapId(), query.getX(), query.getY());
        log.debug("浣嶇疆鍙€氳鎬ф鏌ョ粨鏋? mapId={}, position=({}, {}), passable={}",
                query.getMapId(), query.getX(), query.getY(), isPassable);
        return Result.success(isPassable);
    }
}

package com.example.supermarket2.controller.app;

import com.example.supermarket2.common.exception.BusinessException;
import com.example.supermarket2.common.result.ErrorCode;
import com.example.supermarket2.common.result.Result;
import com.example.supermarket2.dto.location.NavigationRequest;
import com.example.supermarket2.dto.location.NavigationResponse;
import com.example.supermarket2.service.location.NavigationService;
import io.swagger.v3.oas.annotations.Operation;
import io.swagger.v3.oas.annotations.tags.Tag;
import jakarta.validation.Valid;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.validation.annotation.Validated;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PostMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestBody;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;

/**
 * 瀵艰埅鎺ュ彛鎺у埗鍣?
 * 澶勭悊瀹ゅ唴璺緞瑙勫垝璇锋眰
 */
@Slf4j
@Validated
@RestController
@RequestMapping("/app/navigation") // 缁熶竴APP鍓嶇紑
@Tag(name = "APP瀵艰埅绠＄悊", description = "绉诲姩绔鍐呰矾寰勮鍒掔浉鍏虫帴鍙?)
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class AppNavigationController {

    private final NavigationService navigationService;

    /**
     * 澧炲己璺緞瑙勫垝鎺ュ彛
     * 璁＄畻浠庤捣鐐瑰埌缁堢偣鐨勬渶浼樿矾寰勶紝鏀寔涓嶅彲閫氳鐩爣鐐硅嚜鍔ㄨ皟鏁村埌鏈€杩戝彲閫氳鐐?
     */
    @PostMapping("/path")
    @Operation(summary = "澧炲己璺緞瑙勫垝", description = "璁＄畻浠庤捣鐐瑰埌缁堢偣鐨勬渶浼樿矾寰勶紝鏀寔涓嶅彲閫氳鐩爣鐐硅嚜鍔ㄨ皟鏁村埌鏈€杩戝彲閫氳鐐?)
    public Result<NavigationResponse> calculatePath(@RequestBody @Valid NavigationRequest request) {
        log.info("鏀跺埌澧炲己璺緞瑙勫垝璇锋眰: mapId={}, start=({}, {}), end=({}, {})",
                request.getMapId(), request.getStartX(), request.getStartY(),
                request.getEndX(), request.getEndY());

        // 鎵ц澧炲己璺緞瑙勫垝
        NavigationResponse response = navigationService.calculateEnhancedPath(request);

        if (response.isSuccess()) {
            log.info("澧炲己璺緞瑙勫垝鎴愬姛锛氳矾寰勯暱搴?{}, 璋冩暣鐩爣={}",
                    response.getDistance(), response.getTargetAdjusted());
            return Result.success(response);
        } else {
            log.warn("澧炲己璺緞瑙勫垝澶辫触锛歿}", response.getMessage());
            throw new BusinessException(ErrorCode.PATH_PLAN_FAILED, response.getMessage());
        }
    }
}

package com.example.supermarket2.controller.app;

import com.example.supermarket2.common.result.Result;
import com.example.supermarket2.dto.app.request.AppSearchHistoryQuery;

import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;

@Slf4j
@Validated
@RestController
@RequestMapping("/app/search")
@Tag(name = "APP鎼滅储绠＄悊", description = "绉诲姩绔晢鍝佹悳绱€佹悳绱㈠巻鍙茬浉鍏虫帴鍙?)

     */
    @GetMapping("/suggest")
    @Operation(summary = "鎼滅储寤鸿", description = "鏍规嵁鍏抽敭璇嶆ā绯婃悳绱㈠晢鍝佸苟鑷姩淇濆瓨鎼滅储鍘嗗彶锛堝幓閲嶏級")
    public Result<List<SearchResultDto>> searchSuggest(@Valid AppSearchSuggestQuery query) {
        log.debug("璇锋眰鎼滅储寤鸿: userId={}, keyword={}", query.getUserId(), query.getKeyword());
        List<SearchResultDto> results = searchService.searchProducts(query.getKeyword().trim());
        searchService.saveSearchHistory(query.getUserId(), query.getKeyword().trim());
        log.debug("杩斿洖鎼滅储寤鸿锛屾暟閲?{}", results.size());
        return Result.success(results);
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鐑棬鎼滅储鍏抽敭璇?
     * 鍘熸湁鍚堣鎺ュ彛锛屼粎琛ュ厖鏃ュ織
     */
    @GetMapping("/hot")
    @Operation(summary = "鑾峰彇鐑棬鎼滅储鍏抽敭璇?, description = "鑾峰彇鎸夋悳绱㈡鏁伴檷搴忔帓鍒楃殑鍓?0涓儹闂ㄦ悳绱㈠叧閿瘝")
    public Result<List<String>> getHotKeywords() {
        log.debug("璇锋眰鑾峰彇鐑棬鎼滅储鍏抽敭璇?);
        List<String> hotKeywords = searchService.getHotKeywords();
        log.debug("杩斿洖鐑棬鎼滅储鍏抽敭璇嶏紝鏁伴噺={}", hotKeywords.size());
        return Result.success(hotKeywords);
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鎼滅储鍘嗗彶
     * 鏀归€犵偣锛氬叆鍙傚皝瑁呬负DTO锛屾坊鍔爑serId姝ｆ暣鏁版牎楠?
     */
    @GetMapping("/history")
    @Operation(summary = "鑾峰彇鎼滅储鍘嗗彶", description = "鑾峰彇鎸囧畾鐢ㄦ埛鎸夋悳绱㈡椂闂撮檷搴忔帓鍒楃殑鍓?0鏉℃悳绱㈠巻鍙诧紙鍘婚噸锛?)
    public Result<List<String>> getSearchHistory(@Valid AppSearchHistoryQuery query) {
        log.debug("璇锋眰鑾峰彇鎼滅储鍘嗗彶: userId={}", query.getUserId());
        List<String> history = searchService.getSearchHistory(query.getUserId());
        log.debug("杩斿洖鎼滅储鍘嗗彶锛屾暟閲?{}", history.size());
        return Result.success(history);
    }

    /**

     * 鏀归€犵偣锛氬叆鍙傚皝瑁呬负DTO锛屾坊鍔爑serId姝ｆ暣鏁版牎楠?
     */
    @GetMapping("/clear")
    @Operation(summary = "娓呯┖鎼滅储鍘嗗彶", description = "娓呯┖鎸囧畾鐢ㄦ埛鐨勬墍鏈夋悳绱㈠巻鍙茶褰?)
    public Result<Void> clearSearchHistory(@Valid AppSearchHistoryQuery query) {
        log.debug("璇锋眰娓呯┖鎼滅储鍘嗗彶: userId={}", query.getUserId());
        searchService.clearSearchHistory(query.getUserId());
        log.debug("娓呯┖鎼滅储鍘嗗彶鎴愬姛: userId={}", query.getUserId());
        return Result.success();
    }

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\domain\cart\CartDomainService.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.domain.cart;

import com.example.supermarket2.dto.app.response.CartItemDto;
import com.example.supermarket2.entity.Product;
import com.example.supermarket2.infra.redis.model.RedisCartItem;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Component
public class CartDomainService {

    // 鍒ゆ柇鍟嗗搧鏄惁瀛樺湪涓斾笂鏋?
    public boolean isProductAvailable(Product product) {
        return product != null && product.getStatus() == 1;
    }

    // 鏇存柊璐墿杞﹁鏁板晢鍝佺殑鏁伴噺
    public RedisCartItem updateCartItem(RedisCartItem cartItem, Integer quantity) {
        cartItem.setQuantity(cartItem.getQuantity() + quantity);
        cartItem.setUpdateTime(System.currentTimeMillis());
        return cartItem;
    }

    // 鏂板璁℃暟鍟嗗搧鍒拌喘鐗╄溅
    public RedisCartItem addCartItem(Long productId, Integer quantity) {
        RedisCartItem newItem = new RedisCartItem();
        newItem.setProductId(productId);
        newItem.setQuantity(quantity);
        newItem.setSelected(true);
        newItem.setCreateTime(System.currentTimeMillis());
        newItem.setUpdateTime(System.currentTimeMillis());
        return newItem;
    }

    // 鏇存柊璐墿杞︾О閲嶅晢鍝佺殑鏁伴噺
    public RedisCartItem updateCartItem(RedisCartItem cartItem, Double weightInKg) {
        cartItem.setWeight(cartItem.getWeight() + weightInKg);
        cartItem.setUpdateTime(System.currentTimeMillis());
        return cartItem;
    }

    // 鏂板绉伴噸鍟嗗搧鍒拌喘鐗╄溅
    public RedisCartItem addCartItem(Long productId, Double weightInKg) {
        RedisCartItem newItem = new RedisCartItem();
        newItem.setProductId(productId);
        newItem.setWeight(weightInKg);
        newItem.setSelected(true);
        newItem.setCreateTime(System.currentTimeMillis());
        newItem.setUpdateTime(System.currentTimeMillis());
        return newItem;
    }

    // 鍒ゆ柇璐墿杞︽槸鍚︿负绌?
    public boolean isCartEmpty(Long size) {
        if(size != null && size == 0){
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }

    /**
     * 灏哛edis涓殑璐墿杞﹂」鍜屽晢鍝佷俊鎭浆鎹负CartItemDto
     */
    public CartItemDto convertToDto(RedisCartItem redisCartItem, Product product) {
        CartItemDto dto = new CartItemDto();
        dto.setId(redisCartItem.getProductId()); // 浣跨敤productId浣滀负涓存椂ID
        dto.setProductId(redisCartItem.getProductId());
        dto.setQuantity(redisCartItem.getQuantity());
        dto.setWeight(redisCartItem.getWeight());
        dto.setSelected(redisCartItem.getSelected());

        // 璁剧疆鍟嗗搧淇℃伅
        dto.setName(product.getName());
        dto.setPrice(product.getPrice());

        if (product.getImages() != null && !product.getImages().isEmpty()) {
            dto.setImage(product.getImages().get(0));
        }

        return dto;
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\dto\location\BeaconData.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.dto.location;

import jakarta.validation.constraints.NotNull;
import jakarta.validation.constraints.Pattern;
import lombok.Data;

/**
 * 淇℃爣鏁版嵁DTO
 * 灏佽淇℃爣UUID銆丷SSI銆佽窛绂荤瓑淇℃伅
 */
@Data
public class BeaconData {
    @NotNull(message = "淇℃爣UUID涓嶈兘涓虹┖")
    @Pattern(regexp = "^[0-9a-fA-F-]{32,36}$", message = "淇℃爣UUID鏍煎紡鏃犳晥")
    private String uuid;            // 淇℃爣UUID

    @NotNull(message = "淇″彿寮哄害涓嶈兘涓虹┖")
    private Integer rssi;           // RSSI淇″彿寮哄害
    private Double distance;        // 璁＄畻璺濈
    private Long timestamp;         // 鏃堕棿鎴?
    private String macAddress;      // MAC鍦板潃锛堝彲閫夛級
    private Integer txPower;        // 鍙戝皠鍔熺巼锛堝彲閫夛級
    private Boolean isValid = true; // 鏁版嵁鏄惁鏈夋晥

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇瑙勮寖鍖朥UID
     */
    public String getNormalizedUuid() {
        if (uuid == null) return null;
        return uuid.toLowerCase().replace("-", "");
    }

    /**
     * 楠岃瘉淇℃爣鏁版嵁鐨勬湁鏁堟€?
     */
    public boolean isValidBeacon() {
        return uuid != null && !uuid.trim().isEmpty() &&
                rssi != null && rssi < 0 && rssi >= -95;
    }
}


========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\dto\location\BeaconRequest.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.dto.location;

import jakarta.validation.Valid;
import jakarta.validation.constraints.NotBlank;
import jakarta.validation.constraints.NotEmpty;
import jakarta.validation.constraints.NotNull;
import lombok.Data;

import java.util.List;

/**
 * 瀹氫綅璇锋眰DTO
 * 灏佽瀹氫綅璇锋眰鍙傛暟
 */
@Data
public class BeaconRequest {

    @NotBlank(message = "鐢ㄦ埛ID涓嶈兘涓虹┖")
    private String userId;                   // 鐢ㄦ埛ID

    @NotBlank(message = "鍦板浘ID涓嶈兘涓虹┖")
    private String mapId;                    // 鍦板浘ID
    private String sessionId;                // 浼氳瘽ID锛堝彲閫夛級

    @NotNull(message = "淇℃爣鏁版嵁涓嶈兘涓虹┖")
    @NotEmpty(message = "淇℃爣鏁版嵁涓嶈兘涓虹┖")
    @Valid // 绾ц仈鏍￠獙BeaconData鍐呴儴瀛楁
    private List<BeaconData> beacons;        // 淇℃爣鏁版嵁鍒楄〃

    private Long timestamp;                  // 瀹㈡埛绔椂闂存埑
    private String deviceId;                 // 璁惧ID
    private Double lastKnownX;               // 涓婃宸茬煡浣嶇疆X
    private Double lastKnownY;               // 涓婃宸茬煡浣嶇疆Y

    /**
     * 楠岃瘉璇锋眰鏈夋晥鎬?
     */
    public boolean isValid() {
        return userId != null && !userId.trim().isEmpty() &&
                mapId != null && !mapId.trim().isEmpty() &&
                beacons != null && !beacons.isEmpty();
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鏈夋晥淇℃爣鏁伴噺
     */
    public int getValidBeaconCount() {
        if (beacons == null) return 0;
        return (int) beacons.stream()
                .filter(BeaconData::isValidBeacon)
                .count();
    }
}


========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\dto\location\LocationQualityDTO.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.dto.location;

import com.example.supermarket2.entity.location.LocationQuality;
import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Builder;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;

/**
 * 瀹氫綅璐ㄩ噺浼犺緭瀵硅薄
 * 鐢ㄤ簬浼犺緭瀹氫綅璐ㄩ噺鐨勮缁嗕俊鎭?
 */
@Data
@Builder
@NoArgsConstructor
@AllArgsConstructor
public class LocationQualityDTO {
    private String level;           // 璐ㄩ噺绛夌骇
    private Double score;           // 璐ㄩ噺鍒嗘暟
    private Integer beaconCount;    // 淇℃爣鏁伴噺
    private Double avgRSSI;         // 骞冲潎RSSI
    private Double stability;       // 绋冲畾鎬?
    private Double confidence;      // 缃俊搴?
    private String algorithm;       // 浣跨敤绠楁硶
    private String description;     // 璐ㄩ噺鎻忚堪

    /**
     * 浠庡疄浣撶被杞崲
     */
    public static LocationQualityDTO fromEntity(LocationQuality quality) {
        if (quality == null) return null;

        return LocationQualityDTO.builder()
                .level(quality.getLevel().name())
                .score(quality.getScore())
                .beaconCount(quality.getBeaconCount())
                .avgRSSI(quality.getAvgRSSI())
                .stability(quality.getStability())
                .confidence(quality.getConfidence())
                .algorithm(quality.getAlgorithm())
                .description(generateDescription(quality))
                .build();
    }

    /**
     * 鐢熸垚璐ㄩ噺鎻忚堪
     */
    private static String generateDescription(LocationQuality quality) {
        if (quality == null) return "鏈煡璐ㄩ噺";

        switch (quality.getLevel()) {
            case HIGH:
                return String.format("楂樿川閲忓畾浣嶏紙%d涓俊鏍囷紝骞冲潎RSSI: %.1f锛?,
                        quality.getBeaconCount(), quality.getAvgRSSI());
            case MEDIUM:
                return String.format("涓瓑璐ㄩ噺瀹氫綅锛?d涓俊鏍囷紝骞冲潎RSSI: %.1f锛?,
                        quality.getBeaconCount(), quality.getAvgRSSI());
            case LOW:
                return String.format("浣庤川閲忓畾浣嶏紙%d涓俊鏍囷紝骞冲潎RSSI: %.1f锛?,
                        quality.getBeaconCount(), quality.getAvgRSSI());
            case POOR:
                return "淇″彿璐ㄩ噺杈冨樊锛屽畾浣嶅彲鑳戒笉鍑嗙‘";
            case PREDICTED:
                return "鍩轰簬杩愬姩妯″瀷鐨勯娴嬩綅缃?;
            default:
                return "鏈煡瀹氫綅璐ㄩ噺";
        }
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚︿负楂樿川閲忓畾浣?
     */
    public boolean isHighQuality() {
        return "HIGH".equals(level) && score != null && score >= 0.8;
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚︿负鍙潬瀹氫綅
     */
    public boolean isReliable() {
        return !"POOR".equals(level) && confidence != null && confidence >= 0.5;
    }
}


========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\dto\location\LocationResult.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.dto.location;

import com.example.supermarket2.entity.location.LocationQuality;
import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Builder;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;

import java.util.Map;

/**
 * 瀹氫綅缁撴灉DTO
 * 灏佽瀹氫綅鍧愭爣銆佽川閲忋€佺姸鎬佺瓑淇℃伅
 */
@Data
@Builder
@NoArgsConstructor
@AllArgsConstructor
public class LocationResult {
    private Double x;                           // X鍧愭爣
    private Double y;                           // Y鍧愭爣
    private String quality;                     // 璐ㄩ噺绛夌骇
    private Integer beaconCount;                // 淇℃爣鏁伴噺
    private Long timestamp;                     // 鏃堕棿鎴?
    private Boolean success;                    // 鏄惁鎴愬姛
    private String message;                     // 娑堟伅
    private String algorithm;                   // 浣跨敤鐨勭畻娉?
    private Double confidence;                  // 缃俊搴?
    private LocationQuality detailedQuality;    // 璇︾粏璐ㄩ噺淇℃伅
    private Map<String, Object> metadata;       // 鍏冩暟鎹?

    /**
     * 鏋勫缓鎴愬姛瀹氫綅缁撴灉
     */
    public static LocationResult success(Double x, Double y, String quality,
                                         Integer beaconCount, String algorithm,
                                         Double confidence, LocationQuality detailedQuality) {
        return LocationResult.builder()
                .x(x)
                .y(y)
                .quality(quality)
                .beaconCount(beaconCount)
                .timestamp(System.currentTimeMillis())
                .success(true)
                .algorithm(algorithm)
                .confidence(confidence)
                .detailedQuality(detailedQuality)
                .build();
    }

    /**
     * 鏋勫缓澶辫触瀹氫綅缁撴灉
     */
    public static LocationResult error(String message) {
        return LocationResult.builder()
                .success(false)
                .message(message)
                .timestamp(System.currentTimeMillis())
                .build();
    }

    /**
     * 鏋勫缓棰勬祴瀹氫綅缁撴灉
     */
    public static LocationResult predicted(Double x, Double y, Double confidence) {
        return LocationResult.builder()
                .x(x)
                .y(y)
                .quality("predicted")
                .timestamp(System.currentTimeMillis())
                .success(true)
                .algorithm("prediction")
                .confidence(confidence)
                .build();
    }

    public boolean isSuccess() {
        return Boolean.TRUE.equals(success);
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ヤ綅缃槸鍚︽湁鏁?
     */
    public boolean isValidPosition() {
        return success && x != null && y != null &&
                !x.isNaN() && !y.isNaN() &&
                x >= 0 && x <= 100 &&
                y >= 0 && y <= 100;
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\dto\location\NavigationResponse.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.dto.location;

import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;

import java.util.List;

@Data
@NoArgsConstructor
@AllArgsConstructor
public class NavigationResponse {
    private boolean success;
    private String message;
    private List<GridPoint> path;
    private Double distance;
    private GridPoint originalTarget;   // 鍘熷鐩爣鐐?
    private GridPoint adjustedTarget;   // 璋冩暣鍚庣殑鐩爣鐐癸紙濡傛灉鍘熷鐩爣涓嶅彲閫氳锛屽垯璋冩暣鍒版渶杩戝彲閫氳鐐癸級
    private Boolean targetAdjusted;     // 娣诲姞杩欎釜瀛楁

    // GridPoint 绫?
    @Data
    @NoArgsConstructor
    public static class GridPoint {
        private int x;
        private int y;

        // 娣诲姞涓や釜鍙傛暟鐨勬瀯閫犲嚱鏁?
        public GridPoint(int x, int y) {
            this.x = x;
            this.y = y;
        }
    }

    // 鏋勫缓鎴愬姛鍝嶅簲鐨勬柟娉?- 閲嶈浇鐗堟湰锛屾敮鎸佹洿澶氬弬鏁?
    public static NavigationResponse success(List<GridPoint> path, double distance) {
        return success(path, distance, null, null, false);
    }

    public static NavigationResponse success(List<GridPoint> path, double distance,
                                             GridPoint originalTarget, GridPoint adjustedTarget,
                                             boolean targetAdjusted) {
        NavigationResponse response = new NavigationResponse();
        response.setSuccess(true);
        response.setPath(path);
        response.setDistance(distance);
        response.setOriginalTarget(originalTarget);
        response.setAdjustedTarget(adjustedTarget);
        response.setTargetAdjusted(targetAdjusted);
        return response;
    }

    // 鏋勫缓澶辫触鍝嶅簲鐨勬柟娉?
    public static NavigationResponse error(String message) {
        NavigationResponse response = new NavigationResponse();
        response.setSuccess(false);
        response.setMessage(message);
        response.setPath(List.of());
        response.setDistance(0.0);
        response.setTargetAdjusted(false);
        return response;
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\dto\ws\WebSocketMessage.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.dto.ws;

import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;

import java.io.Serializable;

/**
 * WebSocket 缁熶竴娑堟伅鍗忚
 * 鎵€鏈夊墠鍚庣浜や簰鐨勬秷鎭潎浣跨敤姝ょ粨鏋勶紝淇濊瘉鍗忚缁熶竴
 */
@Data
@NoArgsConstructor
@AllArgsConstructor
public class WebSocketMessage<T> implements Serializable {

    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;

    /**
     * 娑堟伅绫诲瀷锛堟牳蹇冨瓧娈碉紝鐢ㄤ簬娑堟伅鍒嗗彂锛?
     * 鍙€夊€硷細
     * - heartbeat锛氬績璺冲寘
     * - cart_update锛氳喘鐗╄溅鏁版嵁鏇存柊
     * - location_update锛氱敤鎴峰畾浣嶆洿鏂?
     * - navigation_update锛氬鑸矾寰勬洿鏂?
     * - device_data锛氭櫤鑳借澶囨暟鎹笂鎶?
     * - system_notice锛氱郴缁熼€氱煡
     * - error锛氶敊璇秷鎭?
     */
    private String type;

    /**
     * 娑堟伅浣擄紙涓氬姟鏁版嵁锛?
     */
    private T data;

    /**
     * 鏃堕棿鎴?
     */
    private Long timestamp;

    /**
     * 娑堟伅鍞竴ID锛堢敤浜庢秷鎭幓閲嶃€佺绾胯ˉ鍙戯級
     */
    private String messageId;

    /**
     * 鍝嶅簲鐮侊紙200鎴愬姛锛岄潪200澶辫触锛?
     */
    private Integer code;

    /**
     * 鍝嶅簲淇℃伅
     */
    private String message;

    // ========== 闈欐€佸揩鎹锋瀯寤烘柟娉?==========
    /**
     * 鏋勫缓鎴愬姛娑堟伅
     */
    public static <T> WebSocketMessage<T> success(String type, T data) {
        WebSocketMessage<T> message = new WebSocketMessage<>();
        message.setType(type);
        message.setData(data);
        message.setTimestamp(System.currentTimeMillis());
        message.setCode(200);
        message.setMessage("success");
        message.setMessageId(generateMessageId());
        return message;
    }

    /**
     * 鏋勫缓蹇冭烦娑堟伅
     */
    public static WebSocketMessage<Void> heartbeat() {
        WebSocketMessage<Void> message = new WebSocketMessage<>();
        message.setType("heartbeat");
        message.setTimestamp(System.currentTimeMillis());
        message.setCode(200);
        message.setMessage("pong");
        return message;
    }

    /**
     * 鏋勫缓閿欒娑堟伅
     */
    public static WebSocketMessage<Void> error(String message) {
        WebSocketMessage<Void> wsMessage = new WebSocketMessage<>();
        wsMessage.setType("error");
        wsMessage.setTimestamp(System.currentTimeMillis());
        wsMessage.setCode(500);
        wsMessage.setMessage(message);
        wsMessage.setMessageId(generateMessageId());
        return wsMessage;
    }

    /**
     * 鐢熸垚娑堟伅鍞竴ID
     */
    private static String generateMessageId() {
        return System.currentTimeMillis() + "_" + (int) (Math.random() * 10000);
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\entity\location\BeaconConfig.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.entity.location;

import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
import org.springframework.boot.context.properties.ConfigurationProperties;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

/**
 * 淇℃爣閰嶇疆鍙傛暟瀹炰綋
 * 瀛樺偍淇℃爣瀹氫綅绯荤粺鐨勯厤缃弬鏁?
 */
@Data
@NoArgsConstructor
@AllArgsConstructor
@Component
@ConfigurationProperties(prefix = "beacon.config")
public class BeaconConfig {
    // RSSI鐩稿叧閰嶇疆
    private Double rssi0 = -55.0;                   // 鍙傝€冭窛绂籖SSI鍊?
    private Double attenuationFactor = 3.2;         // 璺緞鎹熻€楁寚鏁?
    private Integer rssiMin = -95;                  // 鏈€灏忔湁鏁圧SSI
    private Integer rssiMax = -35;                  // 鏈€澶ф湁鏁圧SSI

    // 婊ゆ尝閰嶇疆
    private Integer historySize = 10;               // 鍘嗗彶鏁版嵁澶у皬
    private Double outlierThreshold = 3.0;          // 閲庡€兼娴嬮槇鍊?
    private Double stabilityThreshold = 0.6;        // 绋冲畾鎬ч槇鍊?

    // 瀹氫綅绠楁硶閰嶇疆
    private Double kalmanProcessNoise = 1.0;        // 鍗″皵鏇艰繃绋嬪櫔澹?
    private Double kalmanMeasurementNoise = 2.0;    // 鍗″皵鏇兼祴閲忓櫔澹?
    private Double maxMovementDistance = 5.0;       // 鏈€澶хЩ鍔ㄨ窛绂伙紙绫筹級

    // 璐ㄩ噺璇勪及閰嶇疆
    private Double highQualityRssiThreshold = -65.0;    // 楂樿川閲廟SSI闃堝€?
    private Double mediumQualityRssiThreshold = -70.0;  // 涓瓑璐ㄩ噺RSSI闃堝€?
    private Double lowQualityRssiThreshold = -75.0;     // 浣庤川閲廟SSI闃堝€?

    // 鏉冮噸閰嶇疆
    private Double rssiWeightExponent = 0.2;        // RSSI鏉冮噸鎸囨暟

    /**
     * 楠岃瘉閰嶇疆鍙傛暟鐨勬湁鏁堟€?
     */
    public boolean isValid() {
        return rssi0 != null && attenuationFactor != null &&
                rssiMin != null && rssiMax != null &&
                rssiMin < rssiMax && attenuationFactor > 0;
    }

    /**
     * 鏍规嵁RSSI璁＄畻鏉冮噸
     */
    public Double calculateWeight(Integer rssi) {
        if (rssi == null || rssi >= rssiMin) return 0.0;

        // 浣跨敤鎸囨暟鏉冮噸锛屼俊鍙疯秺寮烘潈閲嶈秺楂?
        return Math.pow(10, rssi * rssiWeightExponent / 10.0);
    }

    /**
     * 闄愬箙澶勭悊RSSI鍊?
     */
    public Integer clampRssi(Integer rssi) {
        if (rssi == null) return rssiMin;
        return Math.max(rssiMin, Math.min(rssiMax, rssi));
    }
}


========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\entity\location\BeaconLocation.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.entity.location;

import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;

/**
 * 淇℃爣浣嶇疆閰嶇疆瀹炰綋
 * 瀛樺偍淇℃爣UUID鍜屽潗鏍囦俊鎭?
 */
@Data
@NoArgsConstructor
@AllArgsConstructor
public class BeaconLocation {
    private String uuid;        // 淇℃爣UUID
    private Double x;           // X鍧愭爣
    private Double y;           // Y鍧愭爣
    private String name;        // 淇℃爣鍚嶇О锛堝彲閫夛級
    private Integer floor;      // 鎵€鍦ㄦゼ灞?
    private Double rssi0;       // 鍙傝€冭窛绂籖SSI鍊硷紙榛樿-55锛?
    private Double attenuation; // 琛板噺鍥犲瓙锛堥粯璁?.2锛?

    public BeaconLocation(String uuid, Double x, Double y) {
        this.uuid = uuid;
        this.x = x;
        this.y = y;
        this.rssi0 = -55.0;
        this.attenuation = 3.2;
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇瑙勮寖鍖朥UID锛堝幓闄ゆí鏉犲苟杞负灏忓啓锛?
     */
    public String getNormalizedUuid() {
        if (uuid == null) return null;
        return uuid.toLowerCase().replace("-", "");
    }

    /**
     * 鏍规嵁RSSI璁＄畻璺濈
     */
    public Double calculateDistance(Integer rssi) {
        if (rssi == null || rssi >= 0) return null;

        double refRssi = rssi0 != null ? rssi0 : -55.0;
        double n = attenuation != null ? attenuation : 3.2;

        // 浣跨敤瀵规暟璺緞鎹熻€楁ā鍨?
        return Math.pow(10, (refRssi - rssi) / (10 * n));
    }
}
