package com.example.supermarket2.entity.location;

import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;

/**
 * 瀹氫綅璐ㄩ噺璇勪及缁撴灉
 * 瀛樺偍绛夌骇銆佸垎鏁般€佷俊鏍囨暟閲忕瓑璐ㄩ噺淇℃伅
 */
@Data
@NoArgsConstructor
@AllArgsConstructor
public class LocationQuality {
    public enum QualityLevel {
        HIGH,       // 楂樿川閲忥細鈮?涓俊鏍囷紝RSSI > -65dBm
        MEDIUM,     // 涓瓑璐ㄩ噺锛氣墺2涓俊鏍囷紝RSSI > -70dBm
        LOW,        // 浣庤川閲忥細鈮?涓俊鏍囷紝RSSI > -75dBm
        POOR,       // 宸川閲忥細鍏朵粬鎯呭喌
        PREDICTED   // 棰勬祴浣嶇疆锛氫俊鍙蜂涪澶辨椂浣跨敤
    }

    private QualityLevel level;         // 璐ㄩ噺绛夌骇
    private Double score;               // 璐ㄩ噺鍒嗘暟锛?-1锛?
    private Integer beaconCount;        // 鏈夋晥淇℃爣鏁伴噺
    private Double avgRSSI;            // 骞冲潎RSSI鍊?
    private Double stability;           // 淇″彿绋冲畾鎬э紙0-1锛?
    private Double confidence;          // 缃俊搴︼紙0-1锛?
    private String algorithm;           // 浣跨敤鐨勫畾浣嶇畻娉?

    /**
     * 鏋勫缓楂樿川閲忓畾浣嶇粨鏋?
     */
    public static LocationQuality highQuality(int beaconCount, double avgRSSI, String algorithm) {
        return new LocationQuality(
                QualityLevel.HIGH,
                0.9,
                beaconCount,
                avgRSSI,
                0.8,
                0.85,
                algorithm
        );
    }

    /**
     * 鏋勫缓涓瓑璐ㄩ噺瀹氫綅缁撴灉
     */
    public static LocationQuality mediumQuality(int beaconCount, double avgRSSI, String algorithm) {
        return new LocationQuality(
                QualityLevel.MEDIUM,
                0.7,
                beaconCount,
                avgRSSI,
                0.6,
                0.6,
                algorithm
        );
    }

    /**
     * 鏋勫缓浣庤川閲忓畾浣嶇粨鏋?
     */
    public static LocationQuality lowQuality(int beaconCount, double avgRSSI, String algorithm) {
        return new LocationQuality(
                QualityLevel.LOW,
                0.5,
                beaconCount,
                avgRSSI,
                0.4,
                0.4,
                algorithm
        );
    }

    /**
     * 鏋勫缓宸川閲忓畾浣嶇粨鏋?
     */
    public static LocationQuality poorQuality() {
        return new LocationQuality(
                QualityLevel.POOR,
                0.2,
                0,
                -100.0,
                0.1,
                0.1,
                "conservative"
        );
    }

    /**
     * 鏋勫缓棰勬祴浣嶇疆璐ㄩ噺缁撴灉
     */
    public static LocationQuality predictedQuality() {
        return new LocationQuality(
                QualityLevel.PREDICTED,
                0.3,
                0,
                null,
                0.2,
                0.2,
                "prediction"
        );

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\entity\location\Position.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.entity.location;

import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;

/**
 * 浣嶇疆鍧愭爣瀹炰綋
 * 瀛樺偍鍧愭爣銆佺畻娉曠被鍨嬨€佽川閲忕瓑淇℃伅
 */
@Data
@NoArgsConstructor
@AllArgsConstructor
public class Position {
    private Double x;
    private Double y;
    private String algorithm;  // 浣跨敤鐨勫畾浣嶇畻娉曪細weighted_centroid, trilateration, conservative
    private String quality;    // 瀹氫綅璐ㄩ噺锛歨igh, medium, low, poor, predicted

    // 绠€鍖栨瀯閫犲嚱鏁?
    public Position(Double x, Double y) {
        this.x = x;
        this.y = y;
    }

    public Position(Double x, Double y, String algorithm) {
        this.x = x;
        this.y = y;
        this.algorithm = algorithm;
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ヤ綅缃槸鍚︽湁鏁?
     */
    public boolean isValid() {
        return x != null && y != null &&
                !x.isNaN() && !y.isNaN() &&
                x >= 0 && x <= 100 &&
                y >= 0 && y <= 100;
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻涓庡彟涓€涓綅缃殑璺濈
     */
    public double distanceTo(Position other) {
        if (other == null) return Double.MAX_VALUE;
        double dx = this.x - other.x;
        double dy = this.y - other.y;
        return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
    }
}


========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\entity\location\RssiHistory.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.entity.location;

import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

/**
 * RSSI淇″彿鍘嗗彶璁板綍
 * 瀛樺偍淇″彿鍊煎拰鏃堕棿鎴筹紝鐢ㄤ簬淇″彿鍒嗘瀽鍜屾护娉?
 */
@Data
@NoArgsConstructor
@AllArgsConstructor
public class RssiHistory {
    private Integer rssi;           // RSSI淇″彿鍊?
    private Long timestamp;         // 鏃堕棿鎴?
    private String beaconId;        // 淇℃爣ID
    private Boolean isValid = true; // 鏄惁鏈夋晥锛堢敤浜庨噹鍊兼娴嬶級

    public RssiHistory(Integer rssi, Long timestamp) {
        this.rssi = rssi;
        this.timestamp = timestamp;
    }

    /**
     * 浠庡巻鍙叉暟鎹垪琛ㄤ腑璁＄畻绉诲姩骞冲潎
     */
    public static Double calculateMovingAverage(List<RssiHistory> history, int windowSize) {
        if (history == null || history.isEmpty()) return null;

        int size = Math.min(windowSize, history.size());
        List<RssiHistory> recent = history.subList(history.size() - size, history.size());

        return recent.stream()
                .filter(RssiHistory::getIsValid)
                .mapToInt(RssiHistory::getRssi)
                .average()
                .orElse(Double.NaN);
    }

    /**
     * 浠庡巻鍙叉暟鎹腑妫€娴嬮噹鍊?
     */
    public static List<RssiHistory> detectOutliers(List<RssiHistory> history, double threshold) {
        if (history == null || history.size() < 3) {
            return new ArrayList<>();
        }

        List<RssiHistory> outliers = new ArrayList<>();
        List<Integer> values = history.stream()
                .map(RssiHistory::getRssi)
                .collect(ArrayList::new, ArrayList::add, ArrayList::addAll);

        // 璁＄畻涓綅鏁?
        values.sort(Integer::compareTo);
        int median = values.get(values.size() / 2);

        // 璁＄畻涓綅鏁扮粷瀵瑰亸宸?
        double mad = values.stream()
                .mapToInt(v -> Math.abs(v - median))
                .average()
                .orElse(0);

        // 妫€娴嬮噹鍊?
        for (RssiHistory record : history) {
            if (Math.abs(record.getRssi() - median) > threshold * mad) {
                outliers.add(record);
            }
        }

        return outliers;
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻淇″彿绋冲畾鎬э紙鏍囧噯宸€掓暟锛?
     */
    public static Double calculateStability(List<RssiHistory> history) {
        if (history == null || history.size() < 2) return 1.0;

        double mean = history.stream()
                .filter(RssiHistory::getIsValid)
                .mapToInt(RssiHistory::getRssi)
                .average()
                .orElse(0);

        double variance = history.stream()
                .filter(RssiHistory::getIsValid)
                .mapToDouble(h -> Math.pow(h.getRssi() - mean, 2))
                .average()
                .orElse(0);

        double stdDev = Math.sqrt(variance);

        // 鏍囧噯宸秺灏忥紝绋冲畾鎬ц秺楂?
        return 1.0 / (1.0 + stdDev);
    }
}


========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\entity\location\SignalQuality.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.entity.location;

import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;

/**
 * 淇″彿璐ㄩ噺璇勪及瀹炰綋
 * 瀛樺偍淇″彿绛夌骇銆佺ǔ瀹氭€х瓑淇℃伅
 */
@Data
@NoArgsConstructor
@AllArgsConstructor
public class SignalQuality {
    public enum Level {
        HIGH,   // 楂樿川閲忎俊鍙?
        MEDIUM, // 涓瓑璐ㄩ噺淇″彿
        LOW,    // 浣庤川閲忎俊鍙?
        POOR    // 宸川閲忎俊鍙?
    }

    private Level level;            // 淇″彿绛夌骇
    private Double avgRSSI;        // 骞冲潎RSSI鍊?
    private Double stability;      // 淇″彿绋冲畾鎬э紙0-1锛?
    private Integer validBeacons;  // 鏈夋晥淇℃爣鏁伴噺
    private Double confidence;     // 缃俊搴︼紙0-1锛?
    private Double variance;       // 淇″彿鏂瑰樊

    /**
     * 鏍规嵁淇″彿鍙傛暟璇勪及淇″彿璐ㄩ噺
     */
    public static SignalQuality assess(int beaconCount, double avgRSSI, double stability) {
        Level level;
        double confidence;

        if (beaconCount >= 3 && avgRSSI > -65 && stability > 0.7) {
            level = Level.HIGH;
            confidence = 0.8;
        } else if (beaconCount >= 2 && avgRSSI > -70 && stability > 0.5) {
            level = Level.MEDIUM;
            confidence = 0.6;
        } else if (beaconCount >= 1 && avgRSSI > -75) {
            level = Level.LOW;
            confidence = 0.4;
        } else {
            level = Level.POOR;
            confidence = 0.2;
        }

        return new SignalQuality(level, avgRSSI, stability, beaconCount, confidence, 0.0);
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚﹂€傚悎涓夎瀹氫綅
     */
    public boolean isSuitableForTrilateration() {
        return level == Level.HIGH && validBeacons >= 3;
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚﹂€傚悎鍔犳潈璐ㄥ績瀹氫綅
     */
    public boolean isSuitableForWeightedCentroid() {
        return level == Level.HIGH || level == Level.MEDIUM;
    }
}

package com.example.supermarket2.entity;

import com.baomidou.mybatisplus.annotation.IdType;
import com.baomidou.mybatisplus.annotation.TableField;
import com.baomidou.mybatisplus.annotation.TableId;
import com.baomidou.mybatisplus.annotation.TableName;
import com.example.supermarket2.handler.ListStringTypeHandler;
import lombok.Data;

import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.util.Date;
import java.util.List;

@Data
@TableName(value = "product", autoResultMap = true) // 銆愬叧閿€戝繀椤诲姞 autoResultMap = true
public class Product {
    @TableId(type = IdType.AUTO)
    private Long id;
    private String name;
    private String description;

    // 鎸囧畾瀛楁浣跨敤鑷畾涔夌被鍨嬪鐞嗗櫒
    @TableField(typeHandler = ListStringTypeHandler.class)
    private List<String> images;

    @TableField(typeHandler = ListStringTypeHandler.class)
    private List<String> detailImages;

    private BigDecimal price;
    private BigDecimal originalPrice;
    private BigDecimal discount;
    private Long categoryId;
    private String location;
    private String brand;
    private Integer stock;
    private String expiryDate;
    private String ingredients;

    @TableField(typeHandler = ListStringTypeHandler.class)
    private List<String> tags;

    private Integer status;
    private Date createTime;
    private Date updateTime;
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\handler\CartWebSocketHandler.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.handler;

import com.example.supermarket2.dto.app.response.CartItemDto;
import com.example.supermarket2.dto.ws.WebSocketMessage;
import com.example.supermarket2.manager.WebSocketSessionManager;
import com.example.supermarket2.service.CartService;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.socket.CloseStatus;
import org.springframework.web.socket.TextMessage;
import org.springframework.web.socket.WebSocketSession;
import org.springframework.web.socket.handler.TextWebSocketHandler;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.List;

/**
 * 璐墿杞︿笓灞濿ebSocket澶勭悊鍣?
 * 鍏煎鍘熸湁涓氬姟閫昏緫锛岄噸鏋勫悗澧炲姞锛氳韩浠芥牎楠屻€佸績璺冲鐞嗐€佷細璇濈粺涓€绠＄悊
 */
@Component
@Slf4j
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class CartWebSocketHandler extends TextWebSocketHandler {

    private final CartService cartService;
    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;
    private final WebSocketSessionManager sessionManager;

    /**
     * 杩炴帴寤虹珛鎴愬姛鍚庢墽琛?
     */
    @Override
    public void afterConnectionEstablished(WebSocketSession session) throws Exception {
        // 浠庢彙鎵嬫嫤鎴櫒娉ㄥ叆鐨勫睘鎬т腑鑾峰彇userId锛堝畨鍏紝涓嶅彲浼€狅級
        Long userId = (Long) session.getAttributes().get("userId");
        if (userId == null) {
            session.close(CloseStatus.POLICY_VIOLATION.withReason("鐢ㄦ埛韬唤鏍￠獙澶辫触"));
            return;
        }

        // 灏嗕細璇濆姞鍏ュ叏灞€绠＄悊鍣?
        sessionManager.addSession(userId, session);

        // 杩炴帴寤虹珛鏃剁珛鍗冲彂閫佸綋鍓嶈喘鐗╄溅鏁版嵁
        sendCartDataToUser(userId, session);
    }

    /**
     * 杩炴帴鍏抽棴鍚庢墽琛?
     */
    @Override
    public void afterConnectionClosed(WebSocketSession session, CloseStatus status) throws Exception {
        Long userId = (Long) session.getAttributes().get("userId");
        if (userId != null) {
            // 浠庡叏灞€绠＄悊鍣ㄧЩ闄や細璇?
            sessionManager.removeSession(userId, session.getId());
        }
        log.info("璐墿杞ebSocket杩炴帴鍏抽棴锛宻essionId={}, 鍏抽棴鍘熷洜={}", session.getId(), status);
    }

    /**
     * 鏀跺埌瀹㈡埛绔秷鎭椂鎵ц
     */
    @Override
    protected void handleTextMessage(WebSocketSession session, TextMessage message) throws Exception {
        // 鏀跺埌娑堟伅鏃讹紝鏇存柊鏈€鍚庢秷鎭椂闂?
        session.getAttributes().put(WebSocketSessionManager.LAST_MESSAGE_TIME_KEY, System.currentTimeMillis());

        Long userId = (Long) session.getAttributes().get("userId");
        String payload = message.getPayload();
        log.debug("鏀跺埌瀹㈡埛绔秷鎭紝userId={}, 鍐呭={}", userId, payload);

        // 瑙ｆ瀽娑堟伅
        WebSocketMessage<?> wsMessage;
        try {
            wsMessage = objectMapper.readValue(payload, WebSocketMessage.class);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            sendMessage(session, WebSocketMessage.error("娑堟伅鏍煎紡閿欒"));
            return;
        }

        // 蹇冭烦鍖呭鐞?
        if ("heartbeat".equals(wsMessage.getType())) {
            sendMessage(session, WebSocketMessage.heartbeat());
            return;
        }

        // 瀹㈡埛绔富鍔ㄨ姹傚埛鏂拌喘鐗╄溅
        if ("cart_refresh".equals(wsMessage.getType())) {
            sendCartDataToUser(userId, session);
            return;
        }

        // 鍏朵粬娑堟伅绫诲瀷鍙墿灞?
        sendMessage(session, WebSocketMessage.error("涓嶆敮鎸佺殑娑堟伅绫诲瀷"));
    }

    /**
     * 浼犺緭寮傚父澶勭悊
     */
    @Override
    public void handleTransportError(WebSocketSession session, Throwable exception) throws Exception {
        Long userId = (Long) session.getAttributes().get("userId");
        log.error("璐墿杞ebSocket浼犺緭寮傚父锛寀serId={}, sessionId={}", userId, session.getId(), exception);
        if (session.isOpen()) {
            session.close(CloseStatus.SERVER_ERROR.withReason("浼犺緭寮傚父"));
        }
    }

    /**
     * 銆愬師鏈夋柟娉曢噸鏋勩€戝悜鎸囧畾鐢ㄦ埛鍙戦€佽喘鐗╄溅鏇存柊锛堝叏閲忔帹閫侊級
     */
    public void sendCartUpdateToUser(Long userId) {
        if (!sessionManager.isUserOnline(userId)) {
            return;
        }
        // 鑾峰彇鐢ㄦ埛鎵€鏈夊湪绾夸細璇?
        var sessions = sessionManager.getUserSessions(userId);
        for (WebSocketSession session : sessions) {
            sendCartDataToUser(userId, session);
        }
    }

    /**
     * 鍚戞寚瀹氫細璇濆彂閫佽喘鐗╄溅鏁版嵁
     */
    private void sendCartDataToUser(Long userId, WebSocketSession session) {
        try {
            if (!session.isOpen()) {
                return;
            }
            List<CartItemDto> cartItems = cartService.getCartItems(userId);
            WebSocketMessage<List<CartItemDto>> wsMessage = WebSocketMessage.success("cart_update", cartItems);
            sendMessage(session, wsMessage);
            log.debug("璐墿杞︽暟鎹帹閫佹垚鍔燂紝userId={}", userId);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("璐墿杞︽暟鎹帹閫佸け璐ワ紝userId={}", userId, e);
        }
    }

    /**
     * 鍙戦€佹秷鎭殑宸ュ叿鏂规硶锛堢嚎绋嬪畨鍏級
     */
    private void sendMessage(WebSocketSession session, WebSocketMessage<?> message) throws IOException {
        if (!session.isOpen()) {
            return;
        }
        String json = objectMapper.writeValueAsString(message);
        synchronized (session) {
            session.sendMessage(new TextMessage(json));
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\handler\ListStringTypeHandler.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.handler;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import org.apache.ibatis.type.BaseTypeHandler;
import org.apache.ibatis.type.JdbcType;
import org.apache.ibatis.type.MappedJdbcTypes;
import org.apache.ibatis.type.MappedTypes;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;

import java.sql.CallableStatement;
import java.sql.PreparedStatement;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.util.List;

/**
 * List<String>涓嶫SON瀛楃涓茬被鍨嬭浆鎹㈠櫒
 * 淇鐐癸細
 * 1. 鍘绘帀 @Component/@RequiredArgsConstructor锛孧yBatis 涓嶉€氳繃 Spring 瀹炰緥鍖?
 * 2. 鏄惧紡娣诲姞 @NoArgsConstructor 鏃犲弬鏋勯€?
 * 3. ObjectMapper 鑷繁 new 涓€涓紙涓嶈渚濊禆 Spring 娉ㄥ叆锛?
 */
@Slf4j
@NoArgsConstructor // 銆愬叧閿慨澶?銆戞樉寮忓０鏄庢棤鍙傛瀯閫犲嚱鏁?
@MappedTypes(List.class)
@MappedJdbcTypes(JdbcType.VARCHAR)
public class ListStringTypeHandler extends BaseTypeHandler<List<String>> {

    // 銆愬叧閿慨澶?銆戣嚜宸?new ObjectMapper锛屼笉瑕佷緷璧?Spring 娉ㄥ叆
    // 濡傛灉闇€瑕佸拰 Spring 鐨勫叏灞€ ObjectMapper 閰嶇疆涓€鑷达紝鍙互閫氳繃闈欐€佹柟娉曡幏鍙栵紝鎴栬€呰繖閲屾墜鍔ㄩ厤缃浉鍚岀殑瑙勫垯
    private static final ObjectMapper objectMapper = new ObjectMapper();

    private static final TypeReference<List<String>> LIST_TYPE_REFERENCE = new TypeReference<List<String>>() {};

    // 鎻掑叆鏁版嵁搴撴椂锛氬皢List<String>杞负JSON瀛楃涓?
    @Override
    public void setNonNullParameter(PreparedStatement ps, int i, List<String> parameter, JdbcType jdbcType) throws SQLException {
        try {
            String json = objectMapper.writeValueAsString(parameter);
            ps.setString(i, json);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("List<String>杞琂SON澶辫触", e);
            throw new SQLException("List<String>杞琂SON澶辫触", e);
        }
    }

    // 鏌ヨ鏃讹細浠庢暟鎹簱JSON瀛楃涓茶浆涓篖ist<String>
    @Override
    public List<String> getNullableResult(ResultSet rs, String columnName) throws SQLException {
        return parseJson(rs.getString(columnName));
    }

    @Override
    public List<String> getNullableResult(ResultSet rs, int columnIndex) throws SQLException {
        return parseJson(rs.getString(columnIndex));
    }

    @Override
    public List<String> getNullableResult(CallableStatement cs, int columnIndex) throws SQLException {
        return parseJson(cs.getString(columnIndex));
    }

    // 瑙ｆ瀽JSON瀛楃涓蹭负List<String>
    private List<String> parseJson(String json) {
        if (json == null || json.trim().isEmpty()) {
            return null;
        }
        try {
            return objectMapper.readValue(json, LIST_TYPE_REFERENCE);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("JSON杞琇ist<String>澶辫触: json={}", json, e);
            throw new RuntimeException("JSON杞琇ist<String>澶辫触: " + json, e);
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\handler\MyMetaObjectHandler.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.handler;

import com.baomidou.mybatisplus.core.handlers.MetaObjectHandler;
import org.apache.ibatis.reflection.MetaObject;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;

 @Component // 娉ㄥ唽涓篠pring Bean
public class MyMetaObjectHandler implements MetaObjectHandler {

    // 鎻掑叆鏃惰嚜鍔ㄥ～鍏?
    @Override
    public void insertFill(MetaObject metaObject) {
        // 濉厖createTime锛堝鏋滃瓧娈典负绌猴級
        this.strictInsertFill(metaObject, "createTime", LocalDateTime.class, LocalDateTime.now());
        // 濉厖updateTime锛堝鏋滃瓧娈典负绌猴級
        this.strictInsertFill(metaObject, "updateTime", LocalDateTime.class, LocalDateTime.now());
    }

    // 鏇存柊鏃惰嚜鍔ㄥ～鍏?
    @Override
    public void updateFill(MetaObject metaObject) {
        // 濉厖updateTime锛堟洿鏂版椂寮哄埗鍒锋柊锛?
        this.strictUpdateFill(metaObject, "updateTime", LocalDateTime.class, LocalDateTime.now());
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\handler\UniversalWebSocketHandler.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.handler;

import com.example.supermarket2.dto.ws.WebSocketMessage;
import com.example.supermarket2.manager.WebSocketSessionManager;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.socket.CloseStatus;
import org.springframework.web.socket.TextMessage;
import org.springframework.web.socket.WebSocketSession;
import org.springframework.web.socket.handler.TextWebSocketHandler;

import java.io.IOException;

/**
 * 閫氱敤鍏ㄤ笟鍔ebSocket澶勭悊鍣?
 * 缁熶竴澶勭悊璐墿杞?瀹氫綅/瀵艰埅/璁惧鏁版嵁鍏ㄤ笟鍔″満鏅殑娑堟伅鏀跺彂
 */
@Component
@Slf4j
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class UniversalWebSocketHandler extends TextWebSocketHandler {

    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;
    private final WebSocketSessionManager sessionManager;

    @Override
    public void afterConnectionEstablished(WebSocketSession session) throws Exception {
        Long userId = (Long) session.getAttributes().get("userId");
        if (userId == null) {
            session.close(CloseStatus.POLICY_VIOLATION.withReason("鐢ㄦ埛韬唤鏍￠獙澶辫触"));
            return;
        }

        sessionManager.addSession(userId, session);
        log.info("閫氱敤WebSocket杩炴帴寤虹珛鎴愬姛锛寀serId={}, sessionId={}", userId, session.getId());

        // 杩炴帴鎴愬姛鍝嶅簲
        sendMessage(session, WebSocketMessage.success("connect_success", "杩炴帴鎴愬姛"));
    }

    @Override
    public void afterConnectionClosed(WebSocketSession session, CloseStatus status) throws Exception {
        Long userId = (Long) session.getAttributes().get("userId");
        if (userId != null) {
            sessionManager.removeSession(userId, session.getId());
        }
        log.info("閫氱敤WebSocket杩炴帴鍏抽棴锛寀serId={}, sessionId={}, 鍘熷洜={}", userId, session.getId(), status);
    }

    @Override
    protected void handleTextMessage(WebSocketSession session, TextMessage message) throws Exception {
        Long userId = (Long) session.getAttributes().get("userId");
        String payload = message.getPayload();

        try {
            WebSocketMessage<?> wsMessage = objectMapper.readValue(payload, WebSocketMessage.class);

            // 蹇冭烦鍖呭鐞?
            if ("heartbeat".equals(wsMessage.getType())) {
                sendMessage(session, WebSocketMessage.heartbeat());
                return;
            }

            log.debug("鏀跺埌瀹㈡埛绔秷鎭紝userId={}, 娑堟伅绫诲瀷={}", userId, wsMessage.getType());

            // 鍏朵粬涓氬姟娑堟伅鍙€氳繃浜嬩欢鏈哄埗鍒嗗彂锛屾垨鐩存帴鍦ㄤ笟鍔″眰閫氳繃PushService鎺ㄩ€?
            // 杩欓噷浠呭仛娑堟伅鎺ユ敹锛屼笟鍔℃帹閫佺粺涓€鐢盬ebSocketPushService澶勭悊

        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("娑堟伅瑙ｆ瀽澶辫触锛寀serId={}", userId, e);
            sendMessage(session, WebSocketMessage.error("娑堟伅鏍煎紡瑙ｆ瀽澶辫触"));
        }
    }

    @Override
    public void handleTransportError(WebSocketSession session, Throwable exception) throws Exception {
        Long userId = (Long) session.getAttributes().get("userId");
        log.error("閫氱敤WebSocket浼犺緭寮傚父锛寀serId={}", userId, exception);
        if (session.isOpen()) {
            session.close(CloseStatus.SERVER_ERROR);
        }
    }

    /**
     * 绾跨▼瀹夊叏鐨勬秷鎭彂閫佹柟娉?
     */
    private void sendMessage(WebSocketSession session, WebSocketMessage<?> message) throws IOException {
        if (!session.isOpen()) {
            return;
        }
        String json = objectMapper.writeValueAsString(message);
        synchronized (session) {
            session.sendMessage(new TextMessage(json));
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\infra\redis\CartRedisRepository.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.infra.redis;

import com.example.supermarket2.common.constants.RedisKeyConstants;
import com.example.supermarket2.infra.redis.model.RedisCartItem;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.data.redis.core.RedisTemplate;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;

import static com.example.supermarket2.common.constants.RedisKeyConstants.CART_USER_KEY;

@Slf4j
@Component
@RequiredArgsConstructor // 鏋勯€犲櫒娉ㄥ叆锛屾浛浠Autowired锛岀鍚圫pring鏈€浣冲疄璺?
public class CartRedisRepository {

    private final RedisTemplate<String, Object> redisTemplate;

    public Map<String, RedisCartItem> getCartItems(Long userId) {
        String key = String.format(CART_USER_KEY, userId);
        Map<Object, Object> map = redisTemplate.opsForHash().entries(key);
        Map<String, RedisCartItem> cartItemMap = new HashMap<>();

        for (Map.Entry<Object, Object> entry : map.entrySet()) {
            String productId = (String) entry.getKey();
            Object value = entry.getValue();

            // 銆愪慨澶嶃€戠被鍨嬫牎楠岋紝浠呭綋绫诲瀷鍖归厤鏃舵墠寮鸿浆
            if (value instanceof RedisCartItem redisCartItem) {
                cartItemMap.put(productId, redisCartItem);
            } else {
                log.warn("璐墿杞︽暟鎹被鍨嬪紓甯革紝userId={}, productId={}, 瀹為檯绫诲瀷={}",
                        userId, productId, value.getClass().getName());
                // 娓呯悊寮傚父鏁版嵁锛岄伩鍏嶅悗缁寔缁姤閿?
                redisTemplate.opsForHash().delete(key, productId);
            }
        }
        return cartItemMap;
    }

    public RedisCartItem getCartItem(Long userId, Long productId) {
        String key = String.format(CART_USER_KEY, userId);
        String field = String.valueOf(productId);
        Object value = redisTemplate.opsForHash().get(key, field);

        // 銆愪慨澶嶃€戠被鍨嬫牎楠岋紝閬垮厤寮鸿浆寮傚父
        if (value instanceof RedisCartItem redisCartItem) {
            return redisCartItem;
        } else if (value != null) {
            log.warn("璐墿杞﹀崟椤规暟鎹被鍨嬪紓甯革紝userId={}, productId={}, 瀹為檯绫诲瀷={}",
                    userId, productId, value.getClass().getName());
            redisTemplate.opsForHash().delete(key, field);
        }
        return null;
    }

    public Integer getCartItemsCount(Long userId) {
        String key = String.format(CART_USER_KEY, userId);
        Long count = redisTemplate.opsForHash().size(key);
        return count != null ? count.intValue() : 0;
    }

    public void addToCart(Long userId, Long productId, RedisCartItem cartItem) {
        String key = String.format(CART_USER_KEY, userId);
        String field = String.valueOf(productId);
        redisTemplate.opsForHash().put(key, field, cartItem);
        // 鏂板鍚庡埛鏂拌繃鏈熸椂闂?
        expireCart(userId);
    }

    public void updateCartItem(Long userId, Long productId, RedisCartItem cartItem) {
        String key = String.format(CART_USER_KEY, userId);
        String field = String.valueOf(productId);
        redisTemplate.opsForHash().put(key, field, cartItem);
        expireCart(userId);
    }

    public void removeCartItem(Long userId, Long productId) {
        String key = String.format(CART_USER_KEY, userId);
        String field = String.valueOf(productId);
        redisTemplate.opsForHash().delete(key, field);
    }

    public void clearCart(Long userId) {
        String key = String.format(CART_USER_KEY, userId);
        redisTemplate.delete(key);
    }

    public void expireCart(Long userId) {
        String key = String.format(CART_USER_KEY, userId);
        redisTemplate.expire(key, RedisKeyConstants.getSecondsUntilEndOfDay(), TimeUnit.SECONDS);
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\interceptor\WebSocketHandshakeInterceptor.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.interceptor;

import com.example.supermarket2.utils.JwtUtil;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.http.server.ServerHttpRequest;
import org.springframework.http.server.ServerHttpResponse;
import org.springframework.http.server.ServletServerHttpRequest;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.socket.WebSocketHandler;
import org.springframework.web.socket.server.HandshakeInterceptor;

import java.util.Map;

/**
 * WebSocket 鎻℃墜鎷︽埅鍣?
 * 鏍稿績鑳藉姏锛氳繛鎺ュ缓绔嬪墠鐨勮韩浠芥牎楠屻€佺敤鎴蜂俊鎭敞鍏ャ€侀潪娉曡繛鎺ユ嫤鎴?
 */
@Slf4j
@Component
public class WebSocketHandshakeInterceptor implements HandshakeInterceptor {

    // 鐢熶骇鐜璇锋浛鎹负鐪熷疄鐨凧WT鏍￠獙锛岃繖閲屽吋瀹逛綘鐜版湁userId=1鐨勬祴璇曞満鏅?
    private static final String TEST_USER_ID = "1";

    /**
     * 鎻℃墜鍓嶆墽琛岋細韬唤鏍￠獙
     */
    @Override
    public boolean beforeHandshake(ServerHttpRequest request, ServerHttpResponse response, WebSocketHandler wsHandler, Map<String, Object> attributes) throws Exception {
        try {
            // 1. 浠庤姹備腑鎻愬彇鍙傛暟
            ServletServerHttpRequest servletRequest = (ServletServerHttpRequest) request;
            String userId = servletRequest.getServletRequest().getParameter("userId");
            String token = servletRequest.getServletRequest().getParameter("token");

            // 2. 鍩虹鍙傛暟鏍￠獙
            if (userId == null || userId.trim().isEmpty()) {
                log.warn("WebSocket鎻℃墜澶辫触锛氱己灏憉serId鍙傛暟");
                return false;
            }

            // 3. 韬唤鏍￠獙锛堢敓浜х幆澧冨惎鐢↗WT鏍￠獙锛屾祴璇曠幆澧冨吋瀹圭幇鏈夐€昏緫锛?
            boolean isAuthPass = false;
            // 娴嬭瘯鐜锛氬吋瀹瑰浐瀹歶serId=1
            if (TEST_USER_ID.equals(userId)) {
                isAuthPass = true;
            }
            // 鐢熶骇鐜锛欽WT浠ょ墝鏍￠獙
            else if (token != null && !token.trim().isEmpty()) {
                // 杩欓噷璋冪敤浣燡wtUtil鐨勬牎楠屾柟娉曪紝瑙ｆ瀽token鑾峰彇userId
                // Long realUserId = jwtUtil.validateTokenAndGetUserId(token);
                // isAuthPass = realUserId != null && realUserId.toString().equals(userId);
                isAuthPass = true; // 娴嬭瘯涓存椂鏀捐
            }

            if (!isAuthPass) {
                log.warn("WebSocket鎻℃墜澶辫触锛氱敤鎴疯韩浠芥牎楠屼笉閫氳繃锛寀serId={}", userId);
                return false;
            }

            // 4. 灏唘serId娉ㄥ叆WebSocket浼氳瘽灞炴€э紝鍚庣画澶勭悊鍣ㄥ彲鐩存帴鑾峰彇
            attributes.put("userId", Long.parseLong(userId));
            log.info("WebSocket鎻℃墜鎴愬姛锛歶serId={}", userId);
            return true;

        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("WebSocket鎻℃墜寮傚父", e);
            return false;
        }
    }

    /**
     * 鎻℃墜鍚庢墽琛岋細鏃ュ織璁板綍
     */
    @Override
    public void afterHandshake(ServerHttpRequest request, ServerHttpResponse response, WebSocketHandler wsHandler, Exception exception) {
        if (exception != null) {
            log.error("WebSocket鎻℃墜鍚庡紓甯?, exception);
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\manager\WebSocketSessionManager.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.manager;

import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.socket.WebSocketSession;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.stream.Collectors;

/**
 * WebSocket 鍏ㄥ眬浼氳瘽绠＄悊鍣?
 * 鏍稿績鑳藉姏锛氱敤鎴蜂細璇濈殑澧炲垹鏀规煡銆佸绔櫥褰曠鐞嗐€佽繛鎺ョ姸鎬佹娴嬨€佹壒閲忔秷鎭帹閫?
 */
@Slf4j
@Component
public class WebSocketSessionManager {

    /**
     * 鏈€鍚庢秷鎭椂闂寸殑Session灞炴€ey
     */
    public static final String LAST_MESSAGE_TIME_KEY = "lastMessageTime";

    /**
     * 鐢ㄦ埛浼氳瘽瀛樺偍
     * key: userId, value: 鐢ㄦ埛鐨勪細璇濋泦鍚堬紙鏀寔澶氱鍚屾椂鐧诲綍锛屽璁惧鍚屾椂鍦ㄧ嚎锛?
     */
    private final ConcurrentHashMap<Long, ConcurrentHashMap<String, WebSocketSession>> userSessionMap = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();

    /**
     * 蹇冭烦瓒呮椂鏃堕棿锛?0绉掓棤蹇冭烦鍒欏垽瀹氫负姝昏繛鎺ワ級
     */
    private static final long HEARTBEAT_TIMEOUT = 30 * 1000L;

    /**
     * 鏂板鐢ㄦ埛浼氳瘽
     * @param userId 鐢ㄦ埛ID
     * @param session WebSocket浼氳瘽
     */
    public void addSession(Long userId, WebSocketSession session) {
        // 鏂板浼氳瘽鏃跺垵濮嬪寲鏈€鍚庢秷鎭椂闂?
        session.getAttributes().put(LAST_MESSAGE_TIME_KEY, System.currentTimeMillis());
        // 涓虹敤鎴峰垱寤轰細璇濋泦鍚堬紙濡傛灉涓嶅瓨鍦級
        userSessionMap.computeIfAbsent(userId, k -> new ConcurrentHashMap<>());
        // 灏嗕細璇濆姞鍏ョ敤鎴风殑闆嗗悎锛宬ey涓轰細璇滻D
        userSessionMap.get(userId).put(session.getId(), session);
        log.info("鐢ㄦ埛{}浼氳瘽鏂板锛屼細璇滻D={}锛屽綋鍓嶅湪绾夸細璇濇暟={}",
                userId, session.getId(), userSessionMap.get(userId).size());
    }

    /**
     * 绉婚櫎鐢ㄦ埛浼氳瘽
     * @param userId 鐢ㄦ埛ID
     * @param sessionId 浼氳瘽ID
     */
    public void removeSession(Long userId, String sessionId) {
        ConcurrentHashMap<String, WebSocketSession> sessionMap = userSessionMap.get(userId);
        if (sessionMap != null) {
            WebSocketSession session = sessionMap.remove(sessionId);
            // try-with-resources 鑷姩鍏抽棴浼氳瘽
            if (session != null) {
                try (session) {
                    if (session.isOpen()) {
                        log.info("鐢ㄦ埛{}浼氳瘽{}宸插叧闂?, userId, sessionId);
                    }
                } catch (IOException e) {
                    log.error("鍏抽棴鐢ㄦ埛{}浼氳瘽{}寮傚父", userId, sessionId, e);
                }
            }
            // 濡傛灉鐢ㄦ埛娌℃湁浼氳瘽浜嗭紝绉婚櫎鐢ㄦ埛key
            if (sessionMap.isEmpty()) {
                userSessionMap.remove(userId);
                log.info("鐢ㄦ埛{}鎵€鏈変細璇濆凡绉婚櫎锛屼笅绾?, userId);
            } else {
                log.info("鐢ㄦ埛{}浼氳瘽{}宸茬Щ闄わ紝鍓╀綑浼氳瘽鏁?{}", userId, sessionId, sessionMap.size());
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鐢ㄦ埛鐨勬墍鏈夊湪绾夸細璇?
     * @param userId 鐢ㄦ埛ID
     * @return 浼氳瘽闆嗗悎
     */
    public Set<WebSocketSession> getUserSessions(Long userId) {
        ConcurrentHashMap<String, WebSocketSession> sessionMap = userSessionMap.get(userId);
        if (sessionMap == null || sessionMap.isEmpty()) {
            return Set.of();
        }
        return Set.copyOf(sessionMap.values());
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ョ敤鎴锋槸鍚﹀湪绾?
     * @param userId 鐢ㄦ埛ID
     * @return 鏄惁鍦ㄧ嚎
     */
    public boolean isUserOnline(Long userId) {
        ConcurrentHashMap<String, WebSocketSession> sessionMap = userSessionMap.get(userId);
        if (sessionMap == null || sessionMap.isEmpty()) {
            return false;
        }
        // 浼樺寲锛氬彧瑕佹湁涓€涓細璇濇槸鎵撳紑鐨勶紝灏卞垽瀹氫负鍦ㄧ嚎
        return sessionMap.values().stream().anyMatch(WebSocketSession::isOpen);
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鎵€鏈夊湪绾跨敤鎴稩D
     * @return 鍦ㄧ嚎鐢ㄦ埛ID闆嗗悎
     */
    public Set<Long> getOnlineUserIds() {
        return Set.copyOf(userSessionMap.keySet());
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鍦ㄧ嚎鐢ㄦ埛鎬绘暟
     * @return 鍦ㄧ嚎鐢ㄦ埛鏁?
     */
    public int getOnlineUserCount() {
        return userSessionMap.size();
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鍦ㄧ嚎浼氳瘽鎬绘暟
     * @return 浼氳瘽鏁?
     */
    public int getOnlineSessionCount() {
        return userSessionMap.values().stream()
                .mapToInt(ConcurrentHashMap::size)
                .sum();
    }

    /**
     * 鍏抽棴鎸囧畾鐢ㄦ埛鐨勬墍鏈変細璇?
     * @param userId 鐢ㄦ埛ID
     */
    public void closeUserSessions(Long userId) {
        ConcurrentHashMap<String, WebSocketSession> sessionMap = userSessionMap.get(userId);
        if (sessionMap != null) {
            sessionMap.values().forEach(session -> {
                // try-with-resources 鑷姩鍏抽棴
                try (session) {
                    if (session.isOpen()) {
                        session.close();
                    }
                } catch (IOException e) {
                    log.error("鍏抽棴鐢ㄦ埛{}浼氳瘽寮傚父", userId, e);
                }
            });
            userSessionMap.remove(userId);
            log.info("鐢ㄦ埛{}鎵€鏈変細璇濆凡寮哄埗鍏抽棴", userId);
        }
    }

    /**
     * 娓呯悊瓒呮椂姝昏繛鎺?
     */
    public void cleanTimeoutSessions() {
        long currentTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
        int cleanCount = 0;

        for (Long userId : userSessionMap.keySet()) {
            ConcurrentHashMap<String, WebSocketSession> sessionMap = userSessionMap.get(userId);
            if (sessionMap == null) continue;

            // 杩囨护鍑鸿秴鏃?鍏抽棴鐨勪細璇?
            Set<String> timeoutSessionIds = sessionMap.entrySet().stream()
                    .filter(entry -> {
                        WebSocketSession session = entry.getValue();
                        // 浠嶴ession灞炴€т腑鑾峰彇鏈€鍚庢秷鎭椂闂达紝淇getLastMessageTime涓嶅瓨鍦ㄧ殑鎶ラ敊
                        Long lastMessageTime = (Long) session.getAttributes().get(LAST_MESSAGE_TIME_KEY);
                        // 浼氳瘽宸插叧闂?鎴?鏈€鍚庢秷鎭椂闂磋秴杩囪秴鏃舵椂闂?
                        return !session.isOpen() ||
                                (lastMessageTime != null && (currentTime - lastMessageTime) > HEARTBEAT_TIMEOUT);
                    })
                    .map(Map.Entry::getKey)
                    .collect(Collectors.toSet());

            // 绉婚櫎瓒呮椂浼氳瘽
            for (String sessionId : timeoutSessionIds) {
                WebSocketSession session = sessionMap.remove(sessionId);
                // try-with-resources 鑷姩鍏抽棴
                if (session != null) {
                    try (session) {
                        if (session.isOpen()) {
                            session.close();
                        }
                    } catch (IOException e) {
                        log.error("鍏抽棴瓒呮椂浼氳瘽寮傚父锛宻essionId={}", sessionId, e);
                    }
                }
                cleanCount++;
            }

            // 鐢ㄦ埛鏃犱細璇濆垯绉婚櫎key
            if (sessionMap.isEmpty()) {
                userSessionMap.remove(userId);
            }
        }

        if (cleanCount > 0) {
            log.info("娓呯悊瓒呮椂浼氳瘽瀹屾垚锛屽叡娓呯悊{}涓杩炴帴", cleanCount);
        }
    }
}

package com.example.supermarket2.mapper.location;

import com.example.supermarket2.entity.location.MapGrid;
import org.apache.ibatis.annotations.*;

import java.util.List;

/**
 * 鍦板浘缃戞牸鏁版嵁璁块棶鎺ュ彛
 * MyBatis鏄犲皠锛屾煡璇㈠湴鍥剧綉鏍间俊鎭?
 */
@Mapper
public interface MapGridMapper {

    /**
     * 鏍规嵁鍦板浘ID鏌ヨ缃戞牸鏁版嵁
     */
    @Select("SELECT id, map_id, x, y, color, passable " +
            "FROM map_grid " +
            "WHERE map_id = #{mapId} " +
            "ORDER BY y, x")
    List<MapGrid> getMapGridByMapId(@Param("mapId") String mapId);

    /**
     * 鏌ヨ鎸囧畾鑼冨洿鍐呯殑缃戞牸鏁版嵁
     */
    @Select("SELECT id, map_id, x, y, color, passable " +
            "FROM map_grid " +
            "WHERE map_id = #{mapId} " +
            "AND x BETWEEN #{minX} AND #{maxX} " +
            "AND y BETWEEN #{minY} AND #{maxY} " +
            "ORDER BY y, x")
    List<MapGrid> getMapGridByArea(@Param("mapId") String mapId,
                                   @Param("minX") Integer minX,
                                   @Param("maxX") Integer maxX,
                                   @Param("minY") Integer minY,
                                   @Param("maxY") Integer maxY);

    /**
     * 鏌ヨ鍙€氳缃戞牸鏁版嵁
     */
    @Select("SELECT id, map_id, x, y, color, passable " +
            "FROM map_grid " +
            "WHERE map_id = #{mapId} AND passable = 1 " +
            "ORDER BY y, x")
    List<MapGrid> getPassableMapGrid(@Param("mapId") String mapId);

    /**
     * 鏌ヨ鍦板浘杈圭晫淇℃伅
     */
    @Select("SELECT " +
            "MIN(x) as min_x, MAX(x) as max_x, " +
            "MIN(y) as min_y, MAX(y) as max_y, " +
            "COUNT(*) as total_grids " +
            "FROM map_grid " +
            "WHERE map_id = #{mapId}")
    MapGridBounds getMapBounds(@Param("mapId") String mapId);

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ユ寚瀹氫綅缃槸鍚﹀彲閫氳
     */
    @Select("SELECT COUNT(*) " +
            "FROM map_grid " +
            "WHERE map_id = #{mapId} AND x = #{x} AND y = #{y} AND passable = 1")
    int isPositionPassable(@Param("mapId") String mapId,
                           @Param("x") Integer x,
                           @Param("y") Integer y);

    /**
     * 鍦板浘杈圭晫淇℃伅绫?
     */
    class MapGridBounds {
        private Integer minX;
        private Integer maxX;
        private Integer minY;
        private Integer maxY;
        private Integer totalGrids;

        // getters and setters
        public Integer getMinX() { return minX; }
        public void setMinX(Integer minX) { this.minX = minX; }

        public Integer getMaxX() { return maxX; }
        public void setMaxX(Integer maxX) { this.maxX = maxX; }

        public Integer getMinY() { return minY; }
        public void setMinY(Integer minY) { this.minY = minY; }

        public Integer getMaxY() { return maxY; }
        public void setMaxY(Integer maxY) { this.maxY = maxY; }

        public Integer getTotalGrids() { return totalGrids; }
        public void setTotalGrids(Integer totalGrids) { this.totalGrids = totalGrids; }

        /**
         * 鑾峰彇鍦板浘瀹藉害
         */
        public Integer getWidth() {
            return maxX != null && minX != null ? maxX - minX + 1 : 0;
        }

        /**
         * 鑾峰彇鍦板浘楂樺害
         */
        public Integer getHeight() {
            return maxY != null && minY != null ? maxY - minY + 1 : 0;
        }
    }
}

package com.example.supermarket2.mapper.location;

import com.example.supermarket2.entity.location.UserLocation;
import org.apache.ibatis.annotations.*;

import java.util.List;

/**
 * 鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆鏁版嵁璁块棶鎺ュ彛
 * MyBatis鏄犲皠锛屾搷浣滅敤鎴蜂綅缃俊鎭?
 */
@Mapper
public interface UserLocationMapper {

    /**
     * 鏂板鎴栨洿鏂扮敤鎴蜂綅缃紙鍩轰簬 user_id + map_id 鍞竴閿級
     */
    @Insert("INSERT INTO user_location (user_id, map_id, x, y, timestamp) " +
            "VALUES (#{userId}, #{mapId}, #{x}, #{y}, #{timeStamp}) " +
            "ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE " +
            "x = #{x}, " +
            "y = #{y}, " +
            "timestamp = #{timeStamp}")
    @Options(useGeneratedKeys = true, keyProperty = "id")
    int upsertUserLocation(UserLocation location);

    /**
     * 鏌ヨ鐢ㄦ埛鏈€鏂颁綅缃?
     */
    @Select("SELECT id, user_id as userId, map_id as mapId, x, y, timestamp " +
            "FROM user_location " +
            "WHERE user_id = #{userId} AND map_id = #{mapId} " +
            "ORDER BY timestamp DESC " +
            "LIMIT 1")
    UserLocation getLatestUserLocation(@Param("userId") String userId,
                                       @Param("mapId") String mapId);

    /**
     * 鏌ヨ鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆鍘嗗彶
     */
    @Select("SELECT id, user_id as userId, map_id as mapId, x, y, timestamp " +
            "FROM user_location " +
            "WHERE user_id = #{userId} AND map_id = #{mapId} " +
            "ORDER BY timestamp DESC " +
            "LIMIT #{limit}")
    List<UserLocation> getUserLocationHistory(@Param("userId") String userId,
                                              @Param("mapId") String mapId,
                                              @Param("limit") Integer limit);

    /**
     * 鍒犻櫎杩囨湡鐨勭敤鎴蜂綅缃褰?
     */
    @Delete("DELETE FROM user_location " +
            "WHERE timestamp < DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL #{expireHours} HOUR)")
    int deleteExpiredLocations(@Param("expireHours") Integer expireHours);

    /**
     * 鏌ヨ鍦板浘涓婄殑鎵€鏈夌敤鎴蜂綅缃?
     */
    @Select("SELECT id, user_id as userId, map_id as mapId, x, y, timestamp " +
            "FROM user_location " +
            "WHERE map_id = #{mapId} " +
            "AND timestamp > DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 5 MINUTE) " +
            "ORDER BY timestamp DESC")
    List<UserLocation> getRecentUserLocationsByMap(@Param("mapId") String mapId);

    /**
     * 缁熻鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆鏇存柊棰戠巼
     */
    @Select("SELECT COUNT(*) as update_count, " +
            "AVG(TIMESTAMPDIFF(SECOND, lag_timestamp, timestamp)) as avg_interval " +
            "FROM ( " +
            "    SELECT timestamp, " +
            "           LAG(timestamp) OVER (PARTITION BY user_id, map_id ORDER BY timestamp) as lag_timestamp " +
            "    FROM user_location " +
            "    WHERE user_id = #{userId} AND map_id = #{mapId} " +
            "    AND timestamp > DATE_SUB(NOW(), INTERVAL 1 HOUR) " +
            ") as t " +
            "WHERE lag_timestamp IS NOT NULL")
    LocationUpdateStats getLocationUpdateStats(@Param("userId") String userId,
                                               @Param("mapId") String mapId);

    /**
     * 浣嶇疆鏇存柊缁熻绫?
     */
    class LocationUpdateStats {
        private Integer updateCount;
        private Double avgInterval;

        // getters and setters
        public Integer getUpdateCount() { return updateCount; }
        public void setUpdateCount(Integer updateCount) { this.updateCount = updateCount; }

        public Double getAvgInterval() { return avgInterval; }
        public void setAvgInterval(Double avgInterval) { this.avgInterval = avgInterval; }

        /**
         * 鑾峰彇鏇存柊棰戠巼锛堟/鍒嗛挓锛?
         */
        public Double getUpdatesPerMinute() {
            return avgInterval != null && avgInterval > 0 ? 60.0 / avgInterval : 0.0;
        }
    }

    /**
     * 鎵归噺鎻掑叆鐢ㄦ埛浣嶇疆锛堟€ц兘浼樺寲锛?
     */
    @Insert("<script>" +
            "INSERT INTO user_location (user_id, map_id, x, y, timestamp) VALUES " +
            "<foreach collection='locations' item='location' separator=','>" +
            "(#{location.userId}, #{location.mapId}, #{location.x}, #{location.y}, #{location.timeStamp})" +
            "</foreach>" +
            "ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE " +
            "x = VALUES(x), y = VALUES(y), timestamp = VALUES(timestamp)" +
            "</script>")
    int batchUpsertUserLocations(@Param("locations") List<UserLocation> locations);
}
