package com.example.supermarket2.service.location;

import com.example.supermarket2.dto.location.NavigationRequest;
import com.example.supermarket2.dto.location.NavigationResponse;

/**
 * 瀵艰埅鏈嶅姟鎺ュ彛
 * 瀹氫箟璺緞瑙勫垝鏍稿績鑳藉姏锛屽疄鐜颁笌涓氬姟瑙ｈ€?
 */
public interface NavigationService {

    /**
     * 澧炲己璺緞瑙勫垝锛堟敮鎸佷笉鍙€氳鐩爣鐐硅皟鏁达級
     * @param request 璺緞瑙勫垝璇锋眰
     * @return 瀵艰埅璺緞缁撴灉
     */
    NavigationResponse calculateEnhancedPath(NavigationRequest request);

    /**
     * 娓呯悊杩囨湡缂撳瓨
     */
    void cleanupExpiredCache();

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鏈嶅姟缁熻淇℃伅
     * @return 瀵艰埅鏈嶅姟缁熻鏁版嵁
     */
    NavigationStats getServiceStats();

    /**
     * 瀵艰埅鏈嶅姟缁熻绫?
     */
    class NavigationStats {
        private final int totalRequests;
        private final int successfulPaths;
        private final int cacheHits;
        private final int cacheSize;

        public NavigationStats(int totalRequests, int successfulPaths, int cacheHits, int cacheSize) {
            this.totalRequests = totalRequests;
            this.successfulPaths = successfulPaths;
            this.cacheHits = cacheHits;
            this.cacheSize = cacheSize;
        }

        public int getTotalRequests() { return totalRequests; }
        public int getSuccessfulPaths() { return successfulPaths; }
        public int getCacheHits() { return cacheHits; }
        public int getCacheSize() { return cacheSize; }
        public double getSuccessRate() {
            return totalRequests > 0 ? (double) successfulPaths / totalRequests * 100 : 0;
        }
        public double getCacheHitRate() {
            return totalRequests > 0 ? (double) cacheHits / totalRequests * 100 : 0;
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\service\location\SignalProcessor.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.service.location;

import com.example.supermarket2.dto.location.BeaconData;
import com.example.supermarket2.entity.location.BeaconConfig;
import com.example.supermarket2.entity.location.RssiHistory;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;

import java.util.*;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.stream.Collectors;

/**
 * 淇″彿棰勫鐞嗘湇鍔?
 * 瀵瑰師濮嬭摑鐗欎俊鏍囨暟鎹繘琛岄澶勭悊鍜屾护娉?
 */
@Slf4j
@Service
public class SignalProcessor {

    @Autowired
    private BeaconConfig beaconConfig;

    // RSSI鍘嗗彶璁板綍锛岀敤浜庝俊鍙峰垎鏋愬拰婊ゆ尝
    private final Map<String, List<RssiHistory>> rssiHistoryMap = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    private final int MAX_HISTORY_SIZE = 10;

    /**
     * 棰勫鐞嗕俊鏍囨暟鎹?
     */
    public List<BeaconData> preProcessBeacons(List<BeaconData> rawBeacons) {
        if (rawBeacons == null || rawBeacons.isEmpty()) {
            return new ArrayList<>();
        }

        log.debug("寮€濮嬩俊鍙烽澶勭悊: 鍘熷淇℃爣鏁伴噺={}", rawBeacons.size());

        List<BeaconData> processedBeacons = rawBeacons.stream()
                .filter(this::isValidBeacon) // 鍩虹楠岃瘉
                .map(this::clampRssi) // RSSI闄愬箙
                .map(this::updateHistory) // 鏇存柊鍘嗗彶璁板綍
                .filter(this::filterOutliers) // 寮傚父鍊艰繃婊?
                .sorted(Comparator.comparing(BeaconData::getRssi).reversed()) // 鎸変俊鍙峰己搴︽帓搴?
                .collect(Collectors.toList());

        log.debug("淇″彿棰勫鐞嗗畬鎴? 鏈夋晥淇℃爣鏁伴噺={}", processedBeacons.size());
        return processedBeacons;
    }

    /**
     * 楠岃瘉淇℃爣鏁版嵁鏈夋晥鎬?
     */
    private boolean isValidBeacon(BeaconData beacon) {
        if (beacon == null || beacon.getUuid() == null || beacon.getUuid().trim().isEmpty()) {
            return false;
        }

        if (beacon.getRssi() == null || beacon.getRssi() >= 0) {
            return false;
        }

        // 妫€鏌UID鏍煎紡
        String uuid = beacon.getUuid().toLowerCase().replace("-", "");
        if (uuid.length() != 32) { // 鏍囧噯鐨刄UID闀垮害锛堝幓闄ゆí鏉狅級
            log.warn("鏃犳晥鐨勪俊鏍嘦UID鏍煎紡: {}", beacon.getUuid());
            return false;
        }

        return true;
    }

    /**
     * RSSI闄愬箙澶勭悊
     */
    private BeaconData clampRssi(BeaconData beacon) {
        Integer clampedRssi = beaconConfig.clampRssi(beacon.getRssi());

        if (!clampedRssi.equals(beacon.getRssi())) {
            log.debug("RSSI闄愬箙: {} -> {}", beacon.getRssi(), clampedRssi);
            beacon.setRssi(clampedRssi);
        }

        return beacon;
    }

    /**
     * 鏇存柊鍘嗗彶璁板綍骞舵娴嬪紓甯稿€?
     */
    private BeaconData updateHistory(BeaconData beacon) {
        String beaconKey = beacon.getNormalizedUuid();
        List<RssiHistory> history = rssiHistoryMap.getOrDefault(beaconKey, new ArrayList<>());

        // 鍒涘缓鏂扮殑鍘嗗彶璁板綍
        RssiHistory newRecord = new RssiHistory();
        newRecord.setRssi(beacon.getRssi());
        newRecord.setTimestamp(System.currentTimeMillis());
        newRecord.setBeaconId(beaconKey);  // 娉ㄦ剰锛氱被涓娇鐢ㄧ殑鏄?beaconId锛屼笉鏄?beaconKey
        newRecord.setIsValid(true);

        // 妫€娴嬪紓甯稿€?
        if (isOutlier(newRecord, history)) {
            log.debug("妫€娴嬪埌寮傚父鍊? beacon={}, rssi={}", beaconKey.substring(0, 8), beacon.getRssi());
            beacon.setIsValid(false);
            return beacon;
        }

        // 鏇存柊鍘嗗彶璁板綍
        history.add(newRecord);
        if (history.size() > MAX_HISTORY_SIZE) {
            history = history.subList(history.size() - MAX_HISTORY_SIZE, history.size());
        }
        rssiHistoryMap.put(beaconKey, history);

        beacon.setIsValid(true);
        return beacon;
    }

    /**
     * 寮傚父鍊艰繃婊?
     */
    private boolean filterOutliers(BeaconData beacon) {
        if (!beacon.getIsValid()) {
            return false;
        }

        String beaconKey = beacon.getNormalizedUuid();
        List<RssiHistory> history = rssiHistoryMap.get(beaconKey);

        if (history == null || history.size() < 3) {
            return true; // 鍘嗗彶鏁版嵁涓嶈冻锛屼笉杩囨护
        }

        // 妫€鏌ヤ俊鍙风ǔ瀹氭€?
        return isSignalStable(history, beacon.getRssi());
    }

    /**
     * 妫€娴嬪紓甯稿€硷紙鍩轰簬涓綅鏁扮粷瀵瑰亸宸級
     */
    private boolean isOutlier(RssiHistory newRecord, List<RssiHistory> history) {
        if (history.size() < 3) {
            return false; // 鏁版嵁涓嶈冻锛屼笉鍒ゅ畾涓哄紓甯?
        }

        // 鍒涘缓鍖呭惈鏂拌褰曠殑鍚堝苟鍒楄〃杩涜妫€娴?
        List<RssiHistory> combinedHistory = new ArrayList<>(history);
        combinedHistory.add(newRecord);

        List<RssiHistory> outliers = RssiHistory.detectOutliers(combinedHistory, beaconConfig.getOutlierThreshold());

        // 妫€鏌ユ柊璁板綍鏄惁鍦ㄥ紓甯稿€煎垪琛ㄤ腑
        return outliers.stream()
                .anyMatch(outlier ->
                        outlier.getRssi().equals(newRecord.getRssi()) &&
                                outlier.getTimestamp().equals(newRecord.getTimestamp()));
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ヤ俊鍙风ǔ瀹氭€?
     */
    private boolean isSignalStable(List<RssiHistory> history, int currentRssi) {
        if (history.size() < 2) {
            return true;
        }

        // 璁＄畻鏈€杩戜俊鍙风殑绋冲畾鎬?
        List<RssiHistory> recent = history.subList(
                Math.max(0, history.size() - 3), history.size());

        double stability = RssiHistory.calculateStability(recent);

        // 妫€鏌ュ綋鍓嶅€间笌鍘嗗彶骞冲潎鍊肩殑宸紓
        double recentAvg = recent.stream()
                .mapToInt(RssiHistory::getRssi)
                .average()
                .orElse(currentRssi);

        double diff = Math.abs(currentRssi - recentAvg);
        boolean isStable = stability >= beaconConfig.getStabilityThreshold() && diff < 15;

        log.debug("淇″彿绋冲畾鎬ф鏌? beacon={}, 绋冲畾鎬?{}, 宸紓={}, 绋冲畾={}",
                history.get(0).getBeaconId().substring(0, 8),
                stability, diff, isStable);

        return isStable;
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻淇℃爣鏉冮噸
     */
    public double calculateBeaconWeight(BeaconData beacon) {
        if (beacon == null || !beacon.getIsValid()) {
            return 0.0;
        }

        String beaconKey = beacon.getNormalizedUuid();
        List<RssiHistory> history = rssiHistoryMap.get(beaconKey);

        double baseWeight = beaconConfig.calculateWeight(beacon.getRssi());

        // 鏍规嵁绋冲畾鎬ц皟鏁存潈閲?
        if (history != null && history.size() >= 2) {
            double stability = RssiHistory.calculateStability(history);
            baseWeight *= stability;
        }

        return baseWeight;
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇淇″彿璐ㄩ噺璇勫垎
     */
    public double calculateSignalQualityScore(BeaconData beacon) {
        if (beacon == null || !beacon.getIsValid()) {
            return 0.0;
        }

        double score = 0.0;

        // RSSI寮哄害璇勫垎
        if (beacon.getRssi() > -60) score += 0.4;
        else if (beacon.getRssi() > -70) score += 0.3;
        else if (beacon.getRssi() > -80) score += 0.2;
        else score += 0.1;

        // 绋冲畾鎬ц瘎鍒嗭紙濡傛灉鏈夊巻鍙叉暟鎹級
        String beaconKey = beacon.getNormalizedUuid();
        List<RssiHistory> history = rssiHistoryMap.get(beaconKey);
        if (history != null && history.size() >= 3) {
            double stability = RssiHistory.calculateStability(history);
            score += stability * 0.3;
        } else {
            score += 0.15; // 榛樿绋冲畾鎬у垎鏁?
        }

        return Math.min(1.0, score);
    }

    /**
     * 娓呯悊杩囨湡鐨勫巻鍙茶褰?
     */
    public void cleanupExpiredHistory(long expireTimeMillis) {
        long currentTime = System.currentTimeMillis();
        int removedCount = 0;

        for (String beaconKey : rssiHistoryMap.keySet()) {
            List<RssiHistory> history = rssiHistoryMap.get(beaconKey);
            if (history != null) {
                List<RssiHistory> validHistory = history.stream()
                        .filter(record -> currentTime - record.getTimestamp() <= expireTimeMillis)
                        .collect(Collectors.toList());

                if (validHistory.size() != history.size()) {
                    rssiHistoryMap.put(beaconKey, validHistory);
                    removedCount += (history.size() - validHistory.size());
                }
            }
        }

        if (removedCount > 0) {
            log.info("娓呯悊杩囨湡鍘嗗彶璁板綍: 绉婚櫎{}鏉¤褰?, removedCount);
        }
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇淇″彿澶勭悊缁熻淇℃伅
     */
    public SignalProcessingStats getStats() {
        int totalBeacons = rssiHistoryMap.values().stream()
                .mapToInt(List::size)
                .sum();

        int uniqueBeacons = rssiHistoryMap.size();

        return new SignalProcessingStats(totalBeacons, uniqueBeacons);
    }

    /**
     * 淇″彿澶勭悊缁熻绫?
     */
    public static class SignalProcessingStats {
        private final int totalHistoryRecords;
        private final int uniqueBeacons;

        public SignalProcessingStats(int totalHistoryRecords, int uniqueBeacons) {
            this.totalHistoryRecords = totalHistoryRecords;
            this.uniqueBeacons = uniqueBeacons;
        }

        public int getTotalHistoryRecords() { return totalHistoryRecords; }
        public int getUniqueBeacons() { return uniqueBeacons; }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\service\WebSocketPushService.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.service;

import com.example.supermarket2.dto.ws.WebSocketMessage;
import com.example.supermarket2.manager.WebSocketSessionManager;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import org.springframework.web.socket.TextMessage;
import org.springframework.web.socket.WebSocketSession;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Set;

/**
 * WebSocket 缁熶竴鎺ㄩ€佹湇鍔?
 * 鎵€鏈変笟鍔℃ā鍧楅渶瑕佹帹閫佹秷鎭椂锛屼粎闇€璋冪敤姝ょ被鐨勬柟娉曪紝鏃犻渶鍏冲績浼氳瘽绠＄悊
 */
@Slf4j
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class WebSocketPushService {

    private final WebSocketSessionManager sessionManager;
    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;

    /**
     * 鍚戞寚瀹氱敤鎴锋帹閫佹秷鎭紙鏍稿績鏂规硶锛?
     * @param userId 鐩爣鐢ㄦ埛ID
     * @param message 鎺ㄩ€佺殑娑堟伅浣?
     * @return 鎺ㄩ€佹垚鍔熺殑浼氳瘽鏁?
     */
    public <T> int pushToUser(Long userId, WebSocketMessage<T> message) {
        if (userId == null || message == null) {
            log.warn("鎺ㄩ€佹秷鎭け璐ワ細鍙傛暟涓虹┖");
            return 0;
        }

        // 妫€鏌ョ敤鎴锋槸鍚﹀湪绾?
        if (!sessionManager.isUserOnline(userId)) {
            log.debug("鐢ㄦ埛{}涓嶅湪绾匡紝璺宠繃娑堟伅鎺ㄩ€侊紝娑堟伅绫诲瀷={}", userId, message.getType());
            return 0;
        }

        // 鑾峰彇鐢ㄦ埛鎵€鏈夊湪绾夸細璇?
        Set<WebSocketSession> sessions = sessionManager.getUserSessions(userId);
        int successCount = 0;

        // 搴忓垪鍖栨秷鎭?
        String messageJson;
        try {
            messageJson = objectMapper.writeValueAsString(message);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("娑堟伅搴忓垪鍖栧け璐ワ紝userId={}", userId, e);
            return 0;
        }

        // 鍚戞瘡涓細璇濇帹閫佹秷鎭?
        TextMessage textMessage = new TextMessage(messageJson);
        for (WebSocketSession session : sessions) {
            try {
                if (session.isOpen()) {
                    synchronized (session) { // 绾跨▼瀹夊叏锛氶槻姝㈠绾跨▼鍚屾椂鍚戝悓涓€涓猻ession鍐欐暟鎹?
                        session.sendMessage(textMessage);
                    }
                    successCount++;
                    log.debug("娑堟伅鎺ㄩ€佹垚鍔燂紝userId={}, sessionId={}, 娑堟伅绫诲瀷={}",
                            userId, session.getId(), message.getType());
                }
            } catch (IOException e) {
                log.error("娑堟伅鎺ㄩ€佸け璐ワ紝userId={}, sessionId={}", userId, session.getId(), e);
            }
        }

        return successCount;
    }

    /**
     * 鍚戞墍鏈夊湪绾跨敤鎴峰箍鎾秷鎭?
     * @param message 骞挎挱娑堟伅
     * @return 鎺ㄩ€佹垚鍔熺殑浼氳瘽鏁?
     */
    public <T> int broadcastToAll(WebSocketMessage<T> message) {
        Set<Long> onlineUserIds = sessionManager.getOnlineUserIds();
        int totalSuccess = 0;
        for (Long userId : onlineUserIds) {
            totalSuccess += pushToUser(userId, message);
        }
        log.info("骞挎挱娑堟伅瀹屾垚锛屽湪绾跨敤鎴锋暟={}, 鎺ㄩ€佹垚鍔熸暟={}", onlineUserIds.size(), totalSuccess);
        return totalSuccess;
    }

    /**
     * 鍚戞寚瀹氱敤鎴烽泦鍚堟壒閲忔帹閫佹秷鎭?
     * @param userIds 鐢ㄦ埛ID闆嗗悎
     * @param message 鎺ㄩ€佹秷鎭?
     * @return 鎺ㄩ€佹垚鍔熺殑浼氳瘽鏁?
     */
    public <T> int pushToUsers(Set<Long> userIds, WebSocketMessage<T> message) {
        int totalSuccess = 0;
        for (Long userId : userIds) {
            totalSuccess += pushToUser(userId, message);
        }
        return totalSuccess;
    }

    // ========== 涓氬姟鍦烘櫙蹇嵎鏂规硶 ==========
    /**
     * 鎺ㄩ€佽喘鐗╄溅鏇存柊娑堟伅
     */
    public int pushCartUpdate(Long userId, Object cartData) {
        WebSocketMessage<Object> message = WebSocketMessage.success("cart_update", cartData);
        return pushToUser(userId, message);
    }

    /**
     * 鎺ㄩ€佺敤鎴峰畾浣嶆洿鏂版秷鎭?
     */
    public int pushLocationUpdate(Long userId, Object locationData) {
        WebSocketMessage<Object> message = WebSocketMessage.success("location_update", locationData);
        return pushToUser(userId, message);
    }

    /**
     * 鎺ㄩ€佸鑸矾寰勬洿鏂版秷鎭?
     */
    public int pushNavigationUpdate(Long userId, Object navigationData) {
        WebSocketMessage<Object> message = WebSocketMessage.success("navigation_update", navigationData);
        return pushToUser(userId, message);
    }

    /**
     * 鎺ㄩ€佹櫤鑳借澶囨暟鎹秷鎭?
     */
    public int pushDeviceData(Long userId, Object deviceData) {
        WebSocketMessage<Object> message = WebSocketMessage.success("device_data", deviceData);
        return pushToUser(userId, message);
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\task\WebSocketHeartbeatTask.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.task;

import com.example.supermarket2.manager.WebSocketSessionManager;
import lombok.RequiredArgsConstructor;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import org.springframework.scheduling.annotation.Scheduled;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

/**
 * WebSocket 蹇冭烦瀹氭椂浠诲姟
 * 瀹氭湡娓呯悊瓒呮椂姝昏繛鎺ワ紝淇濊瘉浼氳瘽绠＄悊鍣ㄧ殑鍐呭瓨涓嶆硠婕?
 */
@Slf4j
@Component
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class WebSocketHeartbeatTask {

    private final WebSocketSessionManager sessionManager;

    /**
     * 姣?0绉掓墽琛屼竴娆★紝娓呯悊瓒呮椂姝昏繛鎺?
     */
    @Scheduled(fixedRate = 30 * 1000)
    public void cleanTimeoutSession() {
        log.debug("寮€濮嬫墽琛學ebSocket姝昏繛鎺ユ竻鐞嗕换鍔?);
        sessionManager.cleanTimeoutSessions();
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\utils\location\DecimalUtils.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.utils.location;

import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;

import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.math.RoundingMode;

/**
 * 灏忔暟澶勭悊宸ュ叿绫?
 * 澶勭悊BigDecimal鐨勭簿搴﹀拰鑸嶅叆锛岀‘淇濇暟鍊艰绠楃殑鍑嗙‘鎬?
 */
@Slf4j
public class DecimalUtils {

    private DecimalUtils() {
        // 宸ュ叿绫伙紝闃叉瀹炰緥鍖?
    }

    // 榛樿绮惧害灏哄害
    private static final int DEFAULT_SCALE = 6;

    /**
     * 鍥涜垗浜斿叆鍒版寚瀹氱簿搴?
     */
    public static double round(double value, int scale) {
        if (Double.isNaN(value) || Double.isInfinite(value)) {
            log.warn("灏濊瘯瀵规棤鏁堟暟鍊艰繘琛岃垗鍏? {}", value);
            return 0.0;
        }

        try {
            BigDecimal bd = BigDecimal.valueOf(value);
            bd = bd.setScale(scale, RoundingMode.HALF_UP);
            return bd.doubleValue();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("鏁板€艰垗鍏ュけ璐? value={}, scale={}", value, scale, e);
            return value;
        }
    }

    /**
     * 鍥涜垗浜斿叆鍒伴粯璁ょ簿搴?
     */
    public static double round(double value) {
        return round(value, DEFAULT_SCALE);
    }

    /**
     * 瀹夊叏鐨勫姞娉曡繍绠?
     */
    public static double add(double a, double b) {
        if (Double.isNaN(a) || Double.isInfinite(a) ||
                Double.isNaN(b) || Double.isInfinite(b)) {
            log.warn("鏃犳晥鐨勫姞娉曟搷浣滄暟: {} + {}", a, b);
            return 0.0;
        }

        try {
            BigDecimal bd1 = BigDecimal.valueOf(a);
            BigDecimal bd2 = BigDecimal.valueOf(b);
            return bd1.add(bd2).doubleValue();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("鍔犳硶杩愮畻澶辫触: {} + {}", a, b, e);
            return a + b; // 鍥為€€鍒板師鐢熷姞娉?
        }
    }

    /**
     * 瀹夊叏鐨勫噺娉曡繍绠?
     */
    public static double subtract(double a, double b) {
        if (Double.isNaN(a) || Double.isInfinite(a) ||
                Double.isNaN(b) || Double.isInfinite(b)) {
            log.warn("鏃犳晥鐨勫噺娉曟搷浣滄暟: {} - {}", a, b);
            return 0.0;
        }

        try {
            BigDecimal bd1 = BigDecimal.valueOf(a);
            BigDecimal bd2 = BigDecimal.valueOf(b);
            return bd1.subtract(bd2).doubleValue();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("鍑忔硶杩愮畻澶辫触: {} - {}", a, b, e);
            return a - b; // 鍥為€€鍒板師鐢熷噺娉?
        }
    }

    /**
     * 瀹夊叏鐨勪箻娉曡繍绠?
     */
    public static double multiply(double a, double b) {
        if (Double.isNaN(a) || Double.isInfinite(a) ||
                Double.isNaN(b) || Double.isInfinite(b)) {
            log.warn("鏃犳晥鐨勪箻娉曟搷浣滄暟: {} * {}", a, b);
            return 0.0;
        }

        try {
            BigDecimal bd1 = BigDecimal.valueOf(a);
            BigDecimal bd2 = BigDecimal.valueOf(b);
            return bd1.multiply(bd2).doubleValue();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("涔樻硶杩愮畻澶辫触: {} * {}", a, b, e);
            return a * b; // 鍥為€€鍒板師鐢熶箻娉?
        }
    }

    /**
     * 瀹夊叏鐨勯櫎娉曡繍绠?
     */
    public static double divide(double a, double b) {
        return divide(a, b, DEFAULT_SCALE);
    }

    /**
     * 瀹夊叏鐨勯櫎娉曡繍绠楋紙鎸囧畾绮惧害锛?
     */
    public static double divide(double a, double b, int scale) {
        if (Double.isNaN(a) || Double.isInfinite(a) ||
                Double.isNaN(b) || Double.isInfinite(b)) {
            log.warn("鏃犳晥鐨勯櫎娉曟搷浣滄暟: {} / {}", a, b);
            return 0.0;
        }

        if (b == 0) {
            log.warn("闄ゆ硶杩愮畻闄ゆ暟涓洪浂: {} / {}", a, b);
            return Double.MAX_VALUE * Math.signum(a);
        }

        try {
            BigDecimal bd1 = BigDecimal.valueOf(a);
            BigDecimal bd2 = BigDecimal.valueOf(b);
            return bd1.divide(bd2, scale, RoundingMode.HALF_UP).doubleValue();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("闄ゆ硶杩愮畻澶辫触: {} / {}", a, b, e);
            return a / b; // 鍥為€€鍒板師鐢熼櫎娉?
        }
    }

    /**
     * 姣旇緝涓や釜double鍊硷紙鑰冭檻绮惧害璇樊锛?
     */
    public static boolean equals(double a, double b, double epsilon) {
        if (Double.isNaN(a) && Double.isNaN(b)) return true;
        if (Double.isNaN(a) || Double.isNaN(b)) return false;

        return Math.abs(a - b) <= epsilon;
    }

    /**
     * 姣旇緝涓や釜double鍊硷紙浣跨敤榛樿绮惧害璇樊锛?
     */
    public static boolean equals(double a, double b) {
        return equals(a, b, 1e-10);
    }

    /**
     * 闄愬埗鏁板€煎湪鎸囧畾鑼冨洿鍐?
     */
    public static double clamp(double value, double min, double max) {
        if (Double.isNaN(value)) return min;
        return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, value));
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻骞冲潎鍊硷紙閬垮厤鏁板€兼孩鍑猴級
     */
    public static double average(double[] values) {
        if (values == null || values.length == 0) {
            return Double.NaN;
        }

        try {
            BigDecimal sum = BigDecimal.ZERO;
            for (double value : values) {
                sum = sum.add(BigDecimal.valueOf(value));
            }
            return sum.divide(BigDecimal.valueOf(values.length), DEFAULT_SCALE, RoundingMode.HALF_UP)
                    .doubleValue();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("骞冲潎鍊艰绠楀け璐?, e);

            // 鍥為€€鍒扮畝鍗曞钩鍧?
            double simpleSum = 0;
            for (double value : values) {
                simpleSum += value;
            }
            return simpleSum / values.length;
        }
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻鍔犳潈骞冲潎鍊?
     */
    public static double weightedAverage(double[] values, double[] weights) {
        if (values == null || weights == null ||
                values.length != weights.length || values.length == 0) {
            return Double.NaN;
        }

        try {
            BigDecimal weightedSum = BigDecimal.ZERO;
            BigDecimal weightSum = BigDecimal.ZERO;

            for (int i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
                BigDecimal value = BigDecimal.valueOf(values[i]);
                BigDecimal weight = BigDecimal.valueOf(weights[i]);
                weightedSum = weightedSum.add(value.multiply(weight));
                weightSum = weightSum.add(weight);
            }

            if (weightSum.compareTo(BigDecimal.ZERO) == 0) {
                return average(values);
            }

            return weightedSum.divide(weightSum, DEFAULT_SCALE, RoundingMode.HALF_UP)
                    .doubleValue();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("鍔犳潈骞冲潎鍊艰绠楀け璐?, e);
            return Double.NaN;
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\utils\location\DistanceCalculator.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.utils.location;

import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

/**
 * 璺濈璁＄畻宸ュ叿
 * 鎻愪緵鍩轰簬RSSI鐨勮窛绂昏绠楀拰鐩稿叧宸ュ叿鏂规硶
 */
@Slf4j
public class DistanceCalculator {

    private DistanceCalculator() {
        // 宸ュ叿绫伙紝闃叉瀹炰緥鍖?
    }

    /**
     * 鏍规嵁RSSI璁＄畻璺濈锛堝鏁拌矾寰勬崯鑰楁ā鍨嬶級
     */
    public static double calculateDistance(double rssi, double rssi0, double pathLossExponent) {
        if (rssi >= 0) {
            log.warn("鏃犳晥鐨凴SSI鍊? {}", rssi);
            return Double.MAX_VALUE;
        }

        try {
            // 浣跨敤瀵规暟璺緞鎹熻€楁ā鍨? RSSI = RSSI0 - 10 * n * log10(d/d0)
            // 鍏朵腑d0=1绫筹紝鎵€浠ョ畝鍖栦负: d = 10^((RSSI0 - RSSI) / (10 * n))
            return Math.pow(10, (rssi0 - rssi) / (10 * pathLossExponent));
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("璺濈璁＄畻澶辫触: RSSI={}, RSSI0={}, n={}", rssi, rssi0, pathLossExponent, e);
            return Double.MAX_VALUE;
        }
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻涓夎瀹氫綅鐨勬潈閲嶈窛绂?
     */
    public static double calculateWeightedDistance(double measuredRssi, double expectedRssi,
                                                   double maxDistance, double weightFactor) {
        double distance = calculateDistance(measuredRssi, expectedRssi, weightFactor);
        return Math.min(distance, maxDistance);
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻涓ょ偣涔嬮棿鐨勮窛绂伙紙娆у嚑閲屽緱璺濈锛?
     */
    public static double calculateEuclideanDistance(double x1, double y1, double x2, double y2) {
        double dx = x1 - x2;
        double dy = y1 - y2;
        return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻淇℃爣淇″彿瑕嗙洊鑼冨洿
     */
    public static double calculateCoverageRadius(double txPower, double sensitivity, double pathLossExponent) {
        // 鏍规嵁鍙戝皠鍔熺巼鍜屾帴鏀剁伒鏁忓害璁＄畻鏈€澶ц鐩栬寖鍥?
        return calculateDistance(sensitivity, txPower, pathLossExponent);
    }

    /**
     * 璺濈鏈夋晥鎬ф鏌?
     */
    public static boolean isValidDistance(double distance, double minDistance, double maxDistance) {
        return !Double.isNaN(distance) &&
                !Double.isInfinite(distance) &&
                distance >= minDistance &&
                distance <= maxDistance;
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻瀹氫綅璇樊鍦嗗崐寰勶紙CEP锛?
     */
    public static double calculateCircularErrorProbability(List<Double> errors, double probability) {
        if (errors == null || errors.isEmpty()) {
            return 0.0;
        }

        // 瀵硅宸繘琛屾帓搴?
        List<Double> sortedErrors = new ArrayList<>(errors);
        sortedErrors.sort(Double::compareTo);

        // 璁＄畻鎸囧畾姒傜巼瀵瑰簲鐨勮宸€?
        int index = (int) (sortedErrors.size() * probability);
        index = Math.min(index, sortedErrors.size() - 1);

        return sortedErrors.get(index);
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻淇℃爣閮ㄧ讲瀵嗗害
     */
    public static double calculateBeaconDensity(int beaconCount, double area) {
        if (area <= 0) {
            return 0.0;
        }
        return beaconCount / area;
    }

    /**
     * 浼扮畻瀹氫綅绮惧害
     */
    public static double estimatePositioningAccuracy(int beaconCount, double avgRssi, double coverageDensity) {
        double accuracy = 5.0; // 鍩虹绮惧害锛堢背锛?

        // 淇℃爣鏁伴噺褰卞搷
        if (beaconCount >= 4) {
            accuracy *= 0.6;
        } else if (beaconCount >= 3) {
            accuracy *= 0.8;
        } else if (beaconCount >= 2) {
            accuracy *= 1.0;
        } else {
            accuracy *= 2.0;
        }

        // 淇″彿寮哄害褰卞搷
        if (avgRssi > -60) {
            accuracy *= 0.7;
        } else if (avgRssi > -70) {
            accuracy *= 0.9;
        } else if (avgRssi > -80) {
            accuracy *= 1.2;
        } else {
            accuracy *= 2.0;
        }

        // 閮ㄧ讲瀵嗗害褰卞搷
        accuracy *= (1.0 / coverageDensity);

        return Math.max(0.5, accuracy); // 鏈€灏忕簿搴?.5绫?
    }
}


========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\utils\location\KalmanFilter2D.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.utils.location;

import com.example.supermarket2.entity.location.Position;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;

/**
 * 浜岀淮鍗″皵鏇兼护娉㈠櫒
 * 鐢ㄤ簬浣嶇疆鏁版嵁婊ゆ尝浼樺寲锛屽钩婊戝畾浣嶈建杩?
 */
@Slf4j
public class KalmanFilter2D {
    private double[] state = new double[2]; // 鐘舵€佸悜閲?[x, y]
    private double[][] covariance = new double[2][2]; // 璇樊鍗忔柟宸煩闃?
    private double[][] processNoise = new double[2][2]; // 杩囩▼鍣０鍗忔柟宸?
    private double[][] measurementNoise = new double[2][2]; // 娴嬮噺鍣０鍗忔柟宸?
    private double[][] stateTransition = {{1, 0}, {0, 1}}; // 鐘舵€佽浆绉荤煩闃?
    private double[][] observationMatrix = {{1, 0}, {0, 1}}; // 瑙傛祴鐭╅樀

    private long lastTimestamp;
    private boolean initialized = false;

    // 閰嶇疆鍙傛暟
    private double defaultProcessNoise;
    private double defaultMeasurementNoise;

    /**
     * 鏋勯€犲嚱鏁?
     */
    public KalmanFilter2D(double processNoise, double measurementNoise) {
        this.defaultProcessNoise = processNoise;
        this.defaultMeasurementNoise = measurementNoise;

        // 鍒濆鍖栧櫔澹扮煩闃?
        initializeNoiseMatrices(processNoise, measurementNoise);

        log.info("鍗″皵鏇兼护娉㈠櫒鍒濆鍖? 杩囩▼鍣０={}, 娴嬮噺鍣０={}", processNoise, measurementNoise);
    }

    /**
     * 鍒濆鍖栨护娉㈠櫒
     */
    public void initialize(double x, double y, long timestamp) {
        state[0] = x;
        state[1] = y;

        // 鍒濆鍖栧崗鏂瑰樊鐭╅樀
        covariance[0][0] = defaultProcessNoise;
        covariance[0][1] = 0;
        covariance[1][0] = 0;
        covariance[1][1] = defaultProcessNoise;

        lastTimestamp = timestamp;
        initialized = true;

        log.debug("鍗″皵鏇兼护娉㈠櫒鍒濆鍖栦綅缃? ({}, {})", x, y);
    }

    /**
     * 婊ゆ尝澶勭悊
     */
    public Position filter(double measuredX, double measuredY, long timestamp, Double qualityFactor) {
        if (!initialized) {
            initialize(measuredX, measuredY, timestamp);
            return new Position(measuredX, measuredY, "kalman", "initial");
        }

        // 鏍规嵁璐ㄩ噺鍥犲瓙璋冩暣鍣０鍙傛暟
        if (qualityFactor != null) {
            adjustNoiseForQuality(qualityFactor);
        }

        // 璁＄畻鏃堕棿闂撮殧
        double dt = (timestamp - lastTimestamp) / 1000.0;
        lastTimestamp = timestamp;

        // 鏇存柊鐘舵€佽浆绉荤煩闃碉紙濡傛灉鏃堕棿闂撮殧杈冨ぇ锛?
        if (dt > 0.1) {
            updateStateTransitionMatrix(dt);
        }

        // 棰勬祴姝ラ
        predict();

        // 鏇存柊姝ラ
        update(measuredX, measuredY);

        // 閲嶇疆鍣０鐭╅樀涓洪粯璁ゅ€?
        initializeNoiseMatrices(defaultProcessNoise, defaultMeasurementNoise);

        return new Position(state[0], state[1], "kalman", "filtered");
    }

    /**
     * 棰勬祴姝ラ
     */
    private void predict() {
        // 鐘舵€侀娴? state = stateTransition * state
        double[] newState = new double[2];
        newState[0] = stateTransition[0][0] * state[0] + stateTransition[0][1] * state[1];
        newState[1] = stateTransition[1][0] * state[0] + stateTransition[1][1] * state[1];
        state = newState;

        // 鍗忔柟宸娴? covariance = stateTransition * covariance * stateTransition^T + processNoise
        double[][] newCovariance = new double[2][2];
        for (int i = 0; i < 2; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < 2; j++) {
                newCovariance[i][j] = 0;
                for (int k = 0; k < 2; k++) {
                    for (int l = 0; l < 2; l++) {
                        newCovariance[i][j] += stateTransition[i][k] * covariance[k][l] * stateTransition[j][l];
                    }
                }
                newCovariance[i][j] += processNoise[i][j];
            }
        }
        covariance = newCovariance;
    }

    /**
     * 鏇存柊姝ラ
     */
    private void update(double measuredX, double measuredY) {
        // 璁＄畻鍒涙柊鍚戦噺: innovation = measurement - observationMatrix * state
        double[] innovation = new double[2];
        innovation[0] = measuredX - (observationMatrix[0][0] * state[0] + observationMatrix[0][1] * state[1]);
        innovation[1] = measuredY - (observationMatrix[1][0] * state[0] + observationMatrix[1][1] * state[1]);

        // 璁＄畻鍒涙柊鍗忔柟宸? S = observationMatrix * covariance * observationMatrix^T + measurementNoise
        double[][] innovationCovariance = new double[2][2];
        for (int i = 0; i < 2; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < 2; j++) {
                innovationCovariance[i][j] = measurementNoise[i][j];
                for (int k = 0; k < 2; k++) {
                    for (int l = 0; l < 2; l++) {
                        innovationCovariance[i][j] += observationMatrix[i][k] * covariance[k][l] * observationMatrix[j][l];
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        // 璁＄畻鍗″皵鏇煎鐩? K = covariance * observationMatrix^T * S^-1
        double detS = innovationCovariance[0][0] * innovationCovariance[1][1] - innovationCovariance[0][1] * innovationCovariance[1][0];
        if (Math.abs(detS) < 1e-10) {
            log.warn("鍗″皵鏇兼护娉? 鍒涙柊鍗忔柟宸煩闃靛寮傦紝璺宠繃鏇存柊");
            return;
        }

        double[][] S_inverse = {
                {innovationCovariance[1][1] / detS, -innovationCovariance[0][1] / detS},
                {-innovationCovariance[1][0] / detS, innovationCovariance[0][0] / detS}
        };

        double[][] kalmanGain = new double[2][2];
        for (int i = 0; i < 2; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < 2; j++) {
                kalmanGain[i][j] = 0;
                for (int k = 0; k < 2; k++) {
                    kalmanGain[i][j] += covariance[i][k] * observationMatrix[j][k];
                }
                kalmanGain[i][j] *= S_inverse[j][j];
            }
        }

        // 鏇存柊鐘舵€佷及璁? state = state + K * innovation
        state[0] += kalmanGain[0][0] * innovation[0] + kalmanGain[0][1] * innovation[1];
        state[1] += kalmanGain[1][0] * innovation[0] + kalmanGain[1][1] * innovation[1];

        // 鏇存柊鍗忔柟宸及璁? covariance = (I - K * observationMatrix) * covariance
        double[][] I = {{1, 0}, {0, 1}};
        double[][] KH = new double[2][2];
        for (int i = 0; i < 2; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < 2; j++) {
                KH[i][j] = 0;
                for (int k = 0; k < 2; k++) {
                    KH[i][j] += kalmanGain[i][k] * observationMatrix[k][j];
                }
            }
        }

        double[][] I_KH = new double[2][2];
        for (int i = 0; i < 2; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < 2; j++) {
                I_KH[i][j] = I[i][j] - KH[i][j];
            }
        }

        double[][] newCovariance = new double[2][2];
        for (int i = 0; i < 2; i++) {
            for (int j = 0; j < 2; j++) {
                newCovariance[i][j] = 0;
                for (int k = 0; k < 2; k++) {
                    newCovariance[i][j] += I_KH[i][k] * covariance[k][j];
                }
            }
        }
        covariance = newCovariance;
    }

    /**
     * 鏍规嵁璐ㄩ噺鍥犲瓙璋冩暣鍣０鍙傛暟
     */
    private void adjustNoiseForQuality(double qualityFactor) {
        // 璐ㄩ噺鍥犲瓙瓒婁綆锛堜俊鍙疯秺宸級锛屾祴閲忓櫔澹拌秺澶?
        double adjustedMeasurementNoise = defaultMeasurementNoise * (2.0 - qualityFactor);
        initializeNoiseMatrices(defaultProcessNoise, adjustedMeasurementNoise);

        log.debug("鍗″皵鏇兼护娉㈣川閲忚皟鏁? 璐ㄩ噺鍥犲瓙={}, 娴嬮噺鍣０={}", qualityFactor, adjustedMeasurementNoise);
    }

    /**
     * 鏇存柊鐘舵€佽浆绉荤煩闃碉紙鑰冭檻閫熷害锛?
     */
    private void updateStateTransitionMatrix(double dt) {
        // 绠€鍗曟ā鍨嬶細鍋囪鍖€閫熻繍鍔?
        // 鍦ㄥ疄闄呭簲鐢ㄤ腑锛岃繖閲屽彲浠ユ牴鎹€熷害淇℃伅鏇存柊鐘舵€佽浆绉荤煩闃?
        stateTransition[0][0] = 1;
        stateTransition[0][1] = 0;
        stateTransition[1][0] = 0;
        stateTransition[1][1] = 1;
    }

    /**
     * 鍒濆鍖栧櫔澹扮煩闃?- 淇鐗堟湰
     */
    private void initializeNoiseMatrices(double processNoiseValue, double measurementNoiseValue) {
        // 浣跨敤this鍏抽敭瀛楁槑纭寚瀹氭垚鍛樺彉閲忥紝閬垮厤鍙傛暟鍚嶅啿绐?
        this.processNoise[0][0] = processNoiseValue;
        this.processNoise[0][1] = 0;
        this.processNoise[1][0] = 0;
        this.processNoise[1][1] = processNoiseValue;

        this.measurementNoise[0][0] = measurementNoiseValue;
        this.measurementNoise[0][1] = 0;
        this.measurementNoise[1][0] = 0;
        this.measurementNoise[1][1] = measurementNoiseValue;
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇褰撳墠鐘舵€?
     */
    public Position getCurrentState() {
        return new Position(state[0], state[1], "kalman", "current");
    }

    /**
     * 閲嶇疆婊ゆ尝鍣?
     */
    public void reset() {
        initialized = false;
        log.info("鍗″皵鏇兼护娉㈠櫒宸查噸缃?);
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚﹀凡鍒濆鍖?
     */
    public boolean isInitialized() {
        return initialized;
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\utils\location\Point.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.utils.location;

import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.Data;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;

/**
 * 鍧愭爣鐐瑰伐鍏风被
 * 鐢ㄤ簬BFS鍜孉*绠楁硶涓殑鍧愭爣澶勭悊锛屼互鍙婁綅缃绠?
 */
@Data
@NoArgsConstructor
@AllArgsConstructor
public class Point {
    public int x;
    public int y;
    public int distance; // 鐢ㄤ簬BFS鎼滅储鐨勮窛绂?
    public Double weight; // 鐢ㄤ簬鍔犳潈璁＄畻鐨勬潈閲?

    public Point(int x, int y) {
        this.x = x;
        this.y = y;
    }

    public Point(int x, int y, int distance) {
        this.x = x;
        this.y = y;
        this.distance = distance;
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻涓庡彟涓€涓偣鐨勬鍑犻噷寰楄窛绂?
     */
    public double distanceTo(Point other) {
        if (other == null) return Double.MAX_VALUE;
        double dx = this.x - other.x;
        double dy = this.y - other.y;
        return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻涓庡彟涓€涓偣鐨勬浖鍝堥】璺濈
     */
    public int manhattanDistanceTo(Point other) {
        if (other == null) return Integer.MAX_VALUE;
        return Math.abs(this.x - other.x) + Math.abs(this.y - other.y);
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ョ偣鏄惁鐩哥瓑
     */
    public boolean equals(Point other) {
        if (other == null) return false;
        return this.x == other.x && this.y == other.y;
    }

    /**
     * 杞崲涓哄瓧绗︿覆琛ㄧず
     */
    public String toKey() {
        return x + "," + y;
    }

    /**
     * 浠庡瓧绗︿覆瑙ｆ瀽鐐?
     */
    public static Point fromKey(String key) {
        if (key == null || !key.contains(",")) return null;
        try {
            String[] parts = key.split(",");
            int x = Integer.parseInt(parts[0]);
            int y = Integer.parseInt(parts[1]);
            return new Point(x, y);
        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
            return null;
        }
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ョ偣鏄惁鍦ㄦ寚瀹氳寖鍥村唴
     */
    public boolean isInBounds(int minX, int maxX, int minY, int maxY) {
        return x >= minX && x <= maxX && y >= minY && y <= maxY;
    }

    /**
     * 绉诲姩鍒扮浉閭荤偣
     */
    public Point move(int dx, int dy) {
        return new Point(x + dx, y + dy, distance + 1);
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鎵€鏈夌浉閭荤偣锛?鏂瑰悜锛?
     */
    public Point[] getNeighbors4() {
        return new Point[] {
                new Point(x - 1, y, distance + 1),
                new Point(x + 1, y, distance + 1),
                new Point(x, y - 1, distance + 1),
                new Point(x, y + 1, distance + 1)
        };
    }

    /**
     * 鑾峰彇鎵€鏈夌浉閭荤偣锛?鏂瑰悜锛?
     */
    public Point[] getNeighbors8() {
        return new Point[] {
                new Point(x - 1, y, distance + 1),
                new Point(x + 1, y, distance + 1),
                new Point(x, y - 1, distance + 1),
                new Point(x, y + 1, distance + 1),
                new Point(x - 1, y - 1, distance + 1),
                new Point(x + 1, y - 1, distance + 1),
                new Point(x - 1, y + 1, distance + 1),
                new Point(x + 1, y + 1, distance + 1)
        };
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\utils\location\PositionUtils.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.utils.location;

import com.example.supermarket2.entity.location.Position;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;

import java.util.List;

/**
 * 浣嶇疆璁＄畻宸ュ叿绫?
 * 鎻愪緵浣嶇疆鐩稿叧鐨勮绠楀拰杞崲鏂规硶
 */
@Slf4j
public class PositionUtils {

    private PositionUtils() {
        // 宸ュ叿绫伙紝闃叉瀹炰緥鍖?
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻涓ょ偣涔嬮棿鐨勬鍑犻噷寰楄窛绂?
     */
    public static double calculateDistance(Position p1, Position p2) {
        if (p1 == null || p2 == null) {
            return Double.MAX_VALUE;
        }

        double dx = p1.getX() - p2.getX();
        double dy = p1.getY() - p2.getY();
        return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻涓ょ偣涔嬮棿鐨勬浖鍝堥】璺濈
     */
    public static double calculateManhattanDistance(Position p1, Position p2) {
        if (p1 == null || p2 == null) {
            return Double.MAX_VALUE;
        }

        return Math.abs(p1.getX() - p2.getX()) + Math.abs(p1.getY() - p2.getY());
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻澶氫釜浣嶇疆鐨勪腑蹇冪偣
     */
    public static Position calculateCentroid(List<Position> positions) {
        if (positions == null || positions.isEmpty()) {
            return null;
        }

        double sumX = 0;
        double sumY = 0;
        int count = 0;

        for (Position pos : positions) {
            if (pos != null && pos.isValid()) {
                sumX += pos.getX();
                sumY += pos.getY();
                count++;
            }
        }

        if (count == 0) {
            return null;
        }

        return new Position(sumX / count, sumY / count, "centroid");
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻鍔犳潈涓績鐐?
     */
    public static Position calculateWeightedCentroid(List<Position> positions, List<Double> weights) {
        if (positions == null || weights == null ||
                positions.size() != weights.size() || positions.isEmpty()) {
            return null;
        }

        double sumX = 0;
        double sumY = 0;
        double totalWeight = 0;

        for (int i = 0; i < positions.size(); i++) {
            Position pos = positions.get(i);
            Double weight = weights.get(i);

            if (pos != null && pos.isValid() && weight != null && weight > 0) {
                sumX += pos.getX() * weight;
                sumY += pos.getY() * weight;
                totalWeight += weight;
            }
        }

        if (totalWeight == 0) {
            return calculateCentroid(positions);
        }

        return new Position(sumX / totalWeight, sumY / totalWeight, "weighted_centroid");
    }

    /**
     * 妫€鏌ヤ綅缃槸鍚﹀湪鍦板浘杈圭晫鍐?
     */
    public static boolean isWithinBounds(Position position, double minX, double maxX, double minY, double maxY) {
        if (position == null || !position.isValid()) {
            return false;
        }

        return position.getX() >= minX && position.getX() <= maxX &&
                position.getY() >= minY && position.getY() <= maxY;
    }

    /**
     * 绾︽潫浣嶇疆鍒板湴鍥捐竟鐣屽唴
     */
    public static Position constrainToBounds(Position position, double minX, double maxX, double minY, double maxY) {
        if (position == null) {
            return null;
        }

        double constrainedX = Math.max(minX, Math.min(maxX, position.getX()));
        double constrainedY = Math.max(minY, Math.min(maxY, position.getY()));

        if (constrainedX != position.getX() || constrainedY != position.getY()) {
            log.debug("浣嶇疆绾︽潫: ({}, {}) -> ({}, {})",
                    position.getX(), position.getY(), constrainedX, constrainedY);
        }

        return new Position(constrainedX, constrainedY, position.getAlgorithm(), "constrained");
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻绉诲姩閫熷害锛堝崟浣嶏細鏍?绉掞級
     */
    public static double calculateSpeed(Position start, Position end, long timeMillis) {
        if (start == null || end == null || timeMillis <= 0) {
            return 0.0;
        }

        double distance = calculateDistance(start, end);
        double timeSeconds = timeMillis / 1000.0;

        return timeSeconds > 0 ? distance / timeSeconds : 0.0;
    }

    /**
     * 鎻掑€艰绠椾腑闂翠綅缃?
     */
    public static Position interpolate(Position start, Position end, double ratio) {
        if (start == null || end == null) {
            return null;
        }

        ratio = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, ratio));

        double x = start.getX() + (end.getX() - start.getX()) * ratio;
        double y = start.getY() + (end.getY() - start.getY()) * ratio;

        return new Position(x, y, "interpolated");
    }

    /**
     * 骞虫粦浣嶇疆杞ㄨ抗锛堢Щ鍔ㄥ钩鍧囷級
     */
    public static Position smoothTrajectory(List<Position> recentPositions) {
        if (recentPositions == null || recentPositions.isEmpty()) {
            return null;
        }

        return calculateCentroid(recentPositions);
    }

    /**
     * 棰勬祴涓嬩竴涓綅缃紙绠€鍗曠嚎鎬ч娴嬶級
     */
    public static Position predictNextPosition(Position current, Position previous, double scale) {
        if (current == null || previous == null) {
            return current;
        }

        double dx = current.getX() - previous.getX();
        double dy = current.getY() - previous.getY();

        double predictedX = current.getX() + dx * scale;
        double predictedY = current.getY() + dy * scale;

        return new Position(predictedX, predictedY, "predicted");
    }
}


========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\utils\location\RssiProcessor.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.utils.location;

import com.example.supermarket2.entity.location.RssiHistory;
import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.stream.Collectors;

/**
 * RSSI淇″彿澶勭悊宸ュ叿
 * 鎻愪緵RSSI淇″彿鐨勯澶勭悊銆佹护娉㈠拰鍒嗘瀽鍔熻兘
 */
@Slf4j
public class RssiProcessor {

    private RssiProcessor() {
        // 宸ュ叿绫伙紝闃叉瀹炰緥鍖?
    }

    /**
     * 闄愬箙澶勭悊RSSI鍊?
     */
    public static int clampRssi(Integer rssi, int min, int max) {
        if (rssi == null) {
            return min;
        }
        return Math.max(min, Math.min(max, rssi));
    }

    /**
     * 杩囨护鏈夋晥鐨勪俊鏍囨暟鎹?
     */
    public static <T> List<T> filterValidBeacons(List<T> beacons, RssiValidator<T> validator) {
        if (beacons == null) {
            return new ArrayList<>();
        }

        return beacons.stream()
                .filter(validator::isValid)
                .sorted(validator.getComparator())
                .collect(Collectors.toList());
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻RSSI绉诲姩骞冲潎
     */
    public static double calculateMovingAverage(List<Integer> rssiValues, int windowSize) {
        if (rssiValues == null || rssiValues.isEmpty()) {
            return Double.NaN;
        }

        int size = Math.min(windowSize, rssiValues.size());
        List<Integer> recent = rssiValues.subList(rssiValues.size() - size, rssiValues.size());

        return recent.stream()
                .mapToInt(Integer::intValue)
                .average()
                .orElse(Double.NaN);
    }

    /**
     * 妫€娴婻SSI寮傚父鍊硷紙鍩轰簬涓綅鏁扮粷瀵瑰亸宸級
     */
    public static List<Integer> detectOutliers(List<Integer> rssiValues, double threshold) {
        if (rssiValues == null || rssiValues.size() < 3) {
            return new ArrayList<>();
        }

        List<Integer> sorted = new ArrayList<>(rssiValues);
        sorted.sort(Integer::compareTo);

        // 璁＄畻涓綅鏁?
        int median = sorted.get(sorted.size() / 2);

        // 璁＄畻涓綅鏁扮粷瀵瑰亸宸?
        List<Integer> deviations = sorted.stream()
                .map(rssi -> Math.abs(rssi - median))
                .collect(Collectors.toList());

        deviations.sort(Integer::compareTo);
        int mad = deviations.get(deviations.size() / 2);

        // 妫€娴嬪紓甯稿€?
        return rssiValues.stream()
                .filter(rssi -> Math.abs(rssi - median) > threshold * mad)
                .collect(Collectors.toList());
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻淇″彿绋冲畾鎬?
     */
    public static double calculateStability(List<Integer> rssiValues) {
        if (rssiValues == null || rssiValues.size() < 2) {
            return 1.0; // 鍗曚釜鍊艰涓虹ǔ瀹?
        }

        double mean = rssiValues.stream()
                .mapToInt(Integer::intValue)
                .average()
                .orElse(0);

        double variance = rssiValues.stream()
                .mapToDouble(rssi -> Math.pow(rssi - mean, 2))
                .average()
                .orElse(0);

        double stdDev = Math.sqrt(variance);

        // 鏍囧噯宸秺灏忥紝绋冲畾鎬ц秺楂?
        // 浣跨敤sigmoid鍑芥暟灏嗙ǔ瀹氭€ф槧灏勫埌0-1鑼冨洿
        return 1.0 / (1.0 + stdDev / 10.0);
    }

    /**
     * 鏍规嵁RSSI璁＄畻鏉冮噸
     */
    public static double calculateWeight(Integer rssi, double exponent) {
        if (rssi == null || rssi >= 0) {
            return 0.0;
        }

        // RSSI瓒婂己锛堝€艰秺澶э級锛屾潈閲嶈秺楂?
        return Math.pow(10, rssi * exponent / 10.0);
    }

    /**
     * 璁＄畻RSSI鍙樺寲瓒嬪娍
     */
    public static double calculateTrend(List<RssiHistory> history) {
        if (history == null || history.size() < 3) {
            return 0.0;
        }

        // 浣跨敤绠€鍗曠嚎鎬у洖褰掕绠楄秼鍔?
        List<RssiHistory> sorted = history.stream()
                .sorted(Comparator.comparing(RssiHistory::getTimestamp))
                .collect(Collectors.toList());

        double sumX = 0, sumY = 0, sumXY = 0, sumX2 = 0;
        int n = sorted.size();

        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            double x = i;
            double y = sorted.get(i).getRssi();
            sumX += x;
            sumY += y;
            sumXY += x * y;
            sumX2 += x * x;
        }

        double slope = (n * sumXY - sumX * sumY) / (n * sumX2 - sumX * sumX);

        // 杩斿洖瓒嬪娍鏂滅巼锛堟瘡鏃堕棿鍗曚綅鐨凴SSI鍙樺寲锛?
        return slope;
    }

    /**
     * 淇″彿璐ㄩ噺璇勪及
     */
    public static String assessSignalQuality(double avgRssi, int beaconCount, double stability) {
        if (beaconCount >= 3 && avgRssi > -65 && stability > 0.7) {
            return "HIGH";
        } else if (beaconCount >= 2 && avgRssi > -70 && stability > 0.5) {
            return "MEDIUM";
        } else if (beaconCount >= 1 && avgRssi > -75) {
            return "LOW";
        } else {
            return "POOR";
        }
    }

    /**
     * RSSI楠岃瘉鍣ㄦ帴鍙?
     */
    public interface RssiValidator<T> {
        boolean isValid(T beacon);
        Comparator<T> getComparator();
    }

    /**
     * 榛樿RSSI楠岃瘉鍣?
     */
    public static class DefaultRssiValidator implements RssiValidator<Object> {
        private final int minRssi;
        private final int maxRssi;

        public DefaultRssiValidator(int minRssi, int maxRssi) {
            this.minRssi = minRssi;
            this.maxRssi = maxRssi;
        }

        @Override
        public boolean isValid(Object beacon) {
            // 闇€瑕佸湪鍏蜂綋瀹炵幇涓幏鍙朢SSI鍊?
            // 杩欓噷鍙槸绀轰緥鎺ュ彛
            return true;
        }

        @Override
        public Comparator<Object> getComparator() {
            // 鎸塕SSI闄嶅簭鎺掑簭
            return (b1, b2) -> 0; // 鍏蜂綋瀹炵幇闇€瑕佹瘮杈僐SSI
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\utils\CryptoUtil.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.utils;

import javax.crypto.Mac;
import javax.crypto.spec.SecretKeySpec;
import java.math.BigInteger;

public class CryptoUtil {
    /**
     * HmacSHA256鍔犲瘑锛岃繑鍥炲崄鍏繘鍒跺瓧绗︿覆
     */
    public static String hmacSha256(String plainText, String key) throws Exception {
        if (plainText == null || key == null) {
            return null;
        }

        Mac mac = Mac.getInstance("HmacSHA256");
        SecretKeySpec secretKeySpec = new SecretKeySpec(key.getBytes(), "HmacSHA256");
        mac.init(secretKeySpec);
        byte[] hmacResult = mac.doFinal(plainText.getBytes());

        // 瀛楄妭鏁扮粍杞?4浣嶅崄鍏繘鍒跺瓧绗︿覆
        return String.format("%064x", new BigInteger(1, hmacResult));
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\utils\HuaweiAmqpSignUtil.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.utils;

import lombok.extern.slf4j.Slf4j;
import javax.crypto.Mac;
import javax.crypto.spec.SecretKeySpec;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.Base64;

/**
 * 鍗庝负浜慖oT AMQP 璁よ瘉绛惧悕宸ュ叿绫?
 * 涓ユ牸閬靛惊鍗庝负浜慉MQP鎺ュ叆瑙勮寖
 */
@Slf4j
public class HuaweiAmqpSignUtil {

    /**
     * 鐢熸垚AMQP杩炴帴鐨勭敤鎴峰悕
     * @param accessKey 鍗庝负浜慉K
     * @param instanceId 瀹炰緥ID锛堝熀纭€鐗堝～绌哄瓧绗︿覆锛?
     * @return 鍚堣鐨勭敤鎴峰悕
     */
    public static String generateUserName(String accessKey, String instanceId) {
        if (instanceId == null || instanceId.trim().isEmpty()) {
            return accessKey + "|";
        }
        return accessKey + "|" + instanceId;
    }

    /**
     * 鐢熸垚AMQP杩炴帴鐨勫瘑鐮侊紙绛惧悕锛?
     * @param accessCode 鍗庝负浜慡K
     * @param queueName 闃熷垪鍚嶇О
     * @return 鍚堣鐨勫瘑鐮?
     */
    public static String generatePassword(String accessCode, String queueName) {
        try {
            long timestamp = System.currentTimeMillis();
            // 璧勬簮鍚嶇О鍥哄畾鏍煎紡锛歝onsumer|{闃熷垪鍚峿
            String resourceName = "consumer|" + queueName;
            // 绛惧悕鍘熸枃锛歿timestamp}\n{resourceName}
            String signContent = timestamp + "\n" + resourceName;

            // HmacSHA256绛惧悕
            Mac mac = Mac.getInstance("HmacSHA256");
            SecretKeySpec secretKeySpec = new SecretKeySpec(accessCode.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8), "HmacSHA256");
            mac.init(secretKeySpec);
            byte[] signResult = mac.doFinal(signContent.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));

            // Base64缂栫爜
            String password = Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(signResult);
            log.debug("AMQP绛惧悕鐢熸垚鎴愬姛锛宼imestamp={}", timestamp);
            return password;
        } catch (Exception e) {
            log.error("AMQP绛惧悕鐢熸垚澶辫触", e);
            throw new RuntimeException("AMQP璁よ瘉绛惧悕鐢熸垚澶辫触", e);
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\utils\MqttSign.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.utils;

public class MqttSign {
    private String username;
    private String password;
    private String clientId;

    public String getUsername() {
        return username;
    }

    public String getPassword() {
        return password;
    }

    public String getClientId() {
        return clientId;
    }

    /**
     * 鐢熸垚鍗庝负浜慖oT MQTT杩炴帴鍙傛暟锛堢敤鎴峰悕銆佸瘑鐮併€丆lientId锛?
     * 鍗庝负浜戞爣鍑嗘帴鍏ヨ鍒?
     */
    public void calculate(String deviceId, String deviceSecret) {
        if (deviceId == null || deviceSecret == null) {
            return;
        }

        try {
            // ============== 鍗庝负浜?IoT 鍥哄畾瑙勫垯 ==============
            // 鐢ㄦ埛鍚?= 璁惧ID
            username = deviceId;

            // 瀹㈡埛绔疘D = 璁惧ID
            clientId = deviceId;

            // 瀵嗙爜 = HmacSHA256(璁惧ID, 璁惧瀵嗛挜) 鈫?Base64
            password = CryptoUtil.hmacSha256(deviceId, deviceSecret);

        } catch (Exception e) {
            e.printStackTrace();
        }
    }
}

========== D:\supermarket21\supermarket2\src\main\java\com\example\supermarket2\utils\ValidationUtil.java ==========
package com.example.supermarket2.utils;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public class ValidationUtil {

    private static final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ValidationUtil.class);

    /**
     * 楠岃瘉璁惧鏁版嵁鏍煎紡鏄惁鏈夋晥锛堥€傞厤闃块噷浜慖oT骞冲彴鏍煎紡锛?
     * 鏈夋晥鏍煎紡锛歿"params":{"product_id":1,"Weight":275.7},"version":"1.0.0"}
     */
    public static boolean isValidDeviceData(JsonNode data) {
        // 1. 鍩虹妫€鏌ワ細鏁版嵁涓嶈兘涓簄ull
        if (data == null || data.isNull()) {
            logger.warn("璁惧鏁版嵁涓虹┖");
            return false;
        }

        // 2. 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚︽湁params鑺傜偣锛屽鏋滄病鏈夊垯浣跨敤鏍硅妭鐐?
        JsonNode paramsNode = data.has("params") ? data.get("params") : data;

        // 3. 妫€鏌ュ繀瑕佸瓧娈垫槸鍚﹀瓨鍦?
        boolean hasProductId = paramsNode.has("product_id");
        boolean hasQuantity = paramsNode.has("quantity");
        boolean hasWeight = paramsNode.has("Weight") || paramsNode.has("weight");

        // 4. 楠岃瘉蹇呴』鍖呭惈浜у搧ID鍜屾暟閲忔垨閲嶉噺涓殑涓€涓?
        if (!hasProductId) {
            logger.warn("璁惧鏁版嵁缂哄皯蹇呰瀛楁: product_id");
            return false;
        }

        if (!hasQuantity && !hasWeight) {
            logger.warn("璁惧鏁版嵁蹇呴』鍖呭惈 quantity 鎴?weight/Weight 瀛楁");
            return false;
        }

        // 5. 楠岃瘉瀛楁鏍煎紡鏈夋晥鎬?
        try {
            // 楠岃瘉product_id鏍煎紡锛堝繀椤绘槸鏁板瓧锛?
            if (!paramsNode.get("product_id").isNumber()) {
                logger.warn("product_id蹇呴』鏄暟瀛楃被鍨?);
                return false;
            }
            long productId = paramsNode.get("product_id").asLong();
            if (productId <= 0) {
                logger.warn("product_id蹇呴』鏄鏁?);
                return false;
            }

            // 楠岃瘉quantity鏍煎紡锛堝鏋滃瓨鍦級
            if (hasQuantity) {
                if (!paramsNode.get("quantity").isNumber()) {
                    logger.warn("quantity蹇呴』鏄暟瀛楃被鍨?);
                    return false;
                }
                int quantity = paramsNode.get("quantity").asInt();
                if (quantity <= 0) {
                    logger.warn("quantity蹇呴』鏄鏁存暟");
                    return false;
                }
            }

            // 楠岃瘉weight鏍煎紡锛堝鏋滃瓨鍦級
            if (hasWeight) {
                JsonNode weightNode = paramsNode.has("Weight") ?
                        paramsNode.get("Weight") : paramsNode.get("weight");

                if (!weightNode.isNumber()) {
                    logger.warn("weight蹇呴』鏄暟瀛楃被鍨?);
                    return false;
                }
                double weight = weightNode.asDouble();
                if (weight <= 0) {
                    logger.warn("weight蹇呴』鏄鏁?);
                    return false;
                }
            }

        } catch (Exception e) {
            logger.warn("璁惧鏁版嵁瀛楁瑙ｆ瀽寮傚父: {}", e.getMessage());
            return false;
        }

        // 鎵€鏈夐獙璇侀€氳繃
        return true;
    }

    /**
     * 楠岃瘉鏁板€艰寖鍥?
     */
    public static boolean isInRange(double value, double min, double max) {
        return value >= min && value <= max;
    }

    /**
     * 楠岃瘉瀛楃涓蹭笉涓虹┖
     */
    public static boolean isNotBlank(String str) {
        return str != null && !str.trim().isEmpty();
    }
}

package com.example.supermarket2.component;

import com.example.supermarket2.service.DeviceDataService;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import org.eclipse.paho.client.mqttv3.MqttMessage;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.extension.ExtendWith;
import org.mockito.InjectMocks;
import org.mockito.Mock;
import org.mockito.junit.jupiter.MockitoExtension;

import static org.mockito.ArgumentMatchers.any;
import static org.mockito.ArgumentMatchers.eq;
import static org.mockito.Mockito.*;

@ExtendWith(MockitoExtension.class)
public class MqttMessageListenerTest {

    @Mock
    private DeviceDataService deviceDataService;

    @Mock
    private ObjectMapper objectMapper;

    @InjectMocks
    private MqttMessageListener mqttMessageListener;

    @Test
    public void testMessageArrived() throws Exception {
        // 鍑嗗娴嬭瘯鏁版嵁
        String topic = "/k2069zW7Drp/gwc_wxx/user/get";
        String payload = "{\"user_id\": \"123\", \"product_id\": 1001, \"quantity\": 1}";
        MqttMessage message = new MqttMessage(payload.getBytes());

        // 鎵ц娴嬭瘯
        mqttMessageListener.messageArrived(topic, message);

        // 楠岃瘉
        verify(deviceDataService, times(1)).processDeviceData(
                eq("k2069zW7Drp:gwc_wxx"), eq(topic), any());
    }

    @Test
    public void testMessageArrivedWithInvalidTopic() throws Exception {
        // 鍑嗗娴嬭瘯鏁版嵁 - 鏃犳晥鐨則opic鏍煎紡
        String topic = "/invalid/topic";
        String payload = "{\"user_id\": \"123\", \"product_id\": 1001, \"quantity\": 1}";
        MqttMessage message = new MqttMessage(payload.getBytes());

        // 鎵ц娴嬭瘯
        mqttMessageListener.messageArrived(topic, message);

        // 楠岃瘉 - 搴旇浣跨敤瑙ｆ瀽鍑虹殑璁惧鏍囪瘑
        verify(deviceDataService, times(1)).processDeviceData(
                eq("invalid:topic"), eq(topic), any());
    }
}
